Chapter 1090: A Thousand Years Later, Xu Ke

However, to Li Fan's surprise, these individuals who had successfully passed the Transmitter's Oath, while no longer in charge, did not leave the power core of the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

Instead, they were granted the power of supervision, serving as a supplement to the Transmitter Council.

It seemed that Jiang, after this incident, had realized the problems within the Transmitters. If not restrained, problems would surely arise in the future.

'I wonder if Mo Rubin will eventually pass the Xuanhuang Heavenly Venerate trial.'

'It's fine to reveal some of the trial illusion's specific content to the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Since they've already mastered the method to enter it, with the Myriad Immortals Alliance's resources, they will eventually find qualified candidates.'

Li Fan thought this way and transmitted a general overview of the first act of the illusion, [Ningyuan Picking Longevity Fruits], to Transmitter Zhou.

However, he did not mention his successful completion of the trial, but instead fabricated a story following the most likely plot development route for the first entry.

When picking the longevity fruits, he was severely injured by Steward Song. Although he narrowly escaped death under Senior Brother Zhang's protection, he fell into a coma and remained dazed all day. Until one night, he was inexplicably possessed and lost consciousness.

Shortly after, Transmitter Zhou replied solemnly, 'The information provided by fellow Daoist is crucial. It will be of great help in our future exploration of the illusion.'

As a token of gratitude, Transmitter Zhou, on behalf of the Transmitter Council, bestowed upon Li Fan an honorary title of senior elder within the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

It held no real power, but allowed him to enter and exit the Alliance Headquarters at will, with an authority level only slightly lower than that of the Transmitters.

'However, fellow Daoist cannot take on this senior elder position. After all, to other unaware Transmitters, you have already been executed by Jiang for false accusations.' Transmitter Zhou reminded him again.

This so-called senior elder position was clearly intended to win over the [Myriad Realms United Front] behind Li Fan.

In this incident involving the Xuan Tian Sect's possession, the Myriad Realms United Front had demonstrated sufficient strength.

They even possessed many secrets unknown to the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

Using a nominal position to deepen the cooperative relationship between the two parties was definitely worthwhile.

However, the Myriad Immortals Alliance likely never expected that the so-called Myriad Realms United Front was actually Li Fan's solo act.

During the more than a year Li Fan was in seclusion, everything within the United Front proceeded orderly, continuing to develop steadily according to the established guidelines, and reporting to Li Fan regularly.

After reviewing all this news.

The most eye-catching report was from the Empire.

The location of Xu Ke's small world had finally been determined!

An old man with a weathered appearance, carrying a coffin on his back.

It was exactly the same as what Li Fan had seen before.

Although the Empress was excited to find her ancestor, she did not lose her head and rashly met Xu Ke against Li Fan's orders.

'Then let me go and meet him.'

'Mr. Bai's contingency plan, I am very interested in.'

'Qinghui Prefecture.'

Li Fan headed straight for his destination.

'Although transforming into seven-colored divine light is very fast, it's still far inferior to the Xuanhuang Heavenly Venerate's instantaneous arrival.'

Although he was merely borrowing Mr. Bai's body in the trial illusion, the stark contrast upon returning to reality made him feel a slight sense of loss.

Even a faint feeling of regret arose in his heart.

The moment this emotion surfaced, Li Fan's heart tightened.

He immediately circulated the Xuanhuang Immortal Heart Incantation, intending to dispel it.

But the technique that had always worked flawlessly now actually failed.

'Hmph.'

'This Xuanhuang Realm holds nothing worthy of my regret. Even Immortal Artifacts that transcend the mortal world can be discarded like mere trifles!'

'How dare a mere Xuanhuang Heavenly Venerate disrupt my state of mind?'

As soon as he thought of Huan Zhen, and that all the things he had lost in the past could be regained.

Li Fan's discordant emotions vanished in an instant.

'The Xuanhuang Immortal Heart Incantation's failure is likely why my experience upon entering the Fallen Immortal Realm from the beginning was different from other cultivators.'

'Perhaps it already served as a special identifier for the Fallen Immortal Realm upon entering, when it was still called the Xuanhuang Refinement Heart Incantation.'

'Regarding matters related to the Xuanhuang Heavenly Venerate, it actually stopped working. It seems that things of unknown origin cannot be absolutely trusted.'

'In the end, everything still relies on oneself.'

A shadow flickered in Li Fan's eyes.

'Xuanhuang Refinement Heart Incantation...'

Li Fan had never considered sharing this technique with anyone before.

But this minor accident now served as a reminder.

'Passing it to a suitable person, encouraging them to inherit the Grand Xuanhuang Heavenly Venerate, or to inherit the immortal spiritual energy and bravely venture beyond the high wall, are both good ideas.'

Faces flashed through Li Fan's mind.

While contemplating suitable candidates, Li Fan also arrived at Xu Ke's hiding place.

'This place...'

'It seems to be like Nine Mountain Prefecture, formed from the remains of some demonic beast.'

At the entrance to the small world, Li Fan keenly sensed some familiar aura.

In the trial illusion, he had spent more than ten years with the demonic beasts, forming an instinctive reaction. Even though he had returned to reality, he could still recognize the residual demonic beast aura here.

'This is the growth of perception.'

In just an instant, he deciphered the formation and restrictions at the entrance of the small world.

Li Fan quietly entered.

The Empire's intelligence was accurate; this small world was a desolate desert landscape.

Everything in sight was a hazy gray.

A towering stone mountain in the distance, seemingly connecting the heavens and the earth, was perhaps the only significant feature of the small world.

Li Fan was immediately drawn to it.

Xu Ke was at the very top of this stone mountain.

Li Fan tried to fly up, but was surprised to find that he couldn't fly.

This was not due to Li Fan's strength, but to the special regulatory restrictions of this small world.

It wasn't impossible to fly forcefully, but one had to be prepared to face the Heavenly Dao's backlash within the small world.

Li Fan did not want to make the atmosphere so tense right from the start.

So he looked up, his gaze piercing through tens of thousands of miles, directly landing on Xu Ke at the mountain peak.

The ancient elder, feeling something, also looked back.

Their gazes met.

The next moment, Li Fan stomped his foot.

Instead of flying, he directly tore through space, appearing beside Xu Ke.

His expression was calm, leaving only two spatial rifts that did not dissipate at the starting and ending points.

'Fellow Daoist Xu Ke?'

Li Fan got straight to the point, directly revealing the elder's identity.

To Li Fan's surprise, Xu Ke did not seem surprised by his sudden appearance. Instead, he directly asked, 'Did you recognize me from the Fallen Immortal Realm?'

Li Fan's gaze sharpened upon hearing this.

His tried-and-true tactic of 'seizing the initiative' had failed this time.

Chapter 1091: The Sir Wants to Save the World

After a moment of contemplation, Li Fan decided not to continue playing coy and nodded, 'Indeed. But how did fellow Daoist figure it out?'

Xu Ke, in his slightly deep voice, chuckled, 'Someone who is at odds with the world, where else in the Xuanhuang Realm would my information exist besides the Fallen Immortal Realm?'

Li Fan was slightly taken aback, 'At odds with the world? What does that mean?'

Now it was Xu Ke's turn to be puzzled, 'Don't you know what I'm sitting on? What is this thing?'

Li Fan frankly shook his head.

'Then why are you looking for me?' Xu Ke stared intently at Li Fan, his expression unreadable.

'I am seeking fellow Daoist, firstly, to help the juniors of the Empire fulfill their lifelong wishes.'

'Secondly, it is to understand the various contingency plans left behind by the late Mr. Bai. After learning about his actions, I was deeply moved by his righteousness. However, I received incomplete information from the Fallen Immortal Realm, consisting only of fragmented memories from different periods. Thus, it took considerable effort to find fellow Daoist's hiding place, and I hope for your guidance.' Li Fan cupped his fists and said sincerely.

It seemed that after hearing Li Fan's attitude towards Mr. Bai, Xu Ke's expression softened considerably.

'The Empire?' His eyes narrowed, as if lost in thought.

'It's the legacy you left behind with Xiao Hei in the world where the Crimson Nine Heads died,' Li Fan prompted.

'Ah...' Xu Ke then remembered.

'Xiao Qing, Xiao Hong...' He revealed a reminiscent expression.

'The two are still alive. However, that Heavenly Mandate Blackbird has died while searching for fellow Daoist's whereabouts,' Li Fan said, handing over an object.

It was the last feather of the Xuan Bird left by Xiao Hei in the Beast Seed Realm.

Xu Ke took the black feather with trembling hands. A flicker of sorrow flashed in his eyes. After a long while, he slowly said, 'I have failed it.'

'May I have this item?' Xu Ke asked.

'It's merely returning it to its rightful owner. If Xiao Hei knew that the Xuan Bird feather he left behind would eventually return to fellow Daoist's side, he could rest in peace,' Li Fan sighed.

'Thank you.' Xu Ke solemnly placed the Xuan Bird feather in his chest.

On the towering stone mountain, absolute silence fell once more.

At the apex of this desolate world, it seemed that even the wind did not exist.

Only an eternal stillness, passed down through the ages.

Li Fan was not in a hurry, simply accompanying Xu Ke through this desolate silence, waiting patiently.

After a long while, Xu Ke finally spoke again.

Due to the effectiveness of the previous combo, his attitude towards Li Fan had changed drastically.

'How much do you know currently?' Xu Ke asked.

'You and Xiao Hei traveled to Southern Nether Sacred Beast Mountain under the assignment given by Mr. Bai to the Beast Taming Sect. The subsequent series of actions were all aimed at ultimately nurturing the Split Void Whales capable of infinite replication and void creation, allowing the mortals of various small worlds, forced to migrate due to the Immortal-Mortal Plague, to stay as far away from the Xuanhuang Realm as possible.'

'As for the so-called Immortal-Mortal Plague, it was also a product of Mr. Bai's reversal of principles. As the Grand Xuanhuang Heavenly Venerate, he ultimately ended his own life because of it.'

...

Li Fan slowly recounted the conclusions he had pieced together from the Fallen Immortal Realm and the real world, sentence by sentence.

'You know quite a lot.'

'You have a kind heart.'

'In this world, how many people still remember Mr. Bai? Xu Ke actually bowed to Li Fan, expressing his respect.

'But there are many things I don't understand and cannot let go of. I implore fellow Daoist to enlighten me, otherwise, I fear I will be unable to eat or sleep peacefully in the future.' Li Fan said solemnly.

'Mr. Bai, as the Grand Xuanhuang Heavenly Venerate, was the strongest being in the Xuanhuang Realm at that time. Why did he choose to sacrifice himself and use means like the Immortal-Mortal Plague to protect mortals?'

'Do you think the Immortal-Mortal Plague is effective? If the Xuanhuang Realm had never given birth to the Immortal-Mortal Plague, how would history have unfolded?' Xu Ke countered.

Li Fan pondered for a moment, then slowly replied, 'Without the Immortal-Mortal Plague, the tribulation of 'Laws Cannot Be Cultivated Together' would still exist. Ultimately, cultivators would still fall into mutual suspicion and slaughter. In such a process...'

'When the gate of the city burns, the fish in the moats also suffer. In the cultivation wasteland, where can mortals find a place to live? Even surviving is fortunate. Being infected by the Immortal-Mortal Plague and then being forced to migrate to small worlds, although many people will die in the process, compared to the fate they would face if they remained in the Xuanhuang Realm, it is almost negligible.' Xu Ke helped Li Fan by saying.

Li Fan nodded slowly in agreement.

'So, Mr. Bai foresaw the fate of the Xuanhuang Realm for the next few thousand years right from the beginning of the great tribulation?' Li Fan asked again.

'That wouldn't be difficult for Mr. Bai,' Xu Ke said matter-of-factly.

'Since that's the case...' Li Fan's tone and expression suddenly changed.

'The great tribulation of 'Laws Cannot Be Cultivated Together' was caused by the Transmitter cultivating new laws. As long as the culprit is killed, it might be possible to correct the course! Why did Mr. Bai choose to retreat without a fight?'

'He doesn't even care about his own life, yet he didn't have the courage to fight the Transmitter?' Li Fan's voice seemed filled with strong resentment.

'There is the saying, "The immortal path ahead cannot be trodden, Transmitter Heavenly Venerate is above,"' After a period of silence, Xu Ke sighed faintly and uttered Mr. Bai's former words.

He then explained, 'Let's not discuss whether Mr. Bai was a match for the Transmitter Heavenly Venerate, who had already succeeded in reversing the principles.'

'In fact, according to Mr. Bai's deductions, even if the Transmitter was killed, the great tribulation of the Xuanhuang Realm could not be prevented.'

'Ningyuan City, the underground secret room, that beast-type monster that combined man and dog, have you seen it?'

'I have.'

'That beast-type creature, with a human body and canine limbs. Mr. Bai once tried to save their lives. He collected suitable human limbs, intending to remove their canine limbs and reattach the human ones.'

'However, because the canine limbs had already integrated with their bodies through daily life, Mr. Bai's multiple attempts inevitably failed.'

'Most of them died directly during the transplant surgery. Even those who seemingly succeeded often did not live past a month. Due to the rapid loss of life force, they all died tragically.'

'No matter how hard Mr. Bai tried, the result remained the same.'

Xu Ke explained calmly.

Li Fan slowly began to recall.

'Are you saying that the Xuanhuang Realm faces the same situation?'

Xu Ke sighed, 'As the saying goes, spilled water cannot be gathered.'

'The changes brought about by the Transmitter to the Xuanhuang Realm have already occurred.'

'To reverse it would require efforts ten, a hundred times greater.'

Chapter 1092: Heavenly Dao Goes Mad

'So it's not that Mr. Bai was inferior to Transmitter Heavenly Venerate, but simply that Mr. Bai achieved his enlightenment later than Transmitter Heavenly Venerate.'

'Conversely, if Mr. Bai had changed the Xuanhuang Realm first, then perhaps Transmitter Heavenly Venerate would have been helpless.'

'But alas, there are no ifs.'

Xu Ke's ancient voice carried a deep sense of regret.

Li Fan fell silent for a long time, finally responding with a sigh.

'I see.'

'But...'

Li Fan frowned, 'Was Mr. Bai's sacrifice in the pursuit of the Dao really that simple?'

'The birth of the Immortal-Mortal Plague could indeed preserve the lives of mortals in the Xuanhuang Realm for a time, but fundamentally, it was merely a delaying tactic.'

'In the end, mortals would still be treated as cattle by cultivators; and the Xuanhuang Realm would still be in mortal danger. Since Mr. Bai could deduce events thousands of years into the future, he naturally would not have overlooked this point.'

'Given his character, how could he have made such hasty departure without any preparations?'

Li Fan stubbornly tried to extract more secrets from Xu Ke.

Because he always felt that there must be something hidden behind Mr. Bai's demise.

Unexpectedly, Xu Ke just smiled and shook his head, 'You, like me, always thought Mr. Bai was an omnipotent sage. But in reality, in his own words...'

'He was just an ordinary person who couldn't bear to see others suffer.'

'From his initial powerlessness when facing Miss Liu'er and the tragic deaths of innocent citizens in Ningyuan City, to his later futile attempts to alter fate. Mr. Bai's life was spent in powerlessness. Therefore, he never thought he had the ability to save everything. All he could do was to do his best.'

'And he truly did give his all.'

Xu Ke fell silent again, 'Do you know what's inside the coffin behind me?'

Li Fan looked behind Xu Ke.

Upon closer inspection, he noticed that the pale white coffin seemed to be connected to the towering stone mountain behind him.

Or rather...

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and observed for a long time before suddenly realizing.

The entire small world inverted in his eyes.

The earth was above, and the sky was below.

The towering stone mountain on the coffin seemed to be supporting the entire sky.

Or perhaps, the weight of the entire world was pressing down on the coffin.

And from this coffin, Li Fan felt an extremely familiar aura.

It was an aura that every Xuanhuang cultivator would be familiar with.

He recalled Xu Ke's self-introduction when they first met, mentioning being "a person who is at odds with the world."

'This... could it be?' Li Fan was greatly startled. He suddenly looked up at Xu Ke.

Xu Ke's expression remained unchanged, only maintaining a faint smile.

'Mr. Bai was favored by the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, almost equivalent to a manifestation of the Heavenly Dao.'

'Not only did he ascend to the Longevity Heavenly Venerate realm in one step as a mortal, but he also took on the mission of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao to abandon the world and leave.'

'But ultimately, Mr. Bai did not choose to leave. He then directly became a member of the new law, participating in the reversal of heavenly principles. This was undoubtedly a complete betrayal to the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.'

'The deeper the Heavenly Dao's favor, the greater the backlash upon betrayal. This is also one of the reasons why Mr. Bai was killed by his own reversed creation, because he had become very weak before that.'

Xu Ke patted the coffin behind him and said, 'In fact, at that time, given Mr. Bai's degree of Heavenly Dao favor, he was fundamentally unable to perform the reversal. He likely would have perished due to the Heavenly Dao's backlash before the reversal was even completed.'

'So...'

'Before the reversal, Mr. Bai stripped away the Heavenly Dao's favor. Then he suppressed it.'

As if sensing Xu Ke's words, the coffin behind him suddenly let out a muffled banging sound.

His head spun, and a pale face, somewhat resembling Mr. Bai's, suddenly appeared before Li Fan's eyes.

He used extremely seductive words, persuading Li Fan to help open the coffin.

After the deed was done, upon returning to the Xuanhuang Realm, he would surely be rewarded a thousandfold.

If it were an ordinary cultivator, they might have been persuaded instantly and become its tool for escape, even fighting Xu Ke.

But who was Li Fan?

Not to mention the toughness of his own state of mind, just the vigilance he had always maintained towards Mr. Bai meant that he would certainly not be swayed by this somewhat creepy-looking Mr. Bai.

With a cold snort, the illusions before him shattered.

Li Fan awoke from the illusion, only to find Xu Ke observing him coldly, as if ready to make a move if they disagreed.

However, upon seeing that Li Fan was not affected by the illusion, the killing intent in his eyes faded.

'Sealed Heavenly Favor? What is that thing?' Li Fan pretended to be still shaken.

'The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao's consciousness attached to Mr. Bai, which Mr. Bai stripped away. After years of sealing and suppression, it has gradually become somewhat extreme. If it were released and returned to the Xuanhuang Realm...' Xu Ke's expression was very serious.

'Perhaps a calamity ten times more terrifying than [Laws Cannot Be Cultivated Together] would descend instantly. This is also why, over the years, even when Xiao Hei died, I dared not leave this place for a single step. The matter is too significant, and absolutely cannot afford any mistakes.'

'An extreme Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao?' A flicker of brilliance flashed deep in Li Fan's eyes.

'Yes, I can feel that over the years of being sealed, the Heavenly Dao consciousness inside has become increasingly strange. I truly worry that one day, I too will lose my resolve.' Xu Ke's eyes flashed with deep worry.

'Recently, I have also been secretly looking for a suitable successor. However, I have not found anyone I can confidently entrust this to. Today, fellow Daoist has come by chance...'

Xu Ke's tone suddenly shifted, 'Isn't this destined by fate?'

'I observe fellow Daoist's character and integrity, both are absolutely top-notch.' He looked at Li Fan sincerely and said earnestly.

Li Fan pondered, not responding immediately.

'Of course, the mission of suppressing the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao is too lonely and perilous. If fellow Daoist is unwilling, I can understand. But I have a request...' Xu Ke said.

'Please speak, fellow Daoist.' Li Fan said solemnly.

'If one day, I am controlled by the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao in this coffin and lose my self-awareness, please, fellow Daoist, take action and kill me.' Xu Ke said very seriously.

Looking at the aged Xu Ke's eyes, Li Fan nodded, 'Alright, I promise you.'

'Moreover, you need not worry about finding a successor.'

Xu Ke's expression slightly stiffened.

'Speaking of which, you might not believe it. I am not alone; I am a member of the [Myriad Realms United Front].'

Chapter 1093: News of Mystic Dharma King

"In our United Front, there are countless young talents. Finding suitable successors will definitely not be a difficult task," Li Fan said confidently.

"This matter concerns the safety of all cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm. The United Front will naturally not stand idly by. If fellow Daoist is unable to leave, I will arrange for them to come once I return, so that fellow Daoist can personally scrutinize them."

"I believe that with fellow Daoist's discerning eye, you will surely find a candidate you are pleased with," Li Fan said with righteous indignation.

"This..." Xu Ke seemed somewhat incredulous.

After a long while, he hastily replied, somewhat at a loss, "If that's the case, then I thank fellow Daoist in advance."

"By the way, Xiao Qing and Xiao Hong, as well as your descendants, and the Imperial Princess, all miss you dearly. Would you be willing to see them?" Without acting on his own, Li Fan proactively inquired.

A hint of sadness flashed across Xu Ke's face.

However, he nodded afterward.

Before leaving this desolate small world, during his conversation with Xu Ke, Li Fan gained a more detailed understanding of the events that transpired back then.

As early as before deciding to reverse the principles and create the Immortal-Mortal Plague, Mr. Bai had traveled to the great sects of the Xuanhuang Realm and made extensive preparations.

For example, he had identified individuals in pivotal positions within almost every sect.

This ensured that once the plan to unleash the Immortal-Mortal Plague and migrate mortals to the small worlds and grotto-heavens was proposed, it would be quickly accepted by the major sects.

As well as the Immortal Severing Grand Formation that sealed the mortal small worlds, and even the Rift Whales beyond the formation...

The ultimate realization of these plans bore the traces of Mr. Bai's prior arrangements.

It was a pity that Xu Ke did not know much about these details.

Back then, he had suddenly heard the dire news of Lu Ya and rushed over. It was on Lu Ya's deathbed that he received his final mission: to guard the stripped Xuanhuang Celestial Favor.

...

"The Heavenly Dao of the world has its own operating mechanisms."

"Just as the world of Li Realm, after facing the crisis of world destruction, the Heavenly Dao consciousness naturally sought potential candidates for escape and descended upon Su Yuqing."

"The Xuanhuang Realm also chose Mr. Bai. It's just a pity that Mr. Bai, caught between the Heavenly Dao and the mortals of Xuanhuang, ultimately chose the latter."

"He then sealed the Heavenly Dao consciousness that possessed him..."

"Judging from the performance of the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao since then, it has consistently been at a disadvantage in battles against cultivators. It no longer possesses countermeasures like 'Laws Cannot Be Cultivated Together.' This is likely due to the impact on the remaining Heavenly Dao's strength."

Li Fan suddenly thought of Ruo Mu.

Similarly, after being deeply harmed by humans, Ruo Mu transformed from a divine tree that nurtured all living beings in the world into a terrifying entity that captured cultivators to form their cores.

This was the power of resentment.

Betrayed by the one who favored him most, and sealed for nearly ten thousand years, one could only imagine what the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao sealed in the coffin behind Xu Ke had become.

"Another killer move. However, it's not suitable for this era and would only introduce unnecessary variables."

"The current remnant Heavenly Dao of the Xuanhuang Realm can still be manipulated by me. If the Heavenly Dao goes berserk, my divine abilities might also become ineffective."

While pondering, Li Fan returned to the Spirit Wood Realm.

After conveying the news of Xu Ke to Xiao Qing and others of the Empire, they were naturally overjoyed and expressed their profound gratitude to Li Fan.

Under Li Fan's reminder, knowing what could and could not be said, the representatives of the Empire eagerly rushed to meet Xu Ke.

Accompanying them were aspiring young talents selected from various small worlds.

Li Fan had only made a rough selection; the specifics would be decided by Xu Ke himself.

After finishing these matters, Li Fan proceeded to [Seeking Seclusion].

More than a year had passed, and more than a dozen stone tablets had already been erected.

Most of them contained insignificant content from forgotten history.

However, the latest discovery from the river of blood had piqued Li Fan's interest.

The time it depicted was after countless years of fighting had subsided, and civilization was slowly recovering in the cultivation wasteland. In the scene, a man dressed in tattered clothes, emanating a strong aura of malevolence, looked warily at an old man who had suddenly appeared before him.

The man in the scene naturally did not recognize the old man.

However, Li Fan, outside the scene, was very familiar with him.

It was Heavenly Physician!

Without any preamble, Heavenly Physician struck instantly, subduing the malevolent man.

It seemed he was also extracting the memories from the malevolent man from those years.

"Has this much time already passed?"

"It seems I should try to stay further away from the Immortal Ruins next time," Heavenly Physician sighed to himself.

He then casually struck the malevolent man dead and vanished from the spot.

...

The scene abruptly ended, but the information it contained was substantial.

At the very least, it confirmed that thousands of years ago, Heavenly Physician possessed the strength to resist the pull of the Immortal Ruins and traverse the void.

Moreover, he had traveled back and forth more than once.

During this process, he was inevitably influenced by the Immortal Ruins, and by the time he reappeared, a considerable amount of time had passed in the Xuanhuang Realm.

"It seems that the sudden disappearances and reappearances of some individuals are likely due to the time dilation effects of the Immortal Ruins."

"This means..."

The speculation that Li Fan had intended to verify in his next life suddenly resurfaced in his mind.

Li Fan's expression grew even more solemn.

"Transmission Law and Heavenly Physician were frequently active in the Xuanhuang Realm. The information contained within the river of blood is very valuable."

Once again issuing generous rewards to boost the morale of his subordinates, Li Fan continued his investigation.

A few days later, Li Fan unexpectedly received news about Mo Rubin from Transmitter Zhou.

"He has appeared?"

"And he hasn't ascended to become the Grand Xuanhuang Heavenly Venerate?" Li Fan frowned.

"Could it be a feint? Given his cautious nature, even if his plan failed, he wouldn't easily reveal his whereabouts."

Transmitter Zhou, however, was very confident: "The place where he appeared is one of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's secret locations."

"Although it appears devoid of other cultivators, we have already established covert surveillance on him."

"Furthermore, Mo Rubin did not appear in his true form. We tracked the residual fluctuations based on the transformation mark he left on Transmitter Chen, which allowed us to finally discover and lock onto him."

"Therefore, I am more inclined to believe that he has miscalculated this time."

Transmitter Zhou harbored great animosity towards this Xuan Tian Sect Dharma King who repeatedly played the Myriad Immortals Alliance members for fools.

He solemnly stated, "This time, the elite forces of our Myriad Immortals Alliance will be deployed to capture him. I wonder if fellow Daoist is interested in cooperating with us again?"

Li Fan immediately agreed: "I will seek instructions and reply to you shortly."

After a short wait, Li Fan sent a message: "The United Front Elders have agreed."

"Moreover, this time, we will also utilize our newly developed technology to assist in the capture!"

Chapter 1094: Array of the Vengeful Glutton

Transmitter Zhou was very pleased to see Li Fan agree so quickly. "Good, then let's meet here."

With that, the location coordinates were transmitted.

After ending the communication, Li Fan began his preparations.

The "newly developed technology" he mentioned was not baseless. It was the result of the derivation of the End Obliteration Disc over the past year.

Since mastering the two celestial-grade formations, [Mysterious Pivot, Myriad Spirits Calculations] and [Desolate Fall, Void Room Blossoms], and after absorbing the nine nascent sub-discs, achieving metamorphosis, the Disintegration Disc's formation analysis capabilities had been increasing at an unimaginable rate.

Every moment, it seemed as if countless new formations were being derived.

The Disintegration Disc was like the Dharma Derivation Jade, aiming to derive all formations in the world!

Even without Li Fan's intentional manipulation as its owner, in one year, it had accumulated an extremely vast formation database.

With a few conditions added, and a simple search, Li Fan found what he was looking for.

Named after its pseudo-celestial-grade formation, the array was called [Gluttonous Revenge: Vengeance Must Be Taken].

The array's effect, as its name suggested, was to automatically scan for objects with grievances around the formation while it was active, and then mark and track them.

Its coverage area was roughly the size of one province of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Once locked by the [Gluttonous Revenge] formation, as long as the target did not leave the array's range, they would be continuously tracked.

The formation had a peculiar characteristic, meaning that one array could only target one grievance object at a time.

Li Fan experimented with it; the locking method of the Gluttonous Revenge formation was completely beyond his current understanding, already subtly approaching the [Celestial] level.

However, Mo Rubin's performance last time was truly unsettling.

So, a single formation was not enough!

Li Fan then took out a small jade bottle.

Inside the bottle were three pills.

They moved at high speed within the bottle in a seemingly chaotic trajectory, yet exuded a divine mystique.

"Soul Wandering Pills."

"After ingestion, to outsiders, the soul will appear to be wandering and extremely chaotic. However, in reality, one can still maintain control over their body. It is highly effective against soul-body usurpation. Mo Rubin's soul usurpation technique is similar to Transmitter Jiang's, transforming from me."

"But when facing a ball of chaos, how can one usurp or influence it?"

A cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes: "Even if it cannot be completely prevented, it can at least significantly delay the process of his soul usurpation."

"Three pills constitute a set. The Medicine King Sect's first batch produced over two hundred sets..."

...

With everything prepared, Li Fan, accompanied by Tian Yang, headed to the agreed location for the rendezvous.

Naturally, he had altered his original appearance.

Transmitter Zhou was already waiting, along with thirty-seven other individuals.

They were roughly divided into three factions. The largest group was a squad of expressionless, grim-faced cultivators in black robes.

Compared to those Li Fan had seen before, their eyes were even more vacant.

Rather than cultivators, they seemed like puppets without their own thoughts, merely executing received commands.

The remaining two factions consisted of two other transmitters who stood with Transmitter Zhou.

The second group was somewhat peculiar.

They were not human in appearance, being short, only about the size of a seven or eight-year-old child.

They had no heads, with their facial features clustered on their chests.

Their entire bodies were black, appearing somewhat comical and ferocious.

"To enter this forbidden area, we also require guides from the [Nether] race," Transmitter Zhou said to Li Fan after greeting him with a slight bow, glancing at Tian Yang, who stood silently behind Li Fan with his eyes closed.

"Nether?" Li Fan observed these strange beings with interest.

"Let's talk as we walk. Here are the precautions for entering."

At Transmitter Zhou's signal, the Nether race members stood together, hand in hand, and began to perform a peculiar dance.

Like some kind of ritual, with their synchronized humming, a faint, obscure aura of confinement silently descended upon them.

Of course, this was merely Li Fan's perception. In reality, whether observed with the naked eye or divine sense, there were no actual changes ahead.

"Let's go in first."

However, the subsequent actions of everyone indicated that Li Fan's premonition was correct.

As the Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators flew towards the space above the Nether race members, they seemed to be suddenly swallowed by an ominous darkness.

They vanished into thin air.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators entered one after another, and Li Fan finally flew in with them.

Light was stripped from the world.

All around was complete, boundless darkness.

Slightly different from the Darkest Star Sea outside the Xuanhuang Realm.

Both were darkness, but the blackness of the Star Sea gave a sense of deathly stillness, emptiness, and vastness.

Here, however...

It felt cramped, damp, and gloomy, as if something were stirring in the darkness, ready to pounce and devour at any moment.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators who had entered earlier seemed to have collectively disappeared.

In the dark forbidden area, it seemed only Li Fan remained.

Li Fan subconsciously tried to scan his surroundings with his divine sense, only to find that divine sense was useless here.

Upon leaving his body, it was as if it were enveloped by boundless darkness, rendering him unable to perceive anything else.

Li Fan then attempted to illuminate the surroundings with light but failed again.

Light, it seemed, could not survive in this forbidden area.

At that moment, without any warning, a hand suddenly rested on Li Fan's shoulder.

His hair stood on end, and Li Fan was instantly ready to retaliate.

However, through physical contact, divine sense could be transmitted.

Li Fan then "heard" the other party's words.

He first introduced himself.

Transmitter Yan.

Only then did he explain to Li Fan: "In this dark forbidden area, divine sense and sound are rendered useless. Only by connecting physically, like the Nether race, can communication be achieved."

"We entered together and did not separate. Everyone should be nearby. Let's regroup first."

Li Fan nodded slightly.

This dark forbidden area was indeed quite strange. Even his connection with Tian Yang had been severed.

Fortunately, Tian Yang had not gone far, and it did not take much effort to find him again.

With a thought, Li Fan, unnoticed, transformed Tian Yang into the Celestial Puppet Armor and attached it to himself.

"The Gluttonous Revenge formation has also been greatly weakened here. The coverage of its sensory range is only about three zhang around me?" Li Fan couldn't help but be inwardly alarmed.

This was, after all, a formation infinitely close to a true celestial-grade formation.

"I didn't expect that within the Xuanhuang Realm, there would be such a perilous place. Why did Mo Rubin come here?"

Just like the Nether race members who held hands before entering, the Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators and Li Fan regrouped through this method.

After taking stock of the numbers and discovering that three were missing, the group did not search for them.

Instead, they issued a kill order for them.

Simultaneously, they ventured deeper into the darkness.

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1095: The Dark Devours the Dharma King

"From now on, we are one entity."

"If anyone discovers the three people who fell behind attempting to return, report it immediately, and then we will all strike them down together."

"Remember, do not trust anyone who returns from the darkness, even if they were once your closest companion."

As they walked step by step, the Myriad Immortals Alliance members reiterated the prohibition.

Simultaneously, through communication with Transmitter Zhou, Li Fan also learned about the origin of this dark forbidden area.

Due to the existence of the Immortal Ruins, the Xuanhuang Realm was constantly being subjected to an immense pulling force.

Under normal circumstances, if not stopped, everything in the Xuanhuang Realm would gradually fall into the Immortal Ruins.

This was what the Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators had always believed.

However, the discovery of the dark forbidden area shattered this perception.

The dark forbidden area was a collection of all terrestrial matter that deviated from the direction of the Immortal Ruins.

Although still a part of the Xuanhuang Realm, it possessed its own unique rules here.

In addition to the previously mentioned inabilities of divine sense and sound to travel beyond one's body,

Lost cultivators would have their divine consciousness seized by unknown entities in the darkness, transforming them into something else.

And they themselves would be unaware of it.

"This... seems somewhat similar to Mo Rubin's soul usurpation technique?" Li Fan's heart stirred.

"That's right. But it's only similar in characteristics. It doesn't prove anything,"

Transmitter Zhou seemed intent on avoiding the topic and continued, "After this place was discovered, the Myriad Immortals Alliance placed great importance on it. Due to the dark's characteristic of deviating from the Immortal Ruins, perhaps by studying it, we could find a method to escape the Immortal Ruins. However, previously, only a few core transmitters knew about this."

"That Xuan Tian Sect Dharma King once occupied the bodies of Chen and the others, thus he also learned of this place's existence."

"The Nether race does not live in the dark forbidden area. Rather, they were the first to discover how to open the dark forbidden area and mastered the method to utilize its power. We discovered this secret during the process of conquering the small world where the Nether race resided and fighting them."

"The power of darkness? Could it be, it's a completely different existence from Immortal Spiritual Power?" Li Fan pondered and asked.

"That's not the case. Based on our observations over the years, the power of darkness does possess certain characteristics of Immortal Spiritual Power. But..." Transmitter Zhou paused, seemingly searching for suitable descriptive words.

"Immortal Spiritual Power and the power of darkness are like a person and their shadow."

"Originally, these two should have been inseparable and merged with each other. However, due to the existence of the Immortal Ruins, the power of darkness was forcibly separated from it."

Li Fan vaguely understood upon hearing this.

It was like a centrifuge separating different components in a liquid.

Due to its characteristic of deviating from the Immortal Ruins, as the entire Xuanhuang Realm gradually fell into the Immortal Ruins, the power of darkness also converged in the opposite direction.

"The pulling force of the Immortal Ruins is due to the existence of the 'Hunger' rune."

"Then what exactly is this power of darkness? It can actually resist the power of True Immortal runes?"

Li Fan felt some doubt in his heart.

"We have already explored the entire dark forbidden area before. Therefore, when Mo Rubin infiltrated and caused an anomaly, we could detect it immediately."

"If you observe carefully, you should also be able to notice something," Transmitter Zhou reminded him.

"Oh?"

Li Fan frowned and sensed the surrounding darkness.

After a long while...

"You mean this rhythmic pulsation, like ripples on water?" Li Fan asked.

"Correct. At the source of this pulsation, we discovered Mo Rubin's aura. However..."

Transmitter Zhou's tone became uncertain, "He has been here for about ten days but has not changed his position. He seems to be severely injured and unconscious."

"Could it be a trap?" Li Fan couldn't help but ask.

"No," Transmitter Zhou stated with certainty.

"Even if it's a trap... so many of us are here today. We don't fear an ancient Dao longevity cultivator at all."

Seeing Transmitter Zhou's confidence, Li Fan stopped objecting.

With no one communicating, the surroundings once again fell into a terrifying silence.

"Maintain vigilance, we are almost there." After an unknown period, Transmitter Zhou's notification came.

Locking onto the direction of the pulsation from afar, the Myriad Immortals Alliance members followed the instructions and formed a circle.

Surrounding Mo Rubin, hidden in the darkness, they were ready to attack at a single command.

At the same time, Li Fan also received constant reminders from the Gluttonous Revenge formation.

"It really is Mo Rubin?" Li Fan couldn't help but feel a little surprised.

"Strange..."

Despite his lingering doubts, Li Fan did not act rashly.

He merely followed the movements of the Myriad Immortals Alliance members, gradually shrinking their hunting circle.

Everyone held their breath, but Mo Rubin remained completely unresponsive.

As if he hadn't even noticed the approaching enemies around him.

This continued even as the Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators finally reached his position.

...

"Cease vigilance."

"He seems to be dead."

Transmitter Zhou's voice was filled with disbelief.

"Hmm?"

A chill suddenly coursed through Li Fan's heart.

Following the bodies of the Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators, he arrived at the center.

The moment he touched Mo Rubin's body, his divine sense also perceived his current appearance.

Mo Rubin's face had disappeared.

Only a mass of darkness, constantly coalescing and dispersing, surged around his head.

This scene was indescribably bizarre, but what made Li Fan even more horrified was Mo Rubin's body.

One half was still a human body.

But the other half seemed to have been occupied by the surrounding darkness.

It was constantly shifting between darkness and physicality.

Under the probing of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's black-clothed death warriors, it was confirmed that the darkness engulfing half of Mo Rubin's body was not an illusion.

Rather, it was real flesh disappearing and reappearing as it transformed.

When the darkness appeared and touched, it encountered only void.

But after a while, when the half-human body reappeared, the darkness suddenly vanished.

Even the death warrior's hand, reaching into the darkness, disappeared along with it.

The darkness seemed to spread contagiously. The black-clothed death warrior made no sound before being engulfed by the darkness emerging from his own hand.

Fortunately, Transmitter Zhou acted decisively, immediately severing contact with the death warrior and ordering them all to strike him down.

This prevented the darkness from spreading among the Myriad Immortals Alliance members.

"What are your thoughts, fellow Daoist?" Transmitter Zhou asked with a heavy tone.

Li Fan remained silent for a long time, then slowly replied, "The darkness on Mo Rubin's corpse seems different from the darkness in the forbidden area."

"The corpse's darkness is contagious, while the surrounding environment's is not."

"Before we understand the reality of this place, it's best not to touch it."

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1096: Legends of Creation

"Although this power of darkness might help us escape the Immortal Ruins, that would be under the condition that we can safely control it."

"Otherwise..."

Li Fan's expression was serious, "If the world is eroded by this darkness, the outcome will be no better than falling into the Immortal Ruins."

As the two spoke, as if receiving some nourishment, the darkness occupying half of Mo Rubin's body suddenly expanded again.

It almost completely enveloped the entire corpse.

However, strangely, the pulsation emanating from him never stopped.

It was even clearer than before.

It was like the throbbing of a heart, echoing in this dark forbidden area, causing an ominous premonition to gradually arise in Li Fan's heart.

Several transmitters in the team also realized that the situation seemed to be amiss.

They soon issued an order to temporarily retreat.

After retreating a considerable distance, Li Fan's strong unease slowly subsided.

"My suggestion is to completely seal this forbidden area. Before understanding the true nature of the power of darkness, do not approach Mo Rubin's corpse easily."

"When I return, I will immediately report this discovery to the Alliance. Once there is any news, I will inform you immediately."

Seeing Li Fan's caution, Transmitter Zhou nodded in agreement on the surface, but inwardly felt somewhat dismissive.

"Fellow Daoist, you don't need to be overly nervous. Regardless, the characteristic of this darkness deviating from the Immortal Ruins will not change. This inherently means that it will not invade the Xuanhuang Realm."

Li Fan shook his head and didn't say much more.

With Mo Rubin dead, Li Fan saw no need to stay any longer.

Although the journey of revenge ended anticlimactically, the discovery of the power of darkness was of great significance.

After bidding farewell to the Myriad Immortals Alliance members, Li Fan quickly summoned members from various departments of the United Front and recounted his experiences in the dark forbidden area.

"The power of darkness..."

Daoist Baihua was the first to speak.

As someone who had survived from ancient times, although Baihua's strength was not great, he was certainly knowledgeable.

"I seem to have heard something similar from a fellow Daoist back then."

"He personally witnessed his homeland fall into the Immortal Ruins from afar, a dreamlike scene of all things disintegrating and forming a bizarre, twisted halo."

"According to his description, just as the cultivation world completely disappeared into the Immortal Ruins, a large amount of matter seemed to erupt from the opposite direction."

"Neither the naked eye nor divine sense could detect it. He was merely unlucky enough to be grazed by it and was immediately severely injured. Even after recovering, he became a grotesque figure, neither human nor ghost."

Looking at the terrifying image of a cultivator drawn by Baihua, with black, wriggling holes covering his face, everyone's expression became somewhat solemn.

And Hermit Gigao seemed to have remembered something: "Back when the power of the Immortal Ruins first enveloped the [Ancestor], we were actually quite confident about overcoming the calamity."

"Because, based on the strength of the Ancestor's remaining body at that time, it was sufficient to resist the attraction of the Immortal Ruins. But later, the attraction of the Immortal Ruins grew stronger, which was one aspect..."

Hermit Gigao's expression turned enlightened, "The weakening of the Ancestor's strength was the fundamental reason! It was as if something critical was constantly being lost, causing the Ancestor's body to slowly decay."

"At that time, all the elders were perplexed. In the end, they could only attribute it to the power of the Immortal Ruins."

"Now it seems that the disappearing element was likely also this power of darkness."

Li Fan mused after hearing their words: "Are you suggesting that the power of darkness is actually a part of the cultivators' cultivation system? It's just that due to its opposite nature to the Immortal Ruins' attraction, it was forcibly separated during the approach to the Immortal Ruins."

"In other cultivation worlds, the power of darkness would dissipate because of this. But in the Xuanhuang Realm, for some unknown reason, it all converged in one place, still bound to the Xuanhuang Realm."

"If, one day, the Xuanhuang Realm can break free from the Immortal Ruins, the power of darkness should return to all things in the Xuanhuang world."

After hearing Li Fan's analysis, Hermit Gigao and Daoist Baihua both nodded.

At this moment, Liu Ruchen of the Medicine King Sect suddenly spoke: "Although I have not personally witnessed this so-called power of darkness, I once read a legend in an ancient text."

"It circulated among various human races, concerning the origin of humanity."

"In the beginning, there were no humans in the world, nor were there various cultivation realms. In absolute nothingness, a few powerful beings drifted. Later, one of them, feeling bored, used himself as raw material to create and open up various worlds."

"Gradually, the void became filled. And other beings were also attracted by these dazzling and strange worlds, and they began to imitate, creating various races based on their own archetypes."

"And the ancestors of humanity were the first to create all realms."

Everyone had clearly never heard this legend before, and they listened with great interest.

"Although the world became much more lively, these powerful beings soon discovered an anomaly. Because all the beings they created, unlike themselves, could not be immortal and undying. They had the limitation of so-called lifespan."

"The liveliness was temporary; soon the world would return to silence. Occasionally, creators might create things out of interest, but continuously creating would become a burden."

"Therefore, the powerful beings gradually lost interest in the life forms they had created."

"But one of them was not like this. He did not wish to see his creations disappear, so he defeated his companions and extracted power from them, bestowing it upon all created life forms."

"Thus, sentient beings gained the ability to reproduce."

Liu Ruchen stopped speaking at this point.

Everyone was listening with great interest and gestured for him to continue with their eyes.

Liu Ruchen shrugged: "That's all there is."

"It's nothing more than saying thanks to the gods for the grace of creation."

"The reason I associate it with the power of darkness is perhaps that it might inspire us to research the effects of losing or gaining the power of darkness on us cultivators."

"If this power of darkness originally existed within us, but was merely separated due to the appearance of the Immortal Ruins, wouldn't that mean that we currently..."

"Are incomplete?"

"Compared to cultivators before the Immortal Ruins appeared, how are we different?"

Hermit Gigao's expression changed slightly upon hearing this.

"I knew it! Ever since the calamity of the Immortal Ruins occurred, my comprehension and creativity seem to have been far inferior to before?"

"Could it be because of this reason?"

Chapter 1097: A Journey into the Unknown in a Foreign Land

"You're saying you've become stupid?" Daoist Baihua stared blankly at Hermit Gigao.

"Should..."

Before Gigao could finish speaking, Baihua interjected, "Compared to the beginning, I haven't noticed any significant changes. Could this be due to your own issues?"

Gigao was rendered speechless.

"Guessing is pointless. Why not try it yourself?" Fang Zaiji's eyes gleamed with eagerness.

Everyone chimed in, one after another.

Finally, it was Li Fan who made the decision: "The return of the power of darkness is not as simple as we imagine."

"If we merely absorb it, we might end up like Mo Rubin, being corroded by it instead."

"Furthermore, the dark forbidden area is currently under the control of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. If we want to enter and study it..."

"They probably won't permit it."

Liu Ruchen said, "Didn't the envoy mention that the Myriad Immortals Alliance was able to enter the dark forbidden area through some ritual performed by the [Nether] race?"

"Do you still remember the specific details of that ritual? If we can imitate it, perhaps we can sneak in."

"After all, it's completely dark inside the dark forbidden area. As long as we are careful, we won't be detected by them."

Fang Zaiji echoed repeatedly, "Sect Master, what a brilliant suggestion! We should definitely try it!"

Li Fan pondered for a moment, then used the Water Mirror Technique to restore the rather peculiar ritual scene.

Including the intonation and pitch of the chanting, everything was perfectly replicated.

After selecting over a dozen young cultivators to learn it, as expected, the ritual failed.

"Does it really require the Nether race?" Fang Zaiji cursed under his breath.

The members of the United Front also shook their heads, feeling somewhat regretful.

"The Nether race..."

Li Fan had mastered the basic information of all small worlds in the Xuanhuang Realm.

However, there was no mention of the Nether race among them. It was likely that the Myriad Immortals Alliance had deliberately concealed this information.

"It doesn't matter; as long as we eliminate options one by one."

During the search for Xu Ke, most of the small worlds had already undergone preliminary investigations.

Completing the remainder would not take much time.

At Li Fan's command, countless inconspicuous exotic beasts swarmed towards the entrances of various small worlds.

In just half a month, there was news.

In the last image transmitted before being annihilated, traces of what appeared to be the [Nether] race were discovered.

There must be someone from the Myriad Immortals Alliance guarding that small world.

Li Fan personally led Tian Yang to infiltrate it.

He was quite interested in the power of darkness.

Not only because it was related to the possibility of escaping the Immortal Ruins but also because of its connection to the so-called "completeness."

Li Fan had always harbored doubts about Mo Rubin's demise.

The treacherous Xuan Tian Sect Dharma King, who had tricked him multiple times, had actually died so incomprehensibly in the darkness.

This made Li Fan find it difficult to believe.

Especially the reason for his entry into the dark forbidden area.

Mo Rubin's objective should have remained unchanged from the beginning: find Xuan Tian King and leave the Darkest Star Sea.

Even if he failed the Grand Xuanhuang Heavenly Venerate illusion trial, he must have discovered some clues from it.

"Could it be that Xuan Tian King is hidden within the dark forbidden area?"

"Or perhaps, his inexplicable disappearance back then was also related to the power of darkness?"

With various doubts, Li Fan found the Nether race hidden underground.

To Li Fan's surprise, there were no Myriad Immortals Alliance troops in this small world.

The number of this Nether race tribe was also very small, less than a hundred.

The tribe was not as robust and healthy as those Li Fan had seen before.

They were all emaciated, as if they could die at any moment.

After Li Fan inquired, he vaguely understood.

This Nether race tribe had fled from their original homeland.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance had captured the Nether race, and they had desperately escaped, finding this hiding place.

"This is even better."

Li Fan no longer hesitated. Unleashing his full power, in coordination with Tian Yang, he intended to suppress these Nether race members into his own Grotto-Heaven.

However, something Li Fan had not anticipated occurred.

Facing Li Fan's attack, these Nether race members, who appeared to possess no supernatural aura, erupted with a peculiar power.

The elder of the tribe, though startled, did not panic.

Chanting loudly, a strange fluctuation instantly enveloped everyone.

Before Li Fan's eyes, he instantly lost track of them.

It wasn't some illusion technique; their attack had genuinely missed its mark.

"Hmm? Interesting."

At that moment, Li Fan clearly felt the fluctuations of the power of darkness.

"You can run, but you can't hide."

When entering this small world, Li Fan had already sealed the exit using formations.

Without his permission, no one could leave this world.

His divine sense swept through the surroundings, searching the entire small world, yet he still could not find the hidden Nether race members.

Li Fan then resorted to indiscriminate attacks.

Destructive black light rained down from the sky, striking every inch of the land.

Countless lives were affected.

Li Fan remained expressionless, cleansing every part of this small world.

Under this large-scale, comprehensive cleansing, the Nether race members finally revealed a flaw.

Sensing something resisting his Great Five Elements Annihilation Sword, Li Fan's eyes flashed with a sharp light.

He instantly sealed the area layer by layer with formations.

Under duress, the Nether race members finally revealed themselves.

They huddled together, looking up at Li Fan in the sky.

There was fear and hatred in their eyes.

The elder at the forefront finally couldn't help but speak: "Immortal Master, why must you be so ruthless?"

"Exploring the sacred land, the number of captured tribesmen you already have is definitely sufficient."

"I believe you are mistaken. I am not part of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. On the contrary, like you, I have an irreconcilable hatred for the Myriad Immortals Alliance." Li Fan declared loudly.

"Otherwise, with your meager strength, could you have survived under my hand?"

With that, Li Fan immediately unleashed the Soul Burning technique with all his might.

The five Grotto-Heavens shone with an eerie beauty under the blood-red light.

Coupled with the enhancement from the Celestial Puppet Tian Yang, the strength Li Fan displayed at this moment was comparable to that of a Longevity Realm cultivator.

The small world itself, unable to contain his power, developed dark spatial cracks.

Heaven and earth trembled and gradually disintegrated.

The mere aura emanating from him caused scenes resembling the apocalypse.

This threw the Nether race members below into extreme panic.

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance is currently exploring your sacred land. I wish to take this opportunity to assassinate them covertly."

"Are you willing to lend me a hand?" Li Fan asked coldly.

There was no other option. Furthermore, coupled with their hatred for the Myriad Immortals Alliance, the Nether race members below quickly chose to surrender.

Bringing them back to the Spirit Wood Realm smoothly, as per custom, they were supposed to pay respects to the Faceless True Immortal.

However, these Nether race members seemed to have seen something terrifying, collapsing to the ground, trembling uncontrollably.

Chapter 1098: The Tides of Darkness Surge

Seeing the abnormality of these Nether race members, Li Fan remained unfazed. Disregarding their extreme fear, he forced them to complete the oath of joining the United Front before the statue of the Faceless True Immortal.

Then, after they finally calmed down, Li Fan inquired about the reason for their extreme fear.

The Nether race leader, trembling, took a long time before finally managing to explain: "We have never had the fortune to see the True Immortal statue before. However, the moment we saw it, our tribesmen instinctively felt boundless fear."

"We have lived in darkness for generations, and our bodies have adapted to the special environment there. In normal daylight, we can still persist for a period, but before the True Immortal statue..."

"It's like being in complete darkness, and a light source a thousand times brighter than the sun suddenly appears."

The Nether race leader spoke intermittently, but Li Fan understood his meaning.

Just as ordinary mortals would feel fear when facing an abyss, the Nether race members felt extreme fear when seeing the statue of the Faceless True Immortal, as if facing a fatal threat.

However, the True Immortal's web was formless and intangible. Even Li Fan, if not an agent of the Faceless True Immortal in the Xuanhuang Realm, would likely not have sensed its existence.

In contrast, these Nether race members, even the children born recently, invariably sensed the power of the True Immortal.

"It seems this has something to do with the power of darkness they wield."

Next, Li Fan learned from the Nether race leader about their understanding of darkness.

The Nether race members were, in fact, originally human.

According to their ancient legends, in the primordial era, their world still had blue skies, white clouds, and bright sunlight.

But one day, after the sun set, it never rose again.

People despaired in the darkness, begging for a miracle, but it never came.

The vast majority of people disappeared forever into the darkness.

And those who survived were, without exception, those favored by the power of darkness.

Under the erosion and transformation of the power of darkness, their bodies gradually changed.

They transformed into terrifying forms with no heads, their facial features crowded onto their chests.

In reality, the Nether race members did not understand the essence of the power of darkness. They merely treated it as their only lifeline, worshipping it as a terrifying evil god that brought doom to the normal world, praying to it.

And this power of darkness seemed to understand their words, responding to them and becoming usable by them.

The Nether race members did not believe they had mastered the power of darkness, but rather considered it a gift from the great Dark God.

...

What the Nether race leader said differed from Transmitter Zhou's explanation.

The Nether race members were supposedly natives of the dark realm, yet Transmitter Zhou claimed they were merely a special race that discovered and utilized the power of the dark realm.

On minor matters like this, Transmitter Zhou likely had no reason to deceive him.

"It seems the Myriad Immortals Alliance's discovery of the dark realm was not as simple as he glossed over."

A cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

Next, he pondered the manifestation of the power of darkness.

"Praying, and then awaiting a response?"

"No wonder the passage to opening the entrance to the dark realm also involved a ritual of song and dance."

Li Fan's eyes flickered.

The power that could respond to a cultivator's inner stirrings was not unfamiliar to Li Fan.

The golden Origin Force Essence was the residual power left behind by True Immortals in their pursuit of the Dao, a being called the Flower of Dao.

"These two can sense each other. Perhaps there is a connection between them."

WWW. c o

According to the Nether race leader's introduction, although the power of darkness only materialized in their homeland, it was actually ubiquitous throughout the Xuanhuang Realm, just not concretely condensed, making it difficult for ordinary people to detect. However, through special methods of prayer and invocation, its power could be accessed across the barriers between small worlds.

Under Li Fan's observation, the Nether race leader, with a devout expression, chanted incantations towards a fierce exotic beast resembling a lion-tiger.

This lion-tiger was a new breed recently cultivated by the Empire, its body as hard as steel. Even a full-powered strike from an ordinary Foundation Establishment cultivator could barely inflict a scratch.

But a extremely bizarre scene occurred.

Without any warning, the once majestic lion-tiger suddenly went limp in all four limbs and collapsed onto the ground.

Its eyes were filled with terror, feebly trying to struggle to its feet.

But beneath it, it was as if there was an invisible mire, and countless hands were pulling at it.

Under Li Fan's gaze, the lion-tiger slowly vanished into the darkness, leaving no trace of its remains.

From beginning to end, Li Fan did not "see" the presence of darkness.

But the lion-tiger had indeed disappeared right before his eyes.

Li Fan carefully examined the ground where the darkness had appeared, but there were no residual power traces.

"Unpredictable and unavoidable," Li Fan stroked his chin, falling into deep thought.

The Nether race members, however, collectively closed their eyes and began to pray again.

"It seems only they can elicit a response from the darkness through prayer like this. Even if ordinary humans resemble them, they cannot invoke the power of darkness."

"This is understandable. Only by joining our Myriad Realms United Front and passing the oath before the True Immortal statue, joining the True Immortal's web, can their prayers be sensed by me. It is likely that the power of darkness also has such an invisible web."

Li Fan pondered inwardly: "So the key is, how to join this web without being devoured by the darkness?"

The bizarre appearance of Mo Rubin's remains in the dark realm was still fresh in his memory. Just the physical contact had led to such a fate. It was difficult to imagine surviving by immersing one's body and soul entirely into the darkness.

Subsequently, Li Fan's subordinates' attempts to emulate the Nether race in communicating with the darkness also proved his hypothesis.

Silently, they were swallowed by the darkness. No bodies were found, dead or alive.

And frequently invoking the power of darkness in a short period seemed to have caused some subtle changes.

As the master of the Spirit Wood Realm, Li Fan vaguely felt that the entire world had darkened for a moment.

After confirming with the Nether race leader, Li Fan knew this was not his hallucination.

The power of darkness was indeed flowing towards this place.

Li Fan decisively halted the experiments for the time being.

After inquiring with the Nether race members for a long time, Li Fan finally gained a general understanding of the current situation of the power of darkness in the Xuanhuang Realm.

It was like an ocean of darkness gathered on the "back" of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Although it was fixed in place by some mysterious power, the pervasive nature of darkness caused it to sometimes flow through any possible "gaps," invading the Xuanhuang Realm, and even various small worlds.

Infiltrating, and eventually returning to the dark realm.

This cycled back and forth, forming something akin to "tides."

Chapter 1099: Stealing Darkness, Seeking Survival

"The more frequently the power of darkness is invoked, the more gaps are created. The possibility of darkness invading also increases," Li Fan analyzed the characteristics of the power of darkness calmly.

It was imaginable that if the mysterious power fixing the ocean of darkness did not exist, the Xuanhuang Realm would have long been riddled with holes by these tides of darkness.

"The existence of the Immortal Ruins created the ocean of darkness. Then what is it that, without anyone's awareness, eliminates this potential crisis?"

Recalling Mo Rubin's desperate efforts to enter the dark realm, Li Fan was almost certain that something related to Xuan Tian King must be there.

Perhaps it was his residual power.

Or perhaps...

It was him himself.

From the Nether race, Li Fan selected three young descendants and ordered them to impart the ritual for communicating with the power of darkness separately.

Li Fan, however, led by the Nether race chief and over a dozen strong tribesmen, left the Spirit Wood Realm.

The existence of the dark tides meant that darkness would inevitably invade. Li Fan naturally would not perform the ritual in his own home.

Fortunately, he knew of many unclaimed small worlds.

Half a day later, Li Fan chose a suitable one and infiltrated it.

This small world had no ground.

Only continuous underground caves. The only source of light was the occasional moss growing on the cave walls.

It was quite suitable for the Nether race to live in.

Urged by Fang Zaiji, the Nether race chief began the ritual to open the passage to the dark realm.

Then, Li Fan ordered him to lead the way.

Li Fan himself, along with Tian Yang, Hermit Gigao, Liu Ruchen, and Fang Zaiji, five people, held hands tightly and followed closely behind.

Once again entering the boundless dark world.

Li Fan had already adapted somewhat.

Gigao and the others, however, clearly exhibited signs of tension and fear.

Even though they had heard about it beforehand and were psychologically prepared,

Experiencing it firsthand made it difficult for them to escape these emotions.

The interconnected group communicated via divine sense.

"Can you sense the presence of the Myriad Immortals Alliance members here?" Li Fan asked the Nether race chief.

He received a negative reply.

"The power of darkness is too profound. Even we who live here find it difficult to see clearly. Moreover, I haven't been home for a long time. Envoy, please allow me to adapt for a while..."

Li Fan's eyes immediately became wary as he heard this.

Fortunately, it was just his overthinking.

After a while, the Nether race chief finally managed to discern their general direction.

"Follow me. Our former residence is not far away. If the Myriad Immortals Alliance members have set up a camp here, they would surely choose that location."

They traveled for an unknown amount of time in the darkness.

The Nether race chief suddenly stopped.

"There are indeed people, quite a few. The sea of darkness has been affected, emitting chaotic fluctuations," he explained to Li Fan and the others, his voice filled with hatred.

At this moment, Li Fan noticed.

The strange pulsation he felt from Mo Rubin's corpse last time seemed to have disappeared.

And in the darkness, position could not be discerned.

"It seems we have to find clues from this Myriad Immortals Alliance outpost," Li Fan thought.

"Can you determine how many people are inside?"

The Nether race chief sensed for a moment.

"There should be around five. As for their strength... similar to this one..."

He was referring to Liu Ruchen among them.

"You can actually discern our strength?" Fang Zaiji asked with some curiosity.

"Outside, naturally not. But here in the sea of darkness, it's effortless for us Nether race members," the Nether race chief replied somewhat proudly.

"It's like items of different weights causing different changes when placed in water. He likely judged it based on this," Hermit Gigao explained, looking at the boundless darkness around them.

Fang Zaiji then realized.

"Can you see what the Myriad Immortals Alliance members are doing inside?" Li Fan frowned and asked.

"We need to get a little closer."

After a moment of thought, Li Fan agreed to his request: "Don't push yourself. It's not the time to confront the Myriad Immortals Alliance head-on."

Having fought against the Myriad Immortals Alliance before, the Nether race chief naturally understood the terrifying strength of their opponents.

He indicated his understanding and then cautiously moved forward step by step.

"What is this..."

"How dare they!"

The Nether race chief's emotions suddenly fluctuated violently.

Fortunately, being in the sea of darkness, they were not discovered by the Myriad Immortals Alliance members.

The Nether race chief shared the scene he perceived.

Several white figures formed a circle.

In their center, there seemed to be a small vortex formed by the power of darkness.

This vortex was very small, less than the size of a palm.

Its appearance was peculiar, with the center vortex pointing upwards, the reverse of ordinary everyday occurrences.

However, the several Dao Integration cultivators guarding it appeared extremely nervous.

"What is this?" Fang Zaiji asked with confusion.

"They are stealing the great power of darkness!" the Nether race chief gritted his teeth.

Li Fan and the others were all startled.

"Even with the limitations of the sea of darkness itself, it cannot stop these despicable thieves!" The Nether race chief wished he could rush over immediately and stop the Myriad Immortals Alliance's actions.

Fortunately, he still possessed some reason and only spoke his mind, not acting on it.

"What do you all think?"

Looking at the scene in his mind, Li Fan asked the others.

"The power of darkness deviates from the Immortal Ruins. It is clear that the Myriad Immortals Alliance is not satisfied with just the meager outward seepage during the tide; they want to draw the power of darkness on a large scale."

"It seems they ultimately couldn't resist the temptation of escaping the Immortal Ruins." Liu Ruchen, who had received Li Fan's intel, couldn't help but sigh faintly.

"I just wonder how they managed to create this vortex. It couldn't be that they specifically used a small world to attract the power of darkness, could it..." Fang Zaiji said casually.

As soon as he finished speaking, he himself froze.

"That's not impossible. It's just a small world with no special value. If it could draw such a massive amount of the power of darkness, it would be worth destroying it," Hermit Gigao stated with certainty.

"Envoy, perhaps we can also emulate the Myriad Immortals Alliance," he even suggested Li Fan do the same.

"I have a hunch that combining this power of darkness with Origin Force Essence and using it on Celestial Puppets might allow us to further advance and create true True Immortal puppets," Hermit Gigao's tone revealed a hint of fanaticism.

Although Li Fan had similar thoughts, he did not agree immediately.

Instead, he asked the Nether race chief if he could sense any residual corpses of cultivators in the vicinity.

"Huh? If the envoy hadn't mentioned it, I would hardly have noticed."

"But this doesn't seem like a corpse."

"It's more like an empty shell."

Chapter 1100: An Old Acquaintance as a Celestial Puppet

"Even our people, after dying in the sea of darkness, do not achieve such a state."

"It's too light, too light."

After the Nether race chief's explanation, Li Fan suddenly understood.

It was still based on the fluctuations caused by being in the sea of darkness.

Mo Rubin's corpse did not exhibit the normal characteristics of a deceased being.

"Either it's just an empty shell used as a diversion, or..."

"This person was deeply favored by the darkness. After his death, most of the spiritual energy within his body immediately returned to the sea of darkness, leaving only the decaying parts to slowly merge into the darkness," the Nether race chief offered another possibility.

"However, even the most powerful cultivator in our tribe's history, after death, did not reach this state. Therefore, I am more inclined to believe that what we are seeing is merely an empty shell."

Li Fan's eyes flickered.

When he heard the Nether race chief's words just now, he couldn't help but feel a shock. But if the power of darkness here was linked to Xuan Tian King, then Mo Rubin's anomaly after death could be explained.

"However, we cannot let our guard down. The Xuan Tian Sect is extraordinarily cunning, with endless tricks up their sleeves. We must remain vigilant."

"Regardless of whether he is truly dead or not, my plan will not change because of it."

A thought flashed through his mind, and Li Fan inquired further about the details of Mo Rubin's corpse.

The location where Li Fan had seen him not long ago was clearly not here.

He hadn't expected the Myriad Immortals Alliance to find a method to resist the contagion of darkness in such a short time and transfer him here.

"If it were truly just a worthless empty shell, the Myriad Immortals Alliance wouldn't have gone to such great lengths to move it. In my opinion, the vortex the Myriad Immortals Alliance is using to steal the darkness is likely stabilized by Mo Rubin's corpse," Hermit Gigao offered his perspective.

"This power of darkness has a similar nature to Origin Force Essence. Under normal circumstances, with the vast scale of the sea of darkness, if such a small outlet were to appear, it would undoubtedly form an unimaginable energy vortex. But here, it's too calm."

Hermit Gigao spoke with conviction. The Nether race chief was taken aback.

He observed carefully for a long time before saying with some surprise, "Envoy, this Celestial Master is right! The power of darkness, which should have been wild, has become stable after being filtered and influenced by that empty shell!"

"Even the darkness can be soothed, what exactly..." The Nether race chief's tone was astonished and uncertain.

Li Fan fell into deep thought upon hearing this.

If the dark realm was indeed related to Xuan Tian King, then besides his former companions from the Xuan Tian Sect, the only other thing that might attract his special attention would be...

Perhaps the statue of the Faceless True Immortal.

However, it was not yet certain what kind of disturbance the True Immortal statue would cause if it appeared in the dark realm, so Li Fan needed to consider carefully whether to do so.

The main objective of this trip was still to study this mysterious power of darkness and gather information about Mo Rubin.

"Is it possible for us to get close to this location and secretly open a rift connected to a small world?" Li Fan asked. "With Mo Rubin's corpse acting as a buffer, the disturbance should not be too significant."

The Nether race chief pondered for a moment and gave an affirmative reply.

"However, it's best not to stir up too much power of darkness, otherwise, two vortexes of the same size might interact and gradually approach each other, forming one large entity."

"Mm, we are only drawing a small amount for research. We won't be too greedy."

With Li Fan's decision, the group immediately took action.

Led by their chief, the Nether race members, almost right beside the Myriad Immortals Alliance's stronghold, secretly opened another spatial passage.

This was their original homeland, and with Li Fan and the others using their respective abilities to mask the fluctuations, the process went quite smoothly, without being discovered by the Myriad Immortals Alliance members from start to finish.
