Of course, this might also be due to their complete focus on guarding the giant vortex.

"Truly wondrous. The surging sea of darkness has become so calm here." Witnessing this miraculous scene firsthand, the Nether race chief couldn't help but sigh with admiration.

And on the other side of the passage, in the underground world.

The power of darkness, once released from the containment, regained its original nature.

At a terrifying speed, it surged outwards, engulfing everything.

The last vestiges of light in the underground world quickly disappeared completely.

Countless beings perished silently and inexplicably.

Fortunately, the scale of this underground small world was not too large.

After quickly filling it, the power of darkness began to flow back towards the dark realm.

It truly resembled the ebb and flow of tides.

And at the entrance of the underground world connected to the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan keenly detected the infiltration of darkness.

However, they had not yet opened the passage, so this process was extremely slow.

"If we have to enter and exit through here, it won't be long before the overflowing darkness is detected by the Myriad Immortals Alliance," Liu Ruchen frowned.

"I'll figure something out," Hermit Gigao volunteered. "Origin Force Essence and the power of darkness are incompatible. Perhaps we can build a buffer zone here. Of course, this might require a large amount of Origin Force Essence."

Hermit Gigao said this while unconsciously looking at Li Fan.

Li Fan was not particularly tempted by this remnant of True Immortal power. He had accumulated a considerable amount during this period, and it had no particular use.

However, after feigning deep thought for a long time, he reluctantly agreed.

Hermit Gigao was overjoyed upon seeing this and immediately set to work, even summoning his beloved creation to assist.

A female celestial puppet, as beautiful as a celestial being, was completely obedient to Gigao.

She used the same technology as the Celestial Puppet Tian Yang. It was unknown where Gigao had obtained the consciousness and personality of the celestial puppet.

Or perhaps Gigao, while building the "buffer zone," boasted and casually revealed her origin.

"Back then, when the [Ancestor] collapsed, I barely managed to survive the calamity and escape my homeland. But some individuals were not as fortunate. Their bodies were destroyed in the disaster, and only their consciousness backups were preserved, which I carried with me."

"Don't let her current obedience fool you; she used to scold me quite a bit! Hahaha!"

"I used to prepare a puppet body for her when I was in the Heavenly Spirit Sect. But it was too rigid, and I didn't like it. I lost interest after playing with it for a short while and dismantled it."

"Unlike this one, she is lifelike and almost indistinguishable from a real person."

Chapter 1101: Scheming Against a True Immortal in the Dark

"Oh, and I even kept the memories from when I dismantled her previous body, and added them when creating her new body..."

"You should have seen her expression when she first woke up."

Hermit Gigao spoke with increasing excitement.

As the golden buffer zone was gradually completed, the surrounding area became brighter. He could see the gazes of those around him fixed on him, making him even more smug.

"I should have realized it sooner. Since you can copy and back up your own consciousness, it shouldn't be a problem to preserve the consciousness backups of other cultivators from the Heavenly Mystery Realm," Li Fan's cold voice suddenly interrupted, causing Gigao to freeze instantly.

"Cultivators from the Heavenly Mystery Realm are all unparalleled refining geniuses. Our United Front is in urgent need of talent. How can you keep this to yourself? You must hand them all over, and I will overlook this matter. Otherwise..."

Gigao felt the killing intent emanating from Li Fan, and his heart pounded.

He felt as if an invisible giant hand was tightly gripping his neck, making it impossible to breathe.

Moreover, with this tightening sensation, it continued to grow stronger.

He felt like an insect caught in a net, unable to break free, only able to await his doom in vain.

Gigao knew this was the power of the Red Dust Compassionate Immortal.

After he recited the oath to join, he had fallen into the True Immortal's net. Unless he could surpass Li Fan in strength, Li Fan, as his superior envoy, could obliterate him with a single thought through this connection alone.

Fortunately, Li Fan did not intend to kill him here.

As Gigao's consciousness began to blur, the constricting sensation instantly disappeared.

Regaining his life, Gigao gasped for breath, wiping the cold sweat from his forehead, and repeatedly explained, "It's just Elder Council's core members."

"I was in a hurry when I fled, so I could only take this much."

"The power of darkness is mysterious and unpredictable. Let them out later to study it together," Li Fan said calmly.

Gigao naturally could only agree.

After being startled by Li Fan once, Gigao became much more obedient.

Three days later, the golden buffer zone was completed.

Looking at the thick darkness not far away, completely blocked outside, everyone couldn't help but marvel at the divine power of the Red Dust Compassionate Immortal once again.

Although the power of darkness was strong, it was still no match for True Immortals.

Although a buffer had been built, there was still a risk of the power of darkness getting out of control.

Li Fan did not intend to bring it back to the Spirit Wood Realm for research.

Instead, he established a separate research facility in this underground world.

The four elders from the Heavenly Mystery Realm were also released by Gigao.

It was then that Li Fan learned that the stunningly beautiful female celestial puppet was actually Shangguan Tuo, the former chief elder of the Heavenly Mystery Realm whom Gigao had mentioned earlier.

Shangguan Tuo had once attempted to gain complete control over the [Ancestor], taking a risky gamble by integrating her divine soul into the [Ancestor]'s damaged core. Before doing so, she had naturally made a backup of her consciousness.

However, her reckless action had nearly led to the collapse of the entire Heavenly Mystery Realm, a truly heinous crime.

Therefore, the elders at that time had vetoed the proposal to reawaken Shangguan Tuo.

They had merely hidden her consciousness backup deep within.

Finally, before the destruction of the Heavenly Mystery Realm, Gigao took it out.

What surprised Li Fan even more was that Shangguan Tuo was actually Gigao's master.

Looking at everyone's gazes, Gigao's expression remained normal, showing no signs of abnormality.

And the remaining three elders of the Heavenly Mystery Realm also remained silent regarding Gigao's actions, which could be considered a betrayal of his master.

After Li Fan inquired if Shangguan Tuo wished to seek freedom, he received a negative answer.

This made Li Fan somewhat curious.

He glanced at Gigao, who shivered and hurriedly explained, "This actually has little to do with me."

"They are, after all, just consciousness backups. To prevent the situation of two 'me's' from fighting each other, their subjective initiative has been suppressed, and they cannot be considered completely equivalent to their original personalities. Only the Great Elder knows how to lift the restrictions."

"This is also a safeguard implemented by our Heavenly Mystery Realm to prevent anyone from widely using consciousness backups and endangering the world's safety."

"As for myself, since the Heavenly Mystery Realm is gone, I naturally have fewer scruples." Gigao's tone couldn't hide his smugness.

"So, are they considered second-class citizens of the Heavenly Mystery Realm, and thus must obey you, the first-class citizen?" Fang Zaiji asked, stroking his chin.

Gigao nodded.

However, upon seeing Li Fan's expression, he immediately patted his chest and guaranteed, "Envoy, please rest assured. Although they consider themselves my inferiors, their research talent is no different from the main body. With the combined efforts of the few of us, I believe it won't be difficult to research the usage of the power of darkness."

"Then I leave it to you."

Li Fan couldn't be bothered with the internal affairs of the Heavenly Mystery Realm.

As long as they could be of use to him, that was sufficient.

After assigning the task, Li Fan returned alone to the underground world.

Alone, enveloped by darkness.

Li Fan felt no fear, only quietly perceiving his surroundings.

"Just as I thought. In the darkness, even the influence of the Faceless True Immortal is greatly weakened."

"Although I cannot completely escape it, for me, it is practically a sanctuary."

"In the depths of the dark realm, I can activate True Return and leave at any time."

With this thought, the threat that had long weighed heavily on Li Fan's heart finally lessened considerably.

"But passive avoidance is useless."

"After making so many preparations in this life, I have a high degree of confidence in safely retreating amidst the confrontation between the Immortal Ruins' immortals and the Faceless True Immortal."

"What choice should I make?"

Li Fan, in a rare moment of calm, pondered alone.

The darkness acted like a protective umbrella, isolating everything, allowing Li Fan to feel an unprecedented sense of relaxation.

"The power of the Faceless True Immortal has always remained in the Xuanhuang Realm. It doesn't mean that as long as I don't provoke it, I can avoid it."

"Once I reach a certain level of cultivation, it is bound to attract its attention. This is an unchangeable fact."

"Unless I can find a way to safely escape the Xuanhuang Realm."

"But beyond the high wall, True Immortals still exist."

"There is no escape..."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

"When facing True Immortals, sometimes being weak is an advantage."

"One can observe carefully while being overlooked by them."

Li Fan looked again at the deep darkness around him.

"Like this darkness. If there is something in the darkness staring at me, and its strength is far weaker than mine, posing no threat to me..."

"Then how could I possibly discover it?"

Chapter 1102: All Essences Gathered

The research on the power of darkness by the Heavenly Mystery Realm group did not proceed as smoothly as expected.

It was understandable, after all, it was a power level comparable to Origin Force Essence. Even the most gifted individuals would undoubtedly require a significant amount of time to complete research from scratch. Fortunately, Hermit Gigao and the others were research fanatics. Since their research began, they had been completely engrossed, with no distractions. Li Fan only needed to wait patiently and enjoy the results.

Meanwhile, Li Fan had quietly begun plotting against the two immortals.

In a secret chamber within the Spirit Wood Realm.

Over a hundred uniquely shaped puppets stood motionless.

Li Fan, with a solemn expression, personally carved formations onto them.

"Bait Puppets. Two are grouped together, totaling seventy-two groups. One from each group will fly into the Immortal Ruins, while the other will be placed in various corners of the Xuanhuang Realm's leylines. When the seventy-two bait puppets fly towards the Immortal Ruins, the formations on them will activate, attracting the attention of the immortals in the Immortal Ruins."

"This formation was derived by the Disintegration Disc and is infinitely close to the celestial-grade formation level. It is named [Bewildering: Flowers Bloom in Illusion]. Upon suddenly sensing a threat during seclusion, they will instinctively react, thereby tracing back to the Xuanhuang Realm."

"And by the side of these bait puppets left in the Xuanhuang Realm, I will lay down a vigilance net using the Origin Force Essence of the Faceless True Immortal. Once the power of the Immortal Ruins' immortals triggers it, it will attract the attention of the Faceless True Immortal."

"If nothing unexpected happens..."

"Once these two unimaginably powerful forces clash, the Xuanhuang Realm will likely be instantly annihilated. Therefore, my plan to deceive the Heavenly Dao and preemptively act on the changes in Xuanhuang needs to be prepared in advance."

The Dao Transformation Stone in Li Fan's mind emitted a blinking blue light.

The enhanced Dao Transformation Stone’s deduction capabilities had been greatly improved. This move of using one wolf to drive away another, involving numerous aspects and variables, did not place too much burden on the Dao Transformation Stone, even with all the complexities.

Of course, this was only because the Faceless True Immortal and the Immortal Ruins' immortals in the deduction only possessed the abilities Li Fan had pre-set.

Li Fan was self-aware; with his current strength, attempting to deduce the actions of True Immortals was akin to dreaming. All he could do was seek a glimmer of hope based on the reality he had already experienced.

"Immortal Ruins' immortals shake the True Immortal's net."

"I will then seize the opportunity to activate True Return and escape in one fell swoop."

"Of course, this is the most ideal scenario. As the saying goes, plan for defeat before victory. I must also consider that if my plan fails, and the power gap between the Immortal Ruins' immortals and the Faceless True Immortal is too large to shake the shackles of the True Immortal's net..."

"Then I must immediately return to the depths of the dark realm and activate True Return to escape the crisis."

"Now that I possess several items that can at least slightly affect a True Immortal, delaying them for a moment should still be possible."

Li Fan examined his own divine soul.

The silver light defense gifted by Heavenly Physician, the golden Origin Force Essence, and the seven-colored divine light wrapped in gray mold...

Various different powers maintained a delicate balance.

Perhaps only someone like Li Fan could remain completely calm under such circumstances, even feeling a sense of peace.

"Borrowing strength to fight, maneuvering between powers. Ultimately, it all comes down to insufficient personal strength. But is the threshold of immortality so easily crossed?"

"Geniuses like Xuan Tian King, Transmitter, and Heavenly Physician are all blocked outside, unable to make any progress."

"Let alone me? If not for possessing True Return, I would have likely given up on this seemingly unrealistic fantasy long ago," Li Fan chuckled self-deprecatingly.

"But since I am fortunate enough to encounter the wondrous item [True Return], no one can stop my path to becoming an immortal..." A cold glint flashed in his eyes.

Li Fan knew that whether it was [Chaos], [Hunger], or [Nonexistence], what he saw were not the original versions.

But rather clumsy imitations by later generations.

Therefore, Li Fan had never given up on deeply studying these three True Immortal runes for a long time.

Even imperfect imitations, the more they resembled the original, the stronger their power became.

Even immortals could achieve enlightenment by comprehending one of these runes. It could be said that any one of these three would consume Li Fan's entire life to fully comprehend.

Li Fan's comprehension was limited, but he could borrow external means.

Besides his clone Li Qing's peerless talent, the prodigies of the Xuanhuang Realm, whom he had tricked and subverted into joining the [Mountain River Xuan] in recent times, had also become Li Fan's resources.

Using the Xuan Tian Sect cultivation technique, the Heaven and Earth Intercourse Harmony, obtained from Senior Sister Zhao, he could harmonize the talents and comprehension of any subject.

After his clone Li Qing achieved minor success, she began selecting suitable subjects.

They were ostensibly sent out on secret missions for the Red Dust Compassionate Immortal, but in reality, they were secretly controlled, and their talents were extracted.

Of course, due to the Intercourse and Harmony technique, these prodigies also received half of Li Qing's talent bonus.

Li Qing's talent was not inferior to theirs, so the prodigies of the Mountain River Xuan, including Shang Tianci, did not perceive anything unusual. They only marveled at the divine efficacy of the "Foundation Building Through Myself" method.

With the talent boost from over a dozen prodigies, Clone Li Qing's comprehension had reached an astonishing level.

She even became aware of Li Fan's act of selectively erasing some of his memories.

But she was, after all, a clone, with no distinction between herself and the main body. She resolutely carried out the task of comprehending the True Immortal runes.

The three True Immortal runes continuously appeared in her mind, as if alive.

Li Qing's eyes seemed to witness the act of a blurred figure transforming the Dao into runes.

"Altar of Dao..."

"An existence even more powerful than the Faceless True Immortal. Perhaps that is my ultimate goal."

...

Just as Li Fan was secretly preparing for the grand plan of this era,

The Reversed Life and Death Heavenly Venerate, who had emerged previously, finally revealed his influence on the Xuanhuang Realm.

It was discovered that after this Heavenly Venerate descended, no new offspring had been born to cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Or rather, this was true for the entire human race.

Initially, people couldn't be sure if it was the Heavenly Venerate's influence.

But when a previously deceased cultivator returned in a way no one had ever imagined, everyone instantly connected the dots.

The Canglang River, the largest river on the southwestern border of the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

A cultivator named Chang Ji, one day, emerged naked from the river.

This unusual scene naturally attracted the attention of onlookers.

But Chang Ji didn't care, looking at his own body with ecstatic disbelief, muttering, "I'm alive again?"

"Reversing life and death, reversing life and death, the Heavenly Venerate truly deceived me!"

Chapter 1103: The Xuanhuang River of Rebirth

Chang Ji, disregarding the strange looks from the onlookers, respectfully bowed to the heavens.

He then transformed into an escape light and flew away.

His parting words immediately caught the attention of those with keen intentions. After some investigation, people finally discovered that this Chang Ji should have died completely a year ago. While exploring the ruins of an outer sect, he unfortunately triggered a defensive formation, resulting in his body being utterly destroyed on the spot. More than a dozen companions from that expedition could testify to this, and it was no fabrication! And now, this Chang Ji had actually been resurrected! The resurrection occurred precisely in the largest river closest to his place of death!

This horrifying discovery quickly spread throughout the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Soon, Chang Ji's former friends rushed to find him, wanting to confirm the reality of his disappearance. Chang Ji himself did not deny it; instead, he generously admitted that he had been resurrected. "All thanks to the Heavenly Venerate's divine power!" he added piously in front of everyone. In the past, when cultivators in the Myriad Immortals Alliance spoke of a Heavenly Venerate, they invariably referred to the Heavenly Venerate of Preaching the Dao. However, from Chang Ji's mouth, everyone knew he was referring to the Heavenly Venerate of Longevity, who had reversed life and death without anyone noticing.

Seeing that his friends and relatives were still somewhat skeptical, Chang Ji directly invited them into his Heavenly Profound Mirror space. As is well known, the Heavenly Profound Mirror space is bound to a cultivator and can only be opened by the cultivator themselves. With the Heavenly Profound Mirror as proof, everyone finally completely believed in Chang Ji's true identity. To die and be resurrected, and by no means an isolated case. This shocking news soon became common knowledge. In the following days, the appearance of more and more resurrected cultivators further validated its authenticity.

Based on their findings, after their resurrection, cultivators in the Myriad Immortals Alliance invariably reappeared from the river closest to their place of death. There were fifty-four rivers of rebirth within the Alliance's territory. As for the Five Elders Society, they also seemed to have a corresponding fifty-four rivers. These one hundred and eight rivers formed the Xuanhuang Realm’s rivers of rebirth. The duration of a cultivator's resurrection seemed to be related to their strength in life. The stronger the cultivation level, the longer the time required for resurrection. The first batch of resurrected cultivators were, without exception, only at the Foundation Establishment stage or below. As for how long it would take for cultivators of higher realms to resurrect, that would require further verification.

After resurrection, they always appeared naked. Possessions carried before death, even those hidden within their divine souls, would not reappear with them. However, being able to reclaim one's life was already a great blessing. These external possessions were not something anyone dwelled on too much. Resurrected cultivators appeared to be the same age as they were before death. However, after detailed measurements, it was discovered that the resurrected body seemed to be one year younger than before their demise.

Not only cultivators, but all living beings within the Xuanhuang Realm, upon death, would be reborn from the rivers. Thus, people could constantly witness the strange sight of creatures emerging from the water and coming ashore in the rivers of rebirth. The rivers seemed to possess a magical power that protected newly resurrected beings, preventing them from drowning immediately after rebirth. However, this power disappeared quickly after leaving the rivers of rebirth, and even re-entering the water could not reveal its trace again.

...

The various miraculous aspects of dying and returning to life became the hottest topic of discussion among the cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Some felt fortunate, believing they no longer had to worry about perishing. Others, however, began to worry that if no new life were born, the future of the Xuanhuang Realm might be bleak. Fortunately, a discovery soon dispelled these concerns. In some states of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, new lives were still being born since the Heavenly Venerate reversed the principles of life and death. Their numbers were just extremely small, less than fifty in the entire Myriad Immortals Alliance per year. But at least the gestation of life had not completely ceased. Even if life were not completely extinguished from now on, an increase of fifty cultivators per year was not a significant issue for the Xuanhuang Realm.

Soon, the cultivators' attention shifted to other critical issues. For example, after dying once, could they resurrect again? How long would the second resurrection take? Were there truly no limits to the number of resurrections? And with each death and rebirth, their age reduced by one year, was there an upper limit to this?

...

That mysterious Heavenly Venerate, from beginning to end, never appeared to explain anything. All of this had to be explored by the cultivators themselves. These would become the rules that must be followed in the future, and cultivators naturally attached great importance to them. Soon, under the command of certain individuals, some recently resurrected cultivators were once again forced to sacrifice their lives to explore the mysteries of rebirth. Fortunately, knowing that they could die and be reborn, and having received promises of generous rewards, these cultivators used as experimental subjects did not harbor too many complaints. After all, they had already died once. They had no conscious awareness after death. One moment they closed their eyes, the next they opened them and were good as new. They could even receive rewards that they wouldn't have earned in a lifetime, so why not?

The secrets of rebirth would likely take some time to be deciphered. Li Fan, after hearing the news, personally went to investigate near one of the rivers of rebirth for a long time. Ultimately, he saw no clues. "Compared to the Hall of Rebirth I experienced before, the Way of Reversing Life and Death in this life is clearly more complete. To actually give birth to life out of thin air from a river... It is truly unimaginable." The principle of reversing life and death had already completely merged with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, making it impossible to distinguish them separately. Even Li Fan, who was proficient in formations, could not find any trace of the "Great Formation of Reversing Life and Death" he had seen before.

Fearing that this mysteriously appearing Heavenly Venerate might affect his grand plan, Li Fan secretly contacted Transmitter Zhou, attempting to glean some inside information from her. To his disappointment, Transmitter Zhou gave the same answer as before: she knew nothing about it. "As far as I know, your Myriad Immortals Alliance has an organization called the Heavenly Oversight Department, specifically monitoring the principles of the Xuanhuang Realm. This Heavenly Venerate has succeeded in reversing the principles for so long, yet you insist you were unaware... Daoist Zhou, this doesn't add up!" Li Fan questioned with a displeased tone.

Transmitter Zhou smiled slightly: "Your Myriad Realms United Front's intelligence is indeed well-informed. You can even keep secrets like the Alliance's Heavenly Oversight Department from your notice. However, I am not trying to deceive you; I genuinely do not know." The smile on Zhou's face gradually faded, and her expression became serious. "Generally speaking, for a cultivator at the Dao Integration stage to successfully reverse the principles, it is a gradual process. During this process, there are significant traces of distortion and change in the principles of heaven and earth, which is why the Heavenly Oversight Department could monitor the signs of the Heavenly Venerate of Longevity's imminent birth."

"But this Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth is different. The speed of His appearance... It was too fast!"

Chapter 1104: Heavenly Beings and Mortals Are Fundamentally Different

"From the appearance of traces of reversed principles of heaven and earth to the successful reversal and attainment of Dao Longevity, the entire process took less than ten years. Under normal circumstances, cultivators at the Dao Integration stage wouldn't even complete the first step of reversing the principles, yet this one had already finished the promotion." Transmitter Zhou's tone was somewhat horrified. "I almost suspect that this Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth might be an outsider, a great cultivator who was already very close to the Longevity realm. That's why everything went so smoothly."

"An outsider?" Li Fan pondered inexplicably upon hearing her words. "However, fortunately, this Heavenly Venerate seems to have no intention of interfering in the conflicts of the Xuanhuang Realm. Neither with us nor with the Five Elders Society has His Highness proactively made contact. As for the impact of reversing life and death, we are still assessing it. However, it is foreseeable that regarding the commencement of war, both sides might become increasingly cautious in the future." Li Fan nodded in agreement.

This might seem like an inexhaustible supply of manpower, with the ability to resurrect infinitely. However, the key issue was that resurrection required time. And the Xuanhuang Realm's capacity to gestate new life had been reduced to its absolute minimum. Any significant casualties would require a long period of recovery, and as the number of resurrections increased, the time required for each subsequent resurrection would likely grow longer. In the short term, there wouldn't be any major issues. But what if it continued over a long period...

Li Fan suddenly spoke, "Daoist Zhou, you don't need to worry too much. If I remember correctly, your Myriad Immortals Alliance has suppressed and eternally imprisoned many cultivators? At critical moments, you could release them to help tide things over." Li Fan was referring to the cultivators suppressed within the Eternal Immortal Wall by the Myriad Immortals Alliance. This included those whose bodies had been occupied by the million gods and demons summoned by him using the "Divine Method of Ten Thousand Calamities and Hundred Tribulations" previously. Although they had largely lost their self-awareness, becoming mere shells, they could still serve as cannon fodder.

Transmitter Zhou gazed at Li Fan for a moment and did not reply. She ended the conversation with a polite smile. "I always have a feeling that the identity of this Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth... Perhaps it can be jointly tested and verified in the next life. Let's not introduce unnecessary variables in this life." Li Fan's eyes flickered, and he returned to his preparations.

...

Time flew by, and in the blink of an eye, it was the 24th year of anchoring. By the Congyun Sea, Li Fan appeared silently and looked up. "Because I previously falsified the heavenly mandate, provoking the wrath of the Heavenly Dao consciousness, the calamity of the Scarlet Flame Burning Sea in this life has not only been advanced by three years, but the intensity of the scarlet flames has also been further increased." He squinted, looking at the scarlet figure that seemed to dance with the wind. It was still a blurry humanoid form, but unlike before, where it stood aloof, holding a flame. In this life, the Scarlet Flame sat cross-legged on clouds formed by flames, its eyes filled with murderous intent, staring down at the lives in the Congyun Sea. Wrapped around its body was a creature like a swimming dragon, also staring at the Congyun Sea below as if at prey.

Suddenly, as if sensing Li Fan's gaze, they both looked sharply in Li Fan’s direction. But Li Fan was covered by formations, making it impossible for them to detect him. "It's a brand new form I haven't seen before. It seems my gradual arrangements over the years have made the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao uneasy and vigilant," Li Fan said with a smile. "But unfortunately, as long as I don't initiate it, no one in this world can predict what I am plotting." "Your resistance is all in vain." Li Fan did not stop the process of the Scarlet Flame Burning Sea; he merely observed from the sidelines.

In this life, he had no intention of luring out Mo Sha. As the strongest in the essence of heaven and earth, once Mo Sha appeared, he would inevitably attract the attention of the Longevity Heavenly Venerates in the world. Even though Li Fan no longer feared them, the world-destroying preparations he was undertaking were not meant to be seen. To avoid affecting his plan of pitting one wolf against another, maintaining a low profile was paramount. Li Fan's reason for coming to the Congyun Sea today was to observe the specific changes that would occur in the Xuanhuang Realm during its self-purification process.

Having thoroughly studied Tianyi's "Book of Mending Heaven," Li Fan now had a completely new understanding of the event of the Scarlet Flame Burning Sea. The Congyun Sea originated from the Heavenly Law Realm and did not belong to the Xuanhuang Realm itself. During the fusion of the two realms, there were bound to be various "rejection" reactions. Representative of this were the various strange occurrences that frequently happened in different parts of the Congyun Sea. And the Scarlet Flame's seemingly world-destroying actions were, in fact, aimed at better promoting the fusion of the Congyun Sea and the Xuanhuang Realm.

"The same event, viewed from a human perspective versus a Heavenly Dao perspective, yields completely different outcomes." "There is no right or wrong." As the mutated Scarlet Flame slowly accumulated power, a layer of sealing force began to appear around the borders of the entire Congyun Sea, attempting to prevent any beings from escaping. And in the final moment before this heavenly prison was to take effect, Li Fan saw a group of people hurriedly arriving by boat from the sea. After finally reaching the shore, they hastily abandoned their boat and fled. The person leading them was someone Li Fan knew: Zhang Haobo!

In this life, Li Fan had no interaction with him. However, relying on a vague premonition in his heart and his own destiny, he managed to lead his friends and family to escape to this unfamiliar continent before the impending catastrophe. "Haobo, you say we were living well on Liuli Island. Why must we leave our homeland and come to this strange continent?" "Yes, boss. Although I will definitely believe in you and follow you forever, I still don't really understand."

Faced with the doubts of those around him, Zhang Haobo's expression did not change much. He simply unfurled a map, identified their location, and methodically directed everyone to continue their journey. As they walked, he said, "Haven't you noticed that some people seem to have disappeared from the island recently? Ever since those Immortal Masters from the Myriad Immortals Alliance visited." "It's not just our island; on other islands, and even the Immortal Masters themselves, are quietly evacuating the Congyun Sea." "It's clear that something big is about to happen," Zhang Haobo analyzed calmly. "Rather than waiting to die on the Congyun Sea, it's better to try our luck here."

The others, hearing this, still looked incredulous. Some even couldn't help but retort, "But didn't they say that under the coverage of the Heavenly Venerate's might, everyone can die and be reborn? Since we can resurrect, what is there to fear?" Zhang Haobo snorted coldly and did not explain. "Those who are willing to follow me, continue to do so. Those who are not, the boat is still by the sea, and you can return at any time." He said indifferently.

Hearing this, everyone fell silent, not daring to say more.

Chapter 1105: The Cycle of Xuanhuang's Destruction and Rebirth

Despite their doubts, they still had great faith in Zhang Haobo, who had repeatedly led them to survive terrifying storms. Not a single person chose to turn back; they all dutifully continued to follow, embarking on an unknown journey. Observing them from the shadows as they slowly departed, Li Fan fell into deep thought. "Even among mortals, there are those like Zhang Haobo who can sense danger before a catastrophe strikes." "Let alone the countless cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm." "It seems I may have been too optimistic. Although all my arrangements are sufficiently discreet, I cannot guarantee that there won't be individuals of destiny who discover something unusual by chance." "If you want to conceal something, the best method is to attract people's attention with something else."

Li Fan's eyes flickered, and he immediately had an idea. However, for now, he would quietly watch the grand spectacle of the Scarlet Flame Burning Sea play out. Not long after Zhang Haobo and his group departed. The Scarlet Flame, which had been sitting cross-legged, finally made its move. The Burning Dragon coiled around its body revealed an excited gaze, instantly transforming into countless streams of scarlet flame, raging towards every corner of the Congyun Sea. The seawater heated up at an incredibly rapid pace, and fear spread among the beings remaining in the Congyun Sea. Faced with a desperate situation, some cultivators fought back. But how could those at the peak of the Nascent Soul stage contend with the enhanced Scarlet Flame?

Li Fan's attention was not on the rapidly perishing lives. Instead, he silently observed the changes in heaven and earth itself. "New life from destruction." "Revival from desolation." The Scarlet Flame Burning Sea lasted for three full months. The ocean dried up, leaving thousands of miles of scorched earth, and the sea turned into a deep valley. But having witnessed all these scenes from beginning to end, Li Fan faintly perceived a hidden vitality within them. "This is the Cycle of Xuanhuang's Destruction and Rebirth." "By comprehending this, I can now be promoted to the Nascent Soul stage at any time. And, like my Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven at the Nascent Soul stage, once I am promoted, I will be the absolute strongest among Nascent Soul cultivators." "It's a pity..." "My ambition does not end here."

Li Fan took a deep breath and forcefully suppressed the surging spiritual energy within his body. "The localized destruction and rebirth within the Xuanhuang Realm, how can it compare to the world's subconscious reactions in the face of a world-ending crisis?" Li Fan recalled the insights he had gained from studying the "Book of Mending Heaven" over the years. The world, like a person, when facing a life-or-death crisis, often unleashes power beyond its limits. The world is the same. The moment a world-ending crisis descends, the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao will undergo all sorts of profound self-evolutions in pursuit of a glimmer of hope. The changes that will occur then will far surpass those during normal stable operation. "If successful, my strength after being promoted to the Nascent Soul stage will be even greater than estimated." "So..." "No one can stop me!" Li Fan's eyes were filled with indifference as he turned and left.

...

In the Spirit Wood Realm. Ou Daozi was carefully examining the corpse before him. "Incredible, truly incredible." "Is this really a substitute for a True Immortal, forged by Lord Envoy? If you hadn't told me personally, I would have truly believed it was a True Immortal's remains." "After all, the feeling it gives me is almost identical to when Shang Tian was nearby." A corpse emitting a faint golden light lay suspended in the air. Illuminated by the golden light, its face was indistinct. However, the divine aura it exuded inspired awe and greed in Ou Daozi.

Li Fan nodded with satisfaction upon hearing Ou Daozi's conclusion. This fabricated True Immortal remains was his trump card for stirring up trouble in the Xuanhuang Realm. The corpse was purchased at great expense, consisting of the remains of a Dao Integration cultivator from thousands of years ago, preserved in excellent condition. It was then meticulously crafted with Golden Origin Force Essence, imbuing it with an aura of power surpassing the mortal realm. Furthermore, to make the disguise more realistic, Li Fan extracted the abilities of some strange treasures he had obtained from the fishing pond and implanted them into this corpse. For example, upon approaching these remains, any strong emotion in a cultivator's heart would be infinitely magnified, almost causing them to lose all reason. Moreover, after being attacked, the remains would actively flee through the void. When someone touched the remains, the pure mutated spiritual energy hidden within would surge into their body, instantly boosting their cultivation.

...

All of this was to make the deception as realistic as possible. "Even a Heavenly Venerate of Longevity would surely be interested in the legendary True Immortal remains." "Then let's stir up some commotion." Besides these tangible benefits, Li Fan had also secretly made some arrangements on this so-called True Immortal remains. It was guaranteed to give the final recipient a big surprise. With the concealment of the Faceless True Immortal's power, it prevented cultivators skilled in divination from calculating the remains' origin. After the final refinements were made, two completely black puppets entered and carried away the "True Immortal remains." They then departed to carry out Li Fan's mission. From their appearance to their disappearance, they were silent. Even if Li Fan were not their master, it would be difficult to track their movements.

These two puppets were the spoils of years of hard work by Qiao Gong Juris and others from the Heavenly Mystery Realm. They were indeed the most gifted individuals from the Heavenly Mystery Realm. After persistent research, although they still hadn't grasped the essence of the power of darkness, they had no problem applying it to a certain extent. The black puppets perfectly embodied the characteristics of the power of darkness. They could, like the darkness, disappear from and reappear in the "gaps" of the world. Divine sense could not lock onto or detect them. Furthermore, they possessed a strong suppressive effect on spiritual energy. Ordinary attacks could hardly cause them damage. The only drawback was that the puppets' destructive power was limited, allowing them only to execute stealth missions. Moreover, the characteristic of darkness deviating from the Immortal Ruins meant that these puppets could not engage in prolonged combat. They had to return to the Void Realm periodically to replenish their power of darkness. Regardless, Li Fan was quite satisfied with these black puppets. Entrusting them with missions would leave virtually no flaws.

After dismissing Ou Daozi, Li Fan went alone to a secluded space. On the bright screen, young faces flickered continuously. Along with the images, there were long lists below, detailing their personalities. "There are countless mortals in the small worlds, but finding someone with a pure heart and absolute sincerity like Mr. Bai is still a bit difficult." "Especially since the power of the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth has already affected many small worlds." "The number of newly born people has noticeably decreased in these past few years." "It can't be helped. We'll have to settle for the next best thing."

Chapter 1106: Humans Go Mad for True Immortals

Collecting information on these children was naturally for the purpose of finding a successor for the Great Heavenly Venerate of Xuanhuang. Li Fan now knew all the answers to the trials, and as long as he could find individuals with roughly compatible personalities and character, the possibility of successfully succeeding him was quite high. There was no need to rush this life. First, identify suitable candidates, and then in the next life, select them and provide special training. Just as Li Fan was conducting various tests on these children through the Illusory Dream Technique, the grand play he had orchestrated to stir up the Xuanhuang Realm was slowly unfolding.

First, a rumor began to spread. Ou Shangtian, who had once caused a sensation and attracted the pursuit of almost all cultivators in the Myriad Immortals Alliance, possessed two heaven-defying abilities, [Kun Qian Bone Hand] and [Myriad Deaths Ledger], because he had come into contact with True Immortal remains in his youth. The [Kun Qian Bone Hand] could reverse the course of heaven and earth, returning an object to a previous state in time. The [Myriad Deaths Ledger] could predict countless ways of one's own death, and when used properly, could avert disasters and ward off misfortune.

The name Ou Shangtian was almost forgotten by the cultivators of the Alliance. However, the mention of these two terrifying abilities instantly rekindled the memories of the Alliance's cultivators. Back then, Ou Shangtian, with a cultivation below the Nascent Soul stage, had managed to hold out for nearly half a year under the pursuit of countless cultivators, proving the might of the [Kun Qian Bone Hand] and the [Myriad Deaths Ledger] through his actions. And these two powerful abilities were merely by-products of True Immortal remains? Then what kind of fortune awaited those who could obtain these so-called True Immortal remains in their entirety? The moment they heard this rumor, the thought flashed through almost every cultivator's mind.

However, the notion of a True Immortal was ethereal and illusory. Most people treated it as a mere rumor and did not take it seriously. Strangely, as time passed, the rumors did not subside; instead, they grew more intense. Observant individuals could tell that someone was behind these rumors, fanning the flames. Just as they were preparing to investigate the mastermind, something entirely unexpected occurred. On this evening, a lone, elegant white figure suddenly appeared above the Xuanhuang Sky Curtain. With his appearance, the entire Xuanhuang Realm trembled slightly. And all the cultivators who looked up at this figure felt an inexpressible feeling surge within them. The figure only lasted for a few breaths before abruptly vanishing.

But combined with the sensational rumors circulating beforehand, cultivators' minds instinctively conjured four words: "True Immortal Remains!" The phenomenon that enveloped the entire sky curtain, and the slight tremor of the Xuanhuang Realm that accompanied the appearance of the white figure, were undeniable! "Even if it's not a True Immortal, it's definitely someone extraordinary!" Just as people were speculating about the true identity of the white figure, in Tianling State, an endless black swamp gushed out from deep within a mountain, threatening to engulf everything around it. When cultivators saw these black, viscous substances, they knew they were the creations of the "Spirit of Heaven and Earth," the Black Swamp.

Faced with this apocalyptic crisis, cultivators did not panic but rejoiced; they did not flee but advanced. Many charged fearlessly towards the Black Swamp. After all, under the might of the Heavenly Venerate, everyone could die and be reborn, so there was nothing to fear. Conversely, if they could happen to slay this Spirit of Heaven and Earth, it would truly be a meteoric rise! Even a Dao Integration-level Spirit of Heaven and Earth, though powerful, couldn't withstand the might of many against one! A significant number of cultivators held this belief. Under their fierce struggle, the outward expansion of the Black Swamp was indeed curbed.

Just as cultivators were overjoyed, thinking the Black Swamp had weakened, a golden figure suddenly flew out from within the black swamp. Before everyone could react, it pierced through the sky and vanished without a trace. And after the golden figure departed, the rioting Black Swamp inexplicably retreated back underground. "That was..." "True Immortal Remains?" After a moment of stunned silence, someone in the crowd exclaimed with a trembling voice.

Boom! After a moment of silence, the crowd erupted. Because from that fleeting glimpse, that figure was indeed very similar to the one that had appeared in the sky curtain not long ago! Moreover, it could suppress the Dao Integration Black Swamp with its aura alone... After a moment of daze, the cultivators present reacted and chased after the direction where the golden light had disappeared. Only a few cultivators, after a moment of hesitation, still chose to attack the Black Swamp that had retreated into the depths of the mountain. However, to their regret, the Black Swamp, having returned to its lair, became even more ferocious and violent than before. Its strength even seemed to have significantly increased. These cultivators, without exception, all met their demise. But even with the complete annihilation, it did not deter the cultivators' greed. After all, everyone could resurrect! Thus, cultivators who rushed to their demise upon hearing the news continued to arrive ceaselessly.

...

The appearance of the Black Swamp and the True Immortal remains quickly spread throughout the Myriad Immortals Alliance. That golden figure, capable of inciting the disturbance of the Spirit of Heaven and Earth, gradually attracted the attention of more and more cultivators. Subsequently, wherever the True Immortal remains appeared, Spirits of Heaven and Earth inexplicably manifested, seemingly aiming to suppress these remains. They had never known that the Xuanhuang Realm hid so many Spirits of Heaven and Earth. For a time, cultivators were stunned by this spectacle. Barely every few days, they would hear news of new Spirits of Heaven and Earth appearing. And those cultivators in the Myriad Immortals Alliance who had been stuck in the Nascent Soul stage for a long time all began to go mad. They could no longer sit still and went to hunt down their desired Spirits of Heaven and Earth.

More cultivators, however, still focused their attention on the True Immortal remains. The desire of cultivators for the True Immortal remains reached its peak after a certain event. A mortal named Zhang Haobo, after fortunately coming into contact with the True Immortal remains that suddenly appeared before him, instantly leaped from being a mere mortal to the peak Golden Core stage! And the miraculous item that allowed him to build his foundation was a bone-shaped mystical item! Unfortunately, the True Immortal remains only stayed by his side for a moment before suddenly disappearing and fleeing again. Otherwise, it was likely not impossible for Zhang Haobo to have instantly advanced to the Nascent Soul stage!

After investigating Zhang Haobo's background, the cultivators ruled out the possibility of him fabricating or acting. After all, the nearly a hundred mortals who witnessed the miracle firsthand beside him had no issues with their memories! "The True Immortal remains should be looking for fated individuals." "Ou Shangtian was like this, and Zhang Haobo is also like this! However, their fate was not enough, and they were ultimately not chosen by the True Immortal remains." "But if one could ultimately obtain it..."

Chapter 1107: Scheming to Disrupt the World

The attraction of True Immortals to cultivators was simply too fatal. Since the severance of the immortal path, becoming an immortal had been an unattainable dream for cultivators. But now, True Immortal remains had suddenly appeared. Moreover, all signs indicated that these True Immortal remains were likely genuine! At this point, regardless of any lingering doubts, the choice made by cultivators was to obtain these remains first. Even if they weren't True Immortal remains, based on the strange phenomena they caused, the benefits gained would not be insignificant! Thus, cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance left their respective Heavenly Cities and searched everywhere for traces of the True Immortal remains.

Even some Five Elders Society cultivators who were shopping in the Nine Mountains State traveled thousands of miles to join the excitement. With the establishment and development of the Nine Mountains Free Trade Zone, the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elders Society had maintained peace for a long time. Their relationship had further eased, and as long as an application was submitted, cultivators from both sides could visit the other for sightseeing. It seemed they intended to prove through these methods that they were more suitable for cultivator survival than the other. However, there was no news of anyone changing their affiliation. The exchange between the two sides remained at the most superficial level.

Cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance were mostly wary of these members of the Five Elders Society. While banding together to search for the True Immortal remains, they tried to keep their distance, as a preca. "Do you think these True Immortal remains might be a ploy by the Five Elders Society to sow discord among us? Everyone is so focused on doing business that their vigilance towards the Five Elders Society is decreasing year by year. Alas, this is not a good thing." "Indeed, who knows when they might suddenly attack again! The Five Elders Society is not to be trifled with!" "What are you thinking? Are the spontaneously appearing Spirits of Heaven and Earth also the work of the Five Elders Society? This is on our Myriad Immortals Alliance territory. If we ourselves don't know about the existence of these Spirits of Heaven and Earth, and the Five Elders Society knows so much, then we might as well surrender now!"

The occasional appearance of Five Elders Society cultivators did not affect the Myriad Immortals Alliance's pursuit of the True Immortal remains. As a second lucky individual appeared, their desire grew even more intense. The second cultivator fortunate enough to have close contact with the True Immortal remains was named Xue Mu. He was a formation master at the Foundation Establishment stage. In reality, he had not truly touched the True Immortal remains, only being blocked by the golden light surrounding it. But the moment the golden light entered his body, countless wondrous and incredible formations instantly appeared in Xue Mu's mind. The vast data was almost enough to shatter his sea of consciousness. At the critical moment of life and death, Xue Mu instinctively let go. The True Immortal remains then vanished again.

However, Xue Mu, having missed out on a heaven-sent opportunity, not only did not regret it, but after a long period of daze, his face turned ecstatic, and he laughed up to the sky. Later, everyone learned that in that seemingly brief moment, he had obtained at least a hundred formations from the True Immortal remains. And, more importantly, the level of these formations generally surpassed the formations of the Xuanhuang Realm by several tiers. It was likely that even the most powerful formation in the current Myriad Immortals Alliance couldn't compare to any single one in his mind! Although his strength had not been improved, for Xue Mu, a formation master, this gain was far more significant than an increase of several major cultivation realms!

Soon, Xue Mu was taken away by people dispatched from the Myriad Immortals Alliance's Formation Hall headquarters. And the internal news that came soon after confirmed the advanced nature of the formations obtained in his sea of consciousness. Besides True Immortals, what other existence could possess such capabilities? This undoubtedly solidified the rumors of the True Immortal remains. After the news spread, some people in the Myriad Immortals Alliance could no longer sit still.

In the Spirit Wood Realm, Li Fan connected with Transmitter Zhou for communication. "The matter of the True Immortal remains has caused quite a stir recently. What are your thoughts on this, Daoist friend?" Li Fan quickly replied, stating firmly: "It's baseless, pure rumor! Daoist Zhou, please don't believe it!" "You are so sure?" This time, it was Transmitter Zhou who sounded suspicious. Li Fan sneered: "The immortal path has been severed for so many years, and none of our colleagues from various realms have ever seen the remains of a True Immortal." "The Xuanhuang Realm... is also like this. How could it be such a coincidence that it suddenly appeared without warning? Moreover, it instantly became known to everyone. I suspect someone is behind this!" Li Fan said convincingly.

"But the Spirits of Heaven and Earth that appeared alongside it are indeed genuine. In fact, two people in the Alliance have already successfully advanced to Dao Integration because of it. I truly can't imagine what force within the Xuanhuang Realm could casually present so many Dao Integration resources as bait?" Transmitter Zhou did not believe Li Fan's words and retorted. Li Fan seemed stumped. After a long silence, he sighed, "The more so, the greater the scheme! Your Myriad Immortals Alliance has reaped immense benefits, while we are living in fear." Transmitter Zhou suddenly asked, "Is it really not your United Front's doing?"

"What are you saying! Our Myriad Realms United Front has been lying low for many years, how could we suddenly cause such a commotion?" Li Fan's tone held a hint of displeasure. "In my opinion, it's more likely to be your enemies. Having ruled the Xuanhuang Realm for thousands of years, don't you have any sworn enemies?" "Hmm?!" Li Fan's words seemed to remind Transmitter Zhou of something. She looked momentarily surprised, and after a brief silence, she hastily ended the communication. Only then did Li Fan reveal a mysterious expression on his face.

There was no need for further words; all this turmoil was naturally the result of Li Fan's actions. Using the power of darkness from the black puppets, the True Immortal remains could traverse various locations, appearing and disappearing mysteriously, evading the pursuit of countless cultivators. And by relying on Li Fan's covert manipulation of the Heavenly Dao decrees, directing various Spirits of Heaven and Earth to manifest, Li Fan had made this play even more convincing. As for the two beneficiaries of this event, Zhang Haobo and Xue Mu, although they had no connection to him in this life, they were acquaintances from past reincarnations. Li Fan didn't mind lending a helping hand.

However, as he had been spreading false heavenly mandates everywhere, the Xuanhuang Realm's tolerance and vigilance were nearing their limit. He would have to lie low for a while. "The stage is set. I'm not afraid they won't fall into the trap. With such a chaotic situation, it should be able to conceal my true intentions." Li Fan chuckled softly. "However, Transmitter Zhou's final reaction was somewhat strange. Did she remember something?" "Could it be that the Myriad Immortals Alliance truly has an opponent capable of using several Dao Integration resources as bait?" Li Fan frowned, pondering.

Chapter 1108: Alien Star Falls to Xuanhuang

Although the Xuanhuang Realm had become much larger than other normal immortal cultivation worlds after thousands of years of being pulled and swallowed, Li Fan couldn't imagine where such a powerful force that the Myriad Immortals Alliance deeply feared could be hidden. The Heavenly Profound Mirror had undergone a complete overhaul and scan of the entire Xuanhuang Realm during its sublimation and transformation. Not only were the information on almost all subsidiary grotto-heavens and small worlds basically explored, but even the world rifts deep within the white mist had been largely investigated. "Unless it's another special hidden area like the Void Realm." "I can only say that it's worthy of being the last surviving gathering place for cultivators of the Darkest Star Sea. You never know when a powerhouse might suddenly emerge." "However, since they didn't survive the Xuanhuang Realm's destruction, even if they are strong, their strength is limited."

After analyzing, Li Fan felt somewhat relieved. "Speaking of which, the history of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's sudden rise from the immortal cultivation wasteland, when considered carefully now, is indeed a bit peculiar." After the great catastrophe of the Xuanhuang Realm, cultivators fell into an era of mutual suspicion and slaughter. Civilization eventually shattered, leaving behind no collective remnants, only solitary individuals as wary, bloodthirsty as wild beasts – the so-called immortal cultivation wasteland. All records that could be accessed agreed on what happened later in the Xuanhuang Realm: the long-lost Heavenly Venerate of Preaching the Dao returned and re-established civilization on the ruined land.

So the question arises. Whether it was the illusion of "Eras" experienced in the God Treasure Museum, or the fragments of history excavated from the bloody river by "Seeking the Hidden" in the Spirit Wood Realm, their descriptions of the cultivators living in that period could be summarized by the word "fierce" and "brutal." A group of people like that, facing the sudden appearance of the Heavenly Venerate of Preaching the Dao, who declared he would unite the Xuanhuang Realm, how would they react? Where are those people now? Both the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elders Society seem to have no trace of them.

"I remember that the Myriad Laws Merchant Guild in Nine Mountains State was passed down from that era. It’s a pity it has been razed to the ground now, otherwise, perhaps I could inquire about relevant information." Li Fan made a note to resolve this matter in his next life, then shifted his attention back to the "True Immortal Remains." After being reminded by Li Fan, the Myriad Immortals Alliance indeed became much more cautious. They directly chose to collectively capture any Spirits of Heaven and Earth that manifested, rather than letting them appear freely. As for the final allocation, it had already been decided in advance, aiming to harmlessly absorb these "baits" as quickly as possible and convert them into their own combat power.

With the Myriad Immortals Alliance officially intervening, the disturbances caused by the appearance of the Spirits of Heaven and Earth were quickly quelled. Regarding the True Immortal remains, the Myriad Immortals Alliance's attitude was very cautious. While they pursued it, they did not allow cultivators to kill each other over it; the final outcome depended on individual destiny. At the same time, in order to quell this controversy quickly, many Transmitter Immortals, who usually remained detached from worldly affairs, also made unprecedented appearances. It seemed their behavior had changed accordingly after the Mo Ru Bin incident.

With the Myriad Immortals Alliance participating in this game, Li Fan clearly felt that it had become much more difficult to manipulate the black puppets to lead the dogs. The Myriad Immortals Alliance's control over its own territory was still very strong. Not long after the puppets carrying the True Immortal remains appeared, they would be discovered and forced to relocate again. With the increased frequency of relocation, the puppets' weakness of being unable to sustain prolonged combat began to show. Fortunately, Li Fan ordered Qiao Gong and others to expedite the construction of more puppets and use them alternately, barely managing to maintain the elusive nature of the True Immortal remains.

However, Li Fan also vaguely sensed that the Myriad Immortals Alliance seemed to have become aware that the True Immortal remains were being transferred using the power of darkness. The time required for tracking was becoming increasingly shorter. "It seems this play won't last much longer." "But it doesn't matter; my objective has been achieved. I'll just wait for the final curtain call to give the inhabitants of the Xuanhuang Realm a surprise." Li Fan smiled kindly as he surveyed the progress of his various arrangements.

"Little friend, why are you doing this?" Three figures suddenly floated out, surrounding Li Fan. They had worried expressions and sallow complexions. They all stared at Li Fan, sighing interminably without speaking. They were the paper figures awakened from the Book of Tribulation Crossing. Since Li Fan began his world-destroying preparations, even though all arrangements were carried out through avatars and puppets, these paper figures from the Tribulation Crossing Sect had somehow sensed the crisis. From one at first, now two more paper figures had successively awakened. Moreover, they could vaguely sense Li Fan's world-destroying thoughts in his mind. Every time Li Fan rehearsed or deduced future scenarios, these bothersome figures would pester him with persuasions.

Li Fan naturally ignored them, facing them with a cold demeanor. After the three paper figures found their persuasion ineffective, they simply gave up. They clung to Li Fan with mournful faces. At first, Li Fan thought they were merely raging in frustration. But later, he discovered that when surrounded by these sad-faced paper figures, he himself would be infected by their emotions. No matter what he had been thinking before, how passionate he was, or how extreme his ideas were, they all eventually turned into utter apathy and emptiness. If not for Li Fan's protection under the "Xuanhuang Immortal Heart Mantra," he would have almost been influenced and changed by them.

The paper figures of the Tribulation Crossing Sect could only sense the general situation. They did not have the ability to remotely know Li Fan's specific actions during this period. Li Fan did not expose the fact that he was completely unaffected. Instead, he played along cooperatively, slowly letting the gloomy expression on his face dissipate, replaced by an unenthusiastic emptiness. His mind slowly cleared of all thoughts related to world destruction. The figures of the three paper figures then changed. They did not directly return to the Book of Tribulation Crossing but became solemn old scholars, sitting properly, recounting the various calamities that the Xuanhuang Realm had experienced to Li Fan. Their names were also interesting. They were all named after the calamities that had occurred in history. For example, one of them was named "Starfall," referring to an incident before the severance of the immortal path when an alien star fell from the sky to the Xuanhuang Realm. The energy surrounding the alien star had briefly caused the spiritual power of all cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm to be greatly affected, leading to a significant drop in strength regardless of their cultivation level.

Chapter 1109: A Scheme Against a True Immortal in the Dark

For instance, a Golden Core cultivator tripped and broke his leg. A Nascent Soul cultivator fell dead mid-air due to unstable spiritual power circulation. A Deity Transformation cultivator died of a sudden heart attack due to fighting too intensely... These were the bizarre examples that occurred during that time. Later, this minor calamity eventually dissipated as the strange energy surrounding the alien star gradually vanished on its own. In this era, it had long been forgotten and did not exist in any historical records. Only the Tribulation Crossing Sect, through its special cultivation methods, had recorded it.

"The power that could affect the entire Xuanhuang immortal cultivation world is undoubtedly at the level of Immortals. It's a pity that the alien star was merely a fleeting visitor to the Xuanhuang Realm and never appeared again." Li Fan couldn't help but feel a sense of regret. Otherwise, thinking about how familiar cultivators would have to live like mortals was quite interesting. The paper figures of the Tribulation Crossing Sect were not telling him these stories of past calamities out of idleness. They clearly had another purpose. As scenes of cruel calamities repeatedly appeared in Li Fan's mind, they eventually faded, and the tormented Xuanhuang Realm finally regained new life. He couldn't help but feel a sense of relief of "surviving a catastrophe." He had a newfound appreciation and cherishment for the current peaceful and stable state of the Xuanhuang Realm. Of course, the effects of this brainwashing were eventually dispelled by the operation of the Xuanhuang Immortal Heart Mantra. However, Li Fan still acted his part with utmost seriousness, displaying appropriate expressions on his face. Finally, when the three paper figures saw their methods were effective, they dutifully returned to the Book of Tribulation Crossing.

"The tricks of the Tribulation Crossing Sect are mostly related to manipulating people's hearts. The notoriety of this sect is evident." "It's a pity they met me. Hmph..." Ever since Li Fan liberated the Book of Tribulation Crossing from the restrictions of the Transmitter Immortals, these figures had latched onto him, persistently shadowing him. Although with Li Fan's current mastery of formations, he could completely re-seal them by force, Li Fan did not do so. Because being pestered by these paper figures also had its benefits. Li Fan narrowed his eyes and looked towards the Xuanhuang Realm. He could vaguely see countless specks of paper figures scattered throughout Xuanhuang. When he focused his consciousness on one of them, that paper figure inexplicably opened its eyes. Li Fan also used the paper figure's eyes as his own to see the scene it was monitoring. However, it was like looking through frosted glass, not very clear, and the sound was intermittent. This connection was forced to break after a short while.

"It seems my authority isn't high enough yet." Li Fan sneered inwardly. The benefit of accepting the brainwashing from the Tribulation Crossing Sect was the gradual acquisition of control authority over the "Divine Eye of World Observation." It seemed that accepting the Tribulation Crossing Sect's philosophy was also a process of joining and becoming a part of the Tribulation Crossing Sect. But obviously, Li Fan only intended to enjoy the benefits without joining the Tribulation Crossing Sect. "Only by becoming strong enough can any disaster be overcome without harm." "What kind of skill is it to constantly cower and hide?" "What's the use of constant evasion? When the Immortal Ruins immortals annihilated worlds with a glance, they couldn't even struggle before disappearing." Having already known the Tribulation Crossing Sect's performance during true calamities, Li Fan disdained their philosophy but did not underestimate them. He merely acted the part diligently, deceiving them.

Just as Li Fan was dealing with the Tribulation Crossing Sect, the grand play of the True Immortal remains was about to reach its climax. The Myriad Immortals Alliance, which had been tracking the remains for a long time, had finally deciphered its pattern of appearance and method. This time, they dispatched a full ten Dao Integration cultivators to surround and intercept it, determined to capture this so-called True Immortal remains that had caused such a huge stir. This operation was even assisted by three Transmitter Immortals. Faced with such a massive force, the black puppets were clearly struggling to cope. Finally, under Li Fan's command, their bodies dissolved, pouring all their remaining power of darkness into the True Immortal remains. Thus, with its power replenished, the True Immortal remains disappeared from the sight of the Myriad Immortals Alliance encirclement! However, this time, the distance it fled was not far. The tracking Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators quickly found its trace. It was not vanishing mysteriously anymore, but escaping by the normal method of fleeing cultivators.

"It seems he's finally tired of this game of hide-and-seek!" one of the Dao Integration cultivators said with a hint of anger in his voice. Anyone who had been led around by a mere remains for so long would inevitably lose their temper. "Quickly pursue! Be careful, don't let your guard down!" "Huh, look at the direction he's flying..." "No good, he's heading into the Yuan Devouring White Mist!" "It's fine. I have the Universal Wisdom True Boat with me. Continue the pursuit!" The leading Transmitter Immortal, Wei, said coldly. He released a flying boat, and the Dao Integration cultivators entered it, then closely pursued the True Immortal remains. Some of them clearly had entered the white mist before. Their eyes showed no fluctuation; instead, they calmly locked onto the location of the True Immortal remains ahead.

"Something's strange. He was always operating outside before, why would he suddenly lead us into the white mist?" "Could it be a trap?" The group exchanged glances. However, with their combined current strength, they could retreat safely even if they encountered a Longevity stage cultivator. They had no more reservations. Without much hesitation, they quickly unified their opinions and continued the pursuit, wanting to see what trick this True Immortal remains was playing. Inside the white mist, time was lost. The unusual scent that the True Immortal remains was luring them with was also very obvious, as if afraid the Myriad Immortals Alliance behind them would lose track. It even slowed down occasionally, maintaining a fixed distance between them. Moreover, the True Immortal remains seemed very familiar with this white mist, constantly changing direction. It clearly had a definite destination. This strange scenario made the Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators inside the Universal Wisdom True Boat's expressions turn grim.

Transmitter Immortal Wei, after pondering for a moment, finally decided to continue following and investigate. After all, as a Transmitter Immortal, he was not afraid of death. And even if this True Immortal remains had some conspiracy, it would be well worth it to understand it at the cost of one life. As for the Dao Integration cultivators beside him... Transmitter Immortal Wei's heart remained calm. True Immortal Remains, Universal Wisdom True Boat. Flying one after the other through the white mist. After an unknown period, the scene before them suddenly changed. Upon seeing what was ahead, the cultivators on the boat, including the several Transmitter Immortals, were all horrified and deeply shaken. An endless ocean, floating with countless corpses.

Chapter 1110: Life and Death Reveal the Heavenly Venerate

These corpses were all frozen in pale blue transparent ice crystals. Through the ice crystals, they could vaguely see the final expressions on the faces of these corpses in life: anger, fear, confusion... Lifelike, as if they were still alive. Dense ice crystal coffins filled the entire field of vision and covered the entire black ocean. Let alone the Dao Integration cultivators, even the three leading Transmitter Immortals were speechless and chilled to the bone upon witnessing this scene. Shocked by this scene, when they regained their senses, the True Immortal remains that had lured them here had already vanished without a trace!

"What... what kind of hellish place is this?!" After a deathly silence, a Dao Integration cultivator named Zhu Gongchuan among the group couldn't help but ask. Fearing that he might disturb the slumbering cultivators here, Zhu Gongchuan's voice was very low. And faintly, his inner fear could be heard. He had seen dead people before. But such a large number of corpses, all gathered in one place, and still preserving their living expressions from life... The shock of this scene was beyond words. No one answered Zhu Gongchuan's question. The group silently flew above the sea of death for a full half day, but still found no end.

"Based on preliminary estimates, there are over two billion corpses here... Perhaps the total number of cultivators and mortals living in the Myriad Immortals Alliance's surface territories doesn't even approach this many. Exactly..." "These people are not from the Xuanhuang Realm. Or rather, the vast majority are not from the Xuanhuang Realm," Transmitter Immortal Wei said slowly. "Judging from their attire, these people should all be from different immortal cultivation realms, but for some reason, they have all been frozen here." "So many corpses, hidden within our Myriad Immortals Alliance's territory, yet for such a long time, we have had no inkling of this." Another Transmitter Immortal, Chu, also looked extremely grim. "What is the purpose of the True Immortal remains bringing us here? Could it be that it also wants to turn us into this?" "No. We have been here for a long time, yet we have not been attacked."

...

The group discussed quietly, but had no clue as to the True Immortal remains' ultimate purpose. "Let's search for a while longer." So they continued to fly above the sea of death for a long time. Finally, Transmitter Immortal Wei discovered some clues: "These countless frozen corpses seem to form a massive formation." "A formation?" The group exchanged glances, then looked around more carefully. "Such a large-scale formation probably possesses world-destroying power. Could it be that the Five Elders Society secretly arranged this over the years to destroy our Myriad Immortals Alliance?" Not everyone present was proficient in formations. After failing to deduce anything, they couldn't help but indulge in wild speculation.

"This formation is extremely complex. We can only see a corner, not the whole picture, so we cannot determine its true purpose. The priority now is to notify the Alliance headquarters of this discovery. Staying here longer makes me feel uneasy," Transmitter Immortal Chu said solemnly. "Fortunately, this formation does not seem to target us outsiders. It's neither a confinement nor a killing formation. As long as we find the formation's eye, we should be able to leave." Transmitter Immortal Wei also made a judgment. With the conclusions of the two Transmitter Immortals, everyone finally breathed a sigh of relief. Wandering within the formation for several days, the group finally found the location of an eye. Passing through the eye of the formation, they thought they would leave this bizarre area, but unexpectedly, they did not return to the white mist. Instead, they appeared above another unfamiliar ocean.

Unlike the dead, frozen black sea before, here, the salty sea breeze was gentle, and the cries of birds could be heard. Fish schools could be seen leaping out of the water or swimming in the sea. It was teeming with life, refreshing and heartwarming. After a brief moment of astonishment, the group quickly scanned their surroundings, finding no apparent danger. The Dao Integration cultivators felt slightly at ease. However, the expressions of the three leading Transmitter Immortals became unusually grave. Transmitter Immortal Wei frowned, gazing at the sky, murmuring, "Different worlds, two sides of the same coin." "One is life, the other is death." Transmitter Immortal Chu interrupted him, "No, death is the source of life, and life is the gathering of death. This is..." The two exchanged glances, their faces filled with horror.

"Reversing Life and Death?" Both of them, with remarkable tacit understanding, avoided saying these four words aloud. Instead, they communicated through telepathic transmission. "So that's how it is. This must be the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth's dojo?" "I was wondering why His Highness's speed in reversing the principles of heaven and earth and attaining Dao Longevity was so rapid. It turns out he had already been hiding in this white mist, using formations as a basis, thoroughly studying the principles of life and death!" "What is the relationship between the True Immortal remains and the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth?" The mystery was solved, but new doubts arose in their minds. "From the current situation, they should not be working together." "Having discovered this dojo long ago, they deliberately led us here to probe the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth's background?"

The two fell into contemplation. After pondering for a long time, they reached no conclusion. "If we find the eye of the world of life, we should be able to leave from here." After finding no answers despite searching the entire dojo for any information related to the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth's true identity, the three Transmitter Immortals decided to return for the time being and plan further. However, just as they were about to leave, Transmitter Immortal Wei's body slightly stiffened, as if he had thought of something. "Reversing Life and Death, Reversing Life and Death..." "The great formation is complete, yet the cultivators who have already died have not awakened. What truly revived was the 'world'?" "This means the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth's true purpose is..." Transmitter Immortal Wei looked as if struck by lightning, his face instantly turning pale.

"Go!" he commanded decisively. However, it seemed as if his thoughts had been perceived. A figure, seemingly made of white mist, quietly appeared, blocking their path. Facing this sudden appearance of an enemy, and potentially the elusive Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth, the group instantly became extremely tense. A battle was imminent.
