Transmitter Immortal Wei stared at the figure before him for a moment, and after a while, disbelief flashed in his eyes. "It's..." Before he could finish speaking, the white mist figure suddenly opened its eyes. Endless white mist surged from its body, vast and overwhelming. In an instant, it engulfed the Myriad Immortals Alliance group. Ten Dao Integration cultivators, three Transmitter Immortals. Such a massive force, yet at this moment, they had no power to resist, disappearing into the white mist in the blink of an eye.

Chapter 1111: Quietly Setting a Trap

Xuanhuang Realm, Myriad Immortals Alliance.

All the floating Heavenly Cities simultaneously rang with hurried bells. The Alliance cultivators stopped their actions and froze in place. After a moment of stunned silence, they finally remembered the meaning of this bell sound. This was the highest level of warning for the Myriad Immortals Alliance. It was only activated when the Alliance faced a crisis of life and death.

After a brief silence, chaos erupted. People were terrified and at a loss.

Li Fan, in the Spirit Wood Realm, naturally heard the bell sound immediately. At first, he thought his world-destroying arrangements had been discovered. However, Li Fan quickly realized that the sudden ringing of the bells was likely related to the events that had occurred within the Great Formation of Life and Death.

And when the recorded footage from the True Immortal remains was transmitted, it confirmed his judgment. The footage finally stopped at the disappearance of the Transmitter Immortals in the white mist. Afterwards, the recording formation was also destroyed by the surging, endless white mist.

Li Fan repeatedly reviewed the footage, a hint of solemnity flickering in his eyes: "The Myriad Immortals Alliance is reacting so strongly, this means..."

"Have the Transmitter Immortals died?" Li Fan was filled with shock and uncertainty.

He knew that each Transmitter Immortal was protected by the "Heavenly Venerate of Preaching the Dao." As long as this protective force remained, they were essentially indestructible within the Xuanhuang Realm. Although they were restricted and unable to advance to the Longevity stage, they were almost equivalent to Longevity cultivators. He never expected that before the newly ascended Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth, they would be so vulnerable.

"To be able to instantly kill Transmitter Immortals?"

"If these three Transmitter Immortals truly died like this, then the strength of Rebirth..." Li Fan's eyes narrowed slightly. He then felt a flicker of doubt.

"If Rebirth is indeed that strong, then what reason did He have to kill the three Transmitter Immortals?"

"It was clearly just an accidental intrusion; there was no disrespect or damage."

Li Fan slowly reviewed the footage from the formation again. He finally discovered something amiss.

"It seems that before their departure, Rebirth had no intention of appearing."

"But Transmitter Immortal Wei seemed to have discovered something, which led to Rebirth's appearance."

"So, it was a cover-up?" Li Fan's expression turned strange. Killing to silence, such an act seemed somewhat beneath a Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth. But He still did it. This could only mean one explanation: if Transmitter Immortal Wei's discovery leaked out, it would cause him irreparable damage. To avoid variables, Rebirth chose to eliminate him.

"In his lifetime, Transmitter Immortal Wei must have been contemplating the Great Formation of Reversing Life and Death."

Following this line of thought, Li Fan put himself in his shoes. With his current level of formation mastery, he quickly understood the key.

"Just as I suspected, the ultimate goal of reversing life and death is not to reverse the life and death of cultivators."

"The resurrection of cultivators is merely an incidental change in the principles of heaven and earth during this process."

"This Heavenly Venerate's true target for reversing life and death is the 'world'."

A brilliant light flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

"To conceal this goal, the Myriad Immortals Alliance group must be eliminated."

"This means His target for revival is not the 'Xuanhuang Realm.' Instead, it is one of the many immortal cultivation worlds that have been swallowed by the Xuanhuang Realm over the years."

"Interesting. Is this a lingering attachment to one's homeland?"

After reviewing the sequence of events again, Li Fan nodded slightly.

"No wonder this person has been acting low-key all these years, never revealing himself to the public. This act is like a return from the dead; if successful, his homeland world might indeed be revived."

"But the fate of the Xuanhuang Realm itself is uncertain."

"If it were leaked, it would surely be met with fierce resistance from the native cultivators of the Xuanhuang Realm."

"So, like me, he is doing something that cannot be seen."

Li Fan's lips curved into a smile.

"But all plans are destined to fail."

The smile instantly vanished. Li Fan's attention returned to the True Immortal remains. It had now returned to the Xuanhuang Realm. As the direct culprit behind the demise of the three Transmitter Immortals, it was pursued by the Myriad Immortals Alliance as soon as it appeared.

This time, the Myriad Immortals Alliance was serious. After all, not even a Transmitter Immortal had died during the Mo Ru Bin possession incident. Now, three had perished at once, the shock to the Council of Transmitter Immortals was immense.

More than a dozen Transmitter Immortals appeared simultaneously, locking onto the True Immortal remains in the center. And among the crowd, Li Fan surprisingly discovered the figure of Emperor San Mo, the curator of the God Treasure Museum.

Compared to his image in the Fallen Immortal Realm, he appeared even more aged. However, he seemed unconcerned about the Myriad Immortals Alliance's pursuit. His expression was blank, his eyes slightly closed. Clearly, his attendance was merely a formality.

Besides him, Li Fan finally saw the lineage of "Mirror Holders." They all wore dark green robes, with mirror-like imprints engraved on their foreheads. The three major powers that truly controlled the Myriad Immortals Alliance had gathered here, showing the immense impact of the three Transmitter Immortals' deaths.

Under the influence of these forces, Li Fan sensed his control over the True Immortal remains weakening. Just as he was preparing to detonate the remains, creating a passage between the Xuanhuang Realm and the Void Realm to trigger a Void Sea tide, something unexpected happened.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance's core, which had been poised to act, seemed to have suddenly received some news. At first, they showed confusion and disbelief. Then, without hesitation, they acted in unison. Their figures blurred, as if they were ignoring the perpetrator and were about to leave the scene!

Li Fan also saw Emperor San Mo, who had previously had his eyes closed, suddenly open them, as if something had arrived and captured his attention. Far away in the Spirit Wood Realm, Li Fan instantly felt a sense of foreboding. Years of experience prompted him to make an immediate decision. He severed the connection with the True Immortal remains and simultaneously detonated it.

The moment the True Immortal remains fragmented, a figure made of white mist quietly appeared beside it. It appeared without warning and so quickly. But ultimately, it was too late.

Endless darkness surged from the cracks of the True Immortal remains. It collided with the white mist that emerged from the white mist figure. The Void Sea tide that Li Fan had expected did not arrive. The white mist acted like bags of waterproof sand, like a dam that stood unyielding by the sea, firmly blocking the Void Sea tide, which was powerful enough to cause catastrophe.

...

In the Spirit Wood Realm, a cold expression flashed across Li Fan's face.

"What is the meaning of this?"

"Have they cooperated?"

"To find me, they are even disregarding the deaths of Transmitter Immortals?"

Chapter 1112: Heavenly Venerate's Annihilation Strategy

After a brief moment of confusion, a strong sense of crisis arose. "The fact that the Myriad Immortals Alliance could react so swiftly and uniformly, there is only one thing in this world..." "The Heavenly Venerate of Preaching the Dao!" Li Fan's thoughts raced. "It's understandable that the fall of Transmitter Immortals would alert the Heavenly Venerate of Preaching the Dao." "But why would He choose to cooperate with Rebirth?" Li Fan frowned deeply. With the strength of the Heavenly Venerate of Preaching the Dao, upon meeting Rebirth, He would undoubtedly recognize Rebirth's origin at a glance. Rebirth intended to use a borrowed body to resurrect its devoured world; and based on previous intelligence, the Heavenly Venerate of Preaching the Dao cared immensely about the Xuanhuang Realm... Their stances were almost diametrically opposed. But according to the current situation, they seemed to have reached some sort of agreement in such a short time.

"Is it out of anger from being toyed with, or are there other deeper reasons?" The joint involvement of two Heavenly Venerates of Longevity was something Li Fan had not anticipated. He decisively severed the connection with the puppets currently carrying out missions in the Xuanhuang Realm. The last command given was to have the puppets self-destruct. Simultaneously, he used formations to seal the entrance from the Spirit Wood Realm to the Xuanhuang Realm. As for the underground world, he also temporarily closed the passage connecting to the Void Realm. He decided to lie low for a while. Li Fan could indeed forcibly initiate his world-destroying arrangements at this time, but first, under the watch of the Transmitter Immortals, the bait puppets flying towards the Immortal Ruins to attract the attention of the immortals within might not even be able to fly out of the Xuanhuang Realm successfully. Although the bait puppets were concealed by the power of darkness and formations, the Heavenly Venerate of Preaching the Dao should by no means be underestimated. Li Fan had no confidence in completing this task under His watch.

Encountering unexpected changes, Li Fan remained calm despite his shock. "I still have plenty of time. I don't believe these two can keep watching forever." "There's no such thing as guarding against a thief for a thousand days." "Besides, in their eyes, I am at most a petty rogue trying to instigate infighting and profit from it." "It's highly unlikely they would guess my true world-destroying plan." "As long as I seize the opportunity..." Thinking this, Li Fan slowly calmed down. He then recalled the scene he had last seen through the True Immortal remains.

"Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth, with a body of white mist. To actually withstand the great tide formed by the power of darkness..." "It definitely possesses the strength to threaten the existence of the Xuanhuang Realm. Perhaps this is also one of the reasons why the Council of Preaching chose to cooperate with Him." Li Fan suddenly thought of another point. "The barrier of white mist began to appear in the Xuanhuang Realm after the great catastrophe. On the surface, it spans heaven and earth, dividing regions. In reality, it is a binding agent that fuses the Xuanhuang Realm with the swallowed worlds." "And the white mist is subtly related to the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth. Looking at it this way, the Transmitter Immortal and Rebirth might have known each other beforehand. That's why they could reach an agreement so quickly."

As for the true identity of Rebirth, Li Fan had a few suspects. Tianyi was one of them. Coming from another immortal cultivation world. Viewing worlds as human bodies, reversing their life and death. Regardless of how one looked at it, he fit this condition. Moreover, Rebirth's attainment of Dao in this life was slightly faster than in previous lives, likely because Li Fan inherited the "Book of Mending Heaven" and resolved the hidden worries of the Yunshui Heavenly Palace crowd for him. Recalling the previous interactions of Tianyi with Tianjue, Tianyu, and others, it was almost certain that the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth was related to Tianyi, if not Tianyi himself. Tianyi was as elusive as a dragon, appearing only to vanish, traversing the void alone in the Darkest Star Sea, searching for remnants of immortal cultivation worlds to strengthen the Xuanhuang Realm. Since their last parting, he had not contacted Li Fan again. Li Fan naturally would not proactively contact Tianyi. Furthermore, he had used the power of the Faceless True Immortal to mask his perceptions from him.

"At my level of strength, no matter what I want to do, I will almost inevitably encounter people at the level of Transmitter Immortals and Tianyi." "This is due to the Xuanhuang Realm being reduced to a corner." "Although I still know little about them, fortunately..." "They know even less about me." Li Fan's gaze was distant. "While there is indeed a gap in strength, I dared to scheme against a True Immortal, so why would I fear them?" "It's just a matter of waiting patiently for now."

...

Although the Spirit Wood Realm was completely sealed off, Li Fan was still fully aware of everything happening in the Xuanhuang Realm. First, by spying on the various idle conversations of cultivators through the origin of the Heavenly Profound Mirror. Second, by gathering intelligence from Transmitter Zhou. "Daoist Zhou, has something major happened in the Myriad Immortals Alliance? That highest-level warning bell, and I couldn't reach you earlier..." Transmitter Zhou's tone held a hint of helplessness. "A fellow Transmitter Immortal has fallen." Li Fan feigned extreme shock and then hastily pressed for details. Transmitter Zhou briefly recounted the cause of the incident. "I knew long ago that this 'True Immortal remains' was a trap. But I never expected the power behind it could harm a Transmitter Immortal?" Li Fan's face was filled with disbelief. "Was the mastermind behind this caught? Are there any clues?" Li Fan also asked. Transmitter Zhou shook her head, not providing a detailed answer. Li Fan did not press further and said earnestly, "I will also report this matter to the United Front. If there are any findings, I will inform you immediately." "Then I thank you in advance." Transmitter Zhou seemed to have no expectations of Li Fan's side and replied perfunctorily.

After ending the communication, Li Fan began to ponder over potential scapegoats. However, after much deliberation, in the vast Xuanhuang Realm, there were very few who possessed the power to accomplish what Li Fan had done. "The remaining few who fit the criteria, such as the Five Elders Society and the Taiyan Sect, it's not easy to frame them. If I try to be clever, I might end up exposing myself." Li Fan sighed inwardly, learning from his mistakes: "I just don't have enough personas." "If I had another identity at this moment, I could frame myself and clear my name." "I will pay attention to this in the future." Even Li Fan, who considered himself wise, could not think of a more suitable method in the current situation, other than patiently waiting for the storm to pass. The main reason was that in this life, he had inadvertently fallen into the True Immortal's net and could not immediately return to his original form. Therefore, whatever he did, he felt somewhat hesitant and restrained. But escaping to the depths of the Void Realm in a panic was not what Li Fan desired.

...

"As the saying goes, circumstances are stronger than people. No matter how much you scheme and maneuver, there will come a time when you lose your room to maneuver."

Chapter 1113: Hidden Alone in the Dark Prison

In solitary confinement, Li Fan was confident that he wouldn't be found by the Heavenly Venerate of Preaching or the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth. After all, the True Immortal puppet was covered in countless concealing formations, far surpassing the Great Reversal of Life and Death Formation. Furthermore, the Frozen Sea of Death had never been visited before, yet the True Immortal’s remains could pinpoint its location precisely. This alone was enough to sow doubt and suspicion in the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth's mind.

"Logically, he should be targeting those who might have existed in previous lives," Li Fan mused. "Even if he wants to investigate me, there's no starting point. The only loophole is the method of transferring the True Immortal puppet: the Power of Darkness. Besides the Myriad Immortals Alliance, only I, from the Myriad Realms United Front, have ever visited the Void Realm."

At this thought, Li Fan's heart grew heavy. At the level of the Heavenly Venerate of Preaching, they no longer needed to "deduce" things based on evidence. A mere possibility was enough for them to make a decision. "Since I've re-examined the situation and concluded that only a few factions in the entire Xuanhuang Realm could have accomplished this, then from their perspective, eliminating them all is the best way to prevent future trouble…" "Although it seems utterly unreasonable, this is the way of a hegemon."

As his thoughts churned, Li Fan's heart pounded. He immediately made a decision. In the Spirit Wood Realm, all defensive formations were activated to full power. The cultivators of the Myriad Realms United Front were prepared for battle. He summoned the key figures from the Heavenly Mystery Realm, the Medicine King Sect, and the Imperial Small Worlds, explaining the gravity of the crisis. Qiao Gong, Liu Ruchen, and the others paled slightly.

"Isn't this too unreasonable? Just because we possess the strength to kill a Transmitter Immortal, and they can't find the murderer, they want to destroy us all?" "Is Your Excellency being too pessimistic? The Myriad Immortals Alliance wouldn't be so reckless, would they?"

Murmurs rippled through the assembly, but upon seeing Li Fan's increasingly grim expression, they all fell silent. "Through pleading for the protection of the Crimson Dust Compassionate Immortal, I have almost confirmed the matter. There is no need for doubt. Prepare yourselves in advance. There is no room for negotiation in this war," Li Fan stated coldly. The color drained from everyone's faces upon hearing this.

"The only chance of survival is if our strength in resistance is sufficient. They are coming to avenge the three Transmitter Immortals, but if we can inflict more than just the loss of three Transmitter Immortals…" "They will have reason to hesitate," Li Fan continued, rallying them. "Although the Myriad Immortals Alliance is powerful, they cannot deploy their entire force against us. Moreover, we have the advantage of terrain. The Spirit Wood Realm is as strong as gold, covered by countless formations, shielded by the Heavenly Mystery Realm's fortifications. Finally, we can even mobilize the power of the Void Realm to launch a surprise attack with a tide of darkness…"

Li Fan spoke with confidence: "As long as we can withstand the initial, fiercest waves of attack, we should be able to overcome this crisis." Despite Li Fan's words, no one looked optimistic. They departed with heavy hearts to prepare for battle. The Spirit Wood Realm was sealed off; even if they had the thought of fleeing, they couldn't. There was only a fight to the death.

As for Li Fan… In the underground secret chamber, a holy fetus, identical to Li Fan, was rapidly taking shape. With the divine power of the Crimson Dust Compassionate Immortal, the holy fetus was forcibly elevated to the Nascent Soul stage. Afterward, the holy fetus left the secret chamber and donned the Heavenly Sun Battle Puppet. As for Li Fan himself… he left the Spirit Wood Realm without taking anything, undetected.

Knowing that the Myriad Immortals Alliance would attack the Spirit Wood Realm, why would Li Fan stay behind with his true body to fight them head-on? For Li Fan, the Myriad Realms United Front, the Spirit Wood Realm, the Heavenly Mystery Medicine King… all of it was merely external. It could be abandoned at any time. Only his own safety was paramount. As long as he preserved his life and weathered this storm, once the Heavenly Venerates of Preaching and Rebirth let down their guard, he could unleash his world-destroying plans. When everything was restored, what was lost would eventually return to his hands. With Li Fan's current stealth capabilities, after leaving the Spirit Wood Realm, he traveled unimpeded, his tracks undiscovered. And he had already decided on his hiding place for the time being.

"The saying goes, 'where the lamp shines brightest, the darkness is deepest.' The most dangerous place is often the safest." Before long, he had reached his destination: the Myriad Immortals Alliance's Prison of Oblivion, from which Transmitter Immortal Wei had been extracted. "Heh heh, am I walking into a trap?" Li Fan chuckled self-mockingly. "However, this so-called trap of the Prison of Oblivion cannot hold me." After careful observation, Li Fan had already deciphered the formations covering the entrance to the Prison of Oblivion. Transforming into a wisp of dim shadow, he silently flew inside.

The scene before him abruptly turned dim, somewhat similar to the conditions in the Void Realm. There was no heaven or earth; only endless darkness met his gaze. But compared to the utter blackness of the Void Realm, there was a faint glimmer of light here. At least his divine sense could vaguely discern the direction of travel, preventing complete disorientation. In the pitch-black, boundless space stood towering prison pillars. Each pillar seemed to suppress a prisoner, and images of various horrific tortures continuously shifted on their surfaces. As for the wardens of this Prison of Oblivion, they were monstrous creatures formed from an unknown black fog-like substance floating in the space. They numbered in the thousands, far exceeding the number of pillars, and occasionally let out guttural roars before diving into the pillars containing prisoners. Soon, faint screams of agony echoed from the cages. After prolonged torment, these black fog creatures would leave the pillars, seemingly content. Similar scenes unfolded endlessly within the Prison of Oblivion, as if without end.

Li Fan observed this purgatorial scene with an unchanged expression. After examining the composition of the prison pillars, he determined they were formed by some kind of formation. His eyes flickered, and in almost an instant, he deciphered them. Then, he selected an empty pillar and voluntarily entered it. "Not bad." Upon entering the black pillar, Li Fan looked around. Inside, it was actually more brightly lit than outside. However, formation attacks would descend at any moment as a form of punishment. Naturally, Li Fan was unharmed. "They've probably scoured the entire Xuanhuang Realm and still wouldn't think I'm hiding here," Li Fan thought. "And when they forget about me, that's when I'll emerge." As if returning home, Li Fan settled comfortably into the Prison of Oblivion. To him, the Spirit Wood Realm and the Prison of Oblivion were essentially indistinguishable.

Chapter 1114: The Battle of the Spirit Wood Begins

In the Prison of Oblivion, time seemed to lose all meaning. Every day, faced only with unchanging gloom and the seemingly ceaseless sounds of agonizing screams. The black fog wardens lacked a high level of intelligence. Towards Li Fan, the sudden new prisoner, they merely let out cackling laughter before mechanically activating the formations within the prison pillars, attempting to torment him. Naturally, all their efforts were easily neutralized by Li Fan. However, he played along, simulating cries of agony to satisfy the black fog wardens before they left.

Besides these regularly appearing low-level wardens, Li Fan occasionally saw patrolling cultivators from the Myriad Immortals Alliance. A total of three, rotating their duties. They generally treated their patrols of the Prison of Oblivion as a mere formality. After all, the prison had been peaceful for thousands of years, with no disturbances. However, after a period of observation, Li Fan realized that the area where he was currently hiding was merely the outermost layer of the Prison of Oblivion. The Myriad Immortals Alliance didn't pay much attention to the prisoners confined here. Li Fan even witnessed a neighbor, unable to bear the torment of the formations, have his soul scatter. Yet, for a long time afterward, no one came to check on it. It was only when the black fog wardens conducted their routine patrol that they discovered it. They then activated a purification formation, cleansed the black pillar, and awaited the next inmate. This situation within the Prison of Oblivion greatly satisfied Li Fan. The probability of him being discovered was very low, and he was not disturbed regularly. While enjoying the peace, Li Fan made preparations for his final world-destroying plan and, through his holy infant, observed the situation in the Spirit Wood Realm.

For a considerable period after Li Fan issued the order for full combat readiness and his own escape, the outside world remained calm, with no signs of the Myriad Immortals Alliance launching an attack. This led many to harbor doubts about Li Fan's predictions. However, deterred by the might of the Crimson Dust Compassionate Immortal, they dared not voice their concerns. Li Fan, however, knew this was merely the calm before the storm. The events proved Li Fan's prediction correct.

One day, the sealing formation at the entrance of the Spirit Wood Realm suddenly showed faint fluctuations without any sound. The holy infant Li Fan immediately detected the anomaly. After concentrating his senses and observing for a moment, Li Fan let out a cold snort: "They've got some tricks up their sleeves. It seems the formations I gifted the Myriad Immortals Alliance have been thoroughly studied. Their formation level has improved by at least a century compared to before. What a pity…" "They are still more than a generation behind me!" "With their snail's pace, it will probably take them at least three months to break through the formation, and that's if I don't repair it. However, conversely, the Myriad Immortals Alliance might not have that much patience. If they can't break the formation, they'll likely resort to a direct assault…"

Li Fan didn't believe that a mere formation could hold back the entire Myriad Immortals Alliance army. "Why not create a weakness and let them send in a batch first, then trap them like a toad in a well!" Li Fan's thoughts raced, and he came up with a plan. Although his true body had fled for safety, facing the Myriad Immortals Alliance's pressure, Li Fan did not intend to completely give up resistance. After all, the accumulation of resources in the Spirit Wood Realm this lifetime was hard-won, requiring immense effort and dedication. Now that the Myriad Immortals Alliance was attacking, he would naturally resist. "This is a good opportunity to test the Myriad Immortals Alliance's strength and see if they are worthy of being one of the two major ruling organizations of the Xuanhuang Realm."

The holy infant Li Fan notified the inhabitants of the Spirit Wood Realm to prepare for battle. Simultaneously, cooperating with the Myriad Immortals Alliance's formation-breaking methods, he gradually weakened the formation's defenses, making it appear as if the formation was truly being broken. The flaws grew larger and larger until a crack appeared at the entrance passage of the Spirit Wood Realm. The first wave of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's attacking force instantly breached these fissures and entered the Spirit Wood Realm.

Upon meeting, both sides were slightly stunned. The Myriad Immortals Alliance was surprised that the people of the Spirit Wood Realm seemed to have S discovered their minor actions and were already prepared. Li Fan, on the other hand, was astonished that the so-called vanguard of the Myriad Immortals Alliance consisted not of elite death warriors, but of over a hundred gleaming arrows emitting a cold light.

"Sky-Patrolling Arrows?!" Li Fan was somewhat surprised. The Sky-Patrolling Arrows were a powerful weapon developed by the Myriad Immortals Alliance in this lifetime. They traveled extremely fast, capable of traversing an entire province within a few breaths, and their power was astonishing, equivalent to the strike of an ordinary Dao Integration cultivator. But that wasn't the most terrifying aspect. The Sky-Patrolling Arrows' true might lay in their ability to form a special formation with each other, creating a vast net that could even distort and influence the laws of heaven and earth. During the previous great battle between the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elder Society, the Myriad Immortals Alliance had used the Sky-Patrolling Arrows to interfere with the general principles of heaven and earth on a large scale, preventing the Longgevity Heavenly Venerates of the Five Elder Society from intervening in the battle.

"It seems the Myriad Immortals Alliance intends to execute a decapitation strategy. With 168 Sky-Patrolling Arrows, if it were an ordinary small world, its fighting strength would be completely annihilated by this single move. But…" Li Fan sneered and reacted swiftly. He first used the grand formation enveloping the Spirit Wood Realm to interfere with these Sky-Patrolling Arrows, preventing them from completing their formation. Then, he dispatched the Heavenly Sun puppet, using its absolute crushing strength to collect and suppress each arrow before they could scatter and cause destruction. Although the Sky-Patrolling Arrows were fast, the Heavenly Sun was faster! The Heavenly Sun transformed into a beam of azure light, streaking back and forth across the sky. In the blink of an eye, all of them were under control.

"Take some to study and see if we can use this thing to our advantage," the holy infant Li Fan said to Qiao Gong. Qiao Gong, greatly excited, eagerly took the Sky-Patrolling Arrows and immediately began dismantling and researching them. Meanwhile, on the Myriad Immortals Alliance's side, the inexplicable loss of over a hundred Sky-Patrolling Arrows seemed to have caught them off guard. After a long period of bewilderment, they delayed launching the next wave of attacks. Seeing this, Li Fan's eyes darted. He feigned activating the formation to repair the entrance, gradually loosening the formation's defenses. As the cracks in the formation grew larger, and a fissure finally appeared at the entrance to the Spirit Wood Realm, the Myriad Immortals Alliance's first attacking force instantly passed through the fissures and entered the Spirit Wood Realm.

Upon their first encounter, both sides were slightly stunned. The Myriad Immortals Alliance was surprised that the Spirit Wood Realm's forces seemed to have discovered their subtle maneuver and were already on high alert. Li Fan, on the other hand, was surprised that the vanguard of the Myriad Immortals Alliance consisted not of elite death warriors, but of over a hundred gleaming arrows emanating a cold light.

Chapter 1115: Defeating the Immortal Alliance with Laughter

Regardless of whether one looked with their eyes or observed with their divine sense, these golden phantoms seemed no different from real cultivators. It was difficult to distinguish them. In just a moment, the entire sky of the Spirit Wood Realm was filled with golden armored figures. Their mission was not simply to attack but to gather intelligence for the main force about the Spirit Wood Realm.

"How are these golden armors?" Li Fan asked Fang Zaiji nonchalantly. Fang Zaiji narrowed his eyes, observing carefully, and then replied with a hint of arrogance, "It's just a high-level illusion technique. I thought the Myriad Immortals Alliance had truly developed armor that could infinitely split itself!" "After a few probes, we can see through the illusion and find the real one!" Fang Zaiji said confidently. "It seems with the infusion of technology from the Heavenly Mystery Realm, the Spirit Wood Realm's artifact refining has surpassed the Myriad Immortals Alliance." Having received a satisfactory answer, Li Fan waved his hand, indicating that Fang Zaiji need not probe further.

Suddenly, a massive arch-shaped light sphere appeared throughout the Spirit Wood Realm. The surface of the light sphere displayed constantly shifting metallic patterns. Under Li Fan's command, numerous dark cannon muzzles instantly formed. "Boom!" The muzzles locked onto the golden armored cultivators dancing in the sky. Then, countless beams of black light erupted violently from them! In the face of this destructive black light, the golden armored cultivators could not resist at all. In an instant, they were torn to shreds and vanished into thin air. With just a single volley, more than half of the countless golden phantoms were annihilated. This terrifying scene caused the movements of the remaining golden armored cultivators to halt for a moment. While they were stunned, another volley of cannon fire arrived instantly. Before the black death rays, the golden armors were as fragile as paper. All the golden phantoms throughout the Spirit Wood Realm were eliminated.

"The Heavenly Mystery Fortress, combined with the Heaven-Splitting Cannon, copied from the Myriad Immortals Alliance. There's no need for fancy illusion techniques; even if there were more, they would all simply be annihilated." "This is the principle of 'strength overcomes all techniques'," Li Fan thought to himself. He also checked the energy reserves stored within the Heavenly Mystery Fortress. The Heavenly Mystery Fortress was integrated with the Spirit Wood Realm. The countless living corpses on the plaza continuously circulating the Vast Crowd Spiritual Energy technique, along with the large number of cultivators in various small worlds, were constantly providing it with energy. After this period of accumulation, it had reached an astonishing level. Li Fan estimated that a full volley of cannon fire of the previous intensity could continue for seven days and seven nights without depleting the energy.

"What other tricks do you have? Feel free to bring them out," Li Fan said coldly, looking toward the flickering entrance fissure. Having lost two vanguard forces in succession, the Myriad Immortals Alliance seemed to have become much more cautious. This time, after a long period of deliberation, they finally dispatched their true elite forces. Before their figures even appeared, a surging killing intent was already felt from afar. The fissure suddenly widened significantly, and Li Fan's heart skipped a beat. He immediately activated the defensive functions of the Heavenly Mystery Fortress. Instantly, the arc-shaped light barrier violently shook, with wave-like patterns continuously flowing across it. After a considerable time, the inexplicable impact was finally neutralized.

Li Fan's eyelids twitched after examining the situation. The energy reserves of the Heavenly Mystery Fortress, which he had previously thought to be quite sufficient, had been depleted by one-sixth in just a few moments! And the Myriad Immortals Alliance forces that launched the attack had not even revealed themselves yet. "What is that thing!?" Li Fan narrowed his eyes. The subordinates of the Spirit Wood Realm also sensed something, their expressions turning tense and uneasy. "My Lord Envoy, be careful. The enemy has likely arrived," Liu Ruchen suddenly warned in a deep voice. Before the words even fell, the Heavenly Mystery Fortress's light barrier shook violently again. This time, the amplitude was even greater than before, and the light barrier dimmed considerably, clearly indicating that it had blocked another attack from the unknown enemy for the Spirit Wood Realm.

Li Fan knew that without the Heavenly Mystery Fortress, the Spirit Wood Realm would likely be riddled with holes by now. However, the enemy had already launched two attacks, yet neither Li Fan nor his subordinates had figured out what kind of entity they were facing. "As expected of a behemoth organization that rules half the land of the Xuanhuang Realm. They indeed possess trump cards that I, despite reincarnating countless times, have never discovered." Facing this troublesome enemy, Li Fan was not alarmed but instead delighted. He felt that even if the Spirit Wood Realm were completely destroyed at this moment, it would have been somewhat worthwhile just for this discovery. However, the Spirit Wood Realm, having gathered remnants of various ancient immortal cultivation realms, would not perish so easily.

While everyone was bewildered and unable to figure out the situation, Baihua Daoist, after careful observation, made a discovery. "This method of attack… I seem to have heard a friend mention it before." "A ferocious beast hidden in the void, feeding on immortal cultivation world continents. Ordinary people cannot see its true form, and each of its claws carries the power to destroy worlds…" "If I'm not mistaken, it should be a Void Giant Beast called [Annihilation]." "In reality, it's not a true life form but a self-operating mechanism of certain rules in the Star Sea," Baihua Daoist quickly explained to everyone. "The world of my friend encountered such a terrifying existence while drifting in the void during the great catastrophe. The method of dealing with it was also simple: Annihilation is only interested in immortal cultivation worlds with life. Barren lands devoid of life do not enter its sight." "I just didn't expect that the Myriad Immortals Alliance could actually control such a beast that operates purely by rules and use it against us?" Baihua Daoist, who had initially underestimated the Myriad Immortals Alliance after their previous two easy failures, now looked extremely solemn. The others, upon hearing this, had their eyes light up. They then all looked towards Li Fan. Concealing the life aura of the entire world was not a difficult task for Li Fan. After a moment of contemplation, as the Annihilation beast continued its incessant attacks and the energy reserves of the Heavenly Mystery Fortress dwindled to one-third, the light barrier of the fortress emitted a soft, silvery glow. With the combined power of the Heavenly Mystery Fortress and the grand formation of the Spirit Wood Realm, the life aura of the entire world finally faded just before the defensive measures were completely breached.

Everyone held their breath and waited. After all, dealing with a monster like Annihilation, whose true form was invisible yet possessed ferocious power, was truly difficult. Fortunately, Baihua Daoist's guess was correct. Having lost its target of sensing life, the terrifying giant beast seemed to lose its motivation to attack and hovered aimlessly in place for a while. Then, as if sensing the delicious aura from the Xuanhuang Realm on the other side of the spatial rift, it turned its attention elsewhere. The spatial rift widened again, and the aura that made Li Fan's heart palpitate vanished instantly. Before the people of the Spirit Wood Realm could celebrate, the entire Spirit Wood Realm began to shake violently without any warning.

Chapter 1116: Strategic Transfer

"What… is this…?"

As the master of the Spirit Wood Realm, Li Fan in the Prison of Oblivion immediately sensed the anomaly. "The anchoring position of the Spirit Wood Realm within the Great Xuanhuang World is changing!" "They intend to uproot it, not to confront it head-on, but to destroy the small world directly?"

Previously, the Myriad Immortals Alliance had forcibly relocated the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven from Tianling State to the central imperial region. By its actual scale, the Spirit Wood Realm was not even as large as the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven. Even with Li Fan's reinforcement through formations, it was likely unable to withstand the Myriad Immortals Alliance's brute force relocation.

Furthermore, even though his true body was far from the battlefield, through the holy infant and his clones, Li Fan could sense the world's tremors and discern the method the Myriad Immortals Alliance was using for relocation. "The Great Star Flipping Formation!"

Li Fan's eyes flashed with a brilliant light. He had long coveted this magnificent grand formation created by King Xuan Tian, which the Xuanhuang Realm used to capture other immortal cultivation worlds. However, even though his Ultimate Dissolution Disk was nearing the level of an immortal artifact, he was still powerless against this Star Domain Formation, unable to forcibly deduce its secrets.

It seemed there were other unknown factors involved besides formations. When Li Fan had previously inquired the Heavenly Profound Mirror about the details of this formation, it had repeatedly evaded the question, using other grand formations to feign an explanation, preventing Li Fan from ever seeing the true face of this formation. To his surprise, he encountered it today while the Spirit Wood Realm was under siege.

In his sea of consciousness, the Dissolution Disk emitted a faint white light and rapidly flickered with excitement. "A glimpse through a tube can reveal the whole picture. The Dissolution Disk can infer the complete picture of the grand formation from this fragment." "As expected, by becoming rivals with the Myriad Immortals Alliance, one can witness more of their trump cards." Li Fan was immensely satisfied with the results of this trial.

As the Spirit Wood Realm's anchoring position gradually shifted, Li Fan's preliminary deduction via the Dissolution Disk yielded results. "The Heavenly Profound Mirror didn't lie; the grand formation is indeed severely damaged." "The Myriad Immortals Alliance is currently using the world-locking and world-dragging capabilities of the Great Star Flipping Formation that spans the starry sea."

"Judging by the speed at which the Spirit Wood Realm is being pulled, the formation's power is less than one-thousandth of its complete state. However, it is still more than enough to absorb the entire Spirit Wood Realm."

"No, no…" "Something is still missing." A situation that had never occurred before. The Dissolution Disk's deduction was interrupted. Despite its profound understanding of formations, it was unable to construct a formation with functions identical to the ancient Great Star Flipping Formation. This reaffirmed Li Fan's previous conjecture. This "Great Star Flipping Formation" was indeed more than just a simple formation.

"No wonder Transmitter Immortal Zhu, with his Transmitter-level qualifications, hasn't succeeded in restoring this formation after so many years and has to personally scour the void for remnants of immortal cultivation worlds." Li Fan mused.

Although he couldn't glimpse the entire formation, the Myriad Immortals Alliance was only utilizing a flawed version. Under Li Fan's instructions, the panicked and bewildered inhabitants of the Spirit Wood Realm quickly took action. As a formation manifested on the land of the Spirit Wood Realm, an invisible wave enveloped the entire small world, and the Spirit Wood Realm, being rapidly dragged along, suddenly seemed to disconnect. The shaking gradually subsided, and it finally stopped at an unknown location.

Li Fan immediately checked the Spirit Wood Realm's current position. It had moved from the eastern region of the Myriad Immortals Alliance to the southern region. It was alarmingly close to the World-Tearing Great Vortex. "They intend to use the natural power of the world tears to directly shatter the world? The Myriad Immortals Alliance truly has a good plan."

The Spirit Wood Realm's performance in dispelling the power of the Star Flipping Formation had far exceeded the Myriad Immortals Alliance's expectations. A division seemed to have occurred within their ranks, and they did not continue their attack. However, Li Fan could faintly sense that cultivators from the Alliance were continuously emerging from the surrounding void, encircling the Spirit Wood Realm. Baihua Daoist, Medicine King Sect, and others also sensed the current situation, their expressions turning grim.

"This is a desperate struggle of cornered beasts." "It seems my preparations this lifetime were not thorough enough. Next time I establish a base in the Spirit Wood Realm, perhaps I can incorporate the ability for the entire small world to teleport." "Before today, achieving this would have been difficult. But with the Myriad Immortals Alliance demonstrating it, hmmph…" Li Fan sneered inwardly. "Every blade aimed at Li Fan will be returned a thousandfold."

"My Lord Envoy, I believe we cannot passively wait any longer," Liu Ruchen said solemnly at this moment. "Although the Spirit Wood Realm's defenses are impeccable, they cannot withstand the Myriad Immortals Alliance's relentless attrition. Perhaps a desperate charge might offer a slim chance of survival." "The Medicine King True Cauldron has been modified over the years, its capacity expanded several times. It should be able to carry most people," Fang Zaiji added. Liu Ruchen's suggestion was approved by the vast majority. They all looked towards the holy infant Li Fan.

"Preserving the people and losing the land means both are preserved; preserving the land and losing the people means both are lost." "Since that is the case, everyone, prepare for the transfer," Li Fan agreed to the group's plan. The crowd immediately acknowledged the order and dispersed. Some were tasked with monitoring the entrance to the spatial rift, anticipating potential sneak attacks from the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Others began the rapid transfer of the Myriad Realms United Front's resources and population.

In fact, if the Spirit Wood Realm's anchored position had not shifted, Li Fan had prepared a plan for "cutting the tail to survive." This involved transferring to interconnected small worlds like the Empire and the Boundary-Leaving Realm. Then, they would destroy the spatial rift. Although this wouldn't completely prevent the Myriad Immortals Alliance from tracking them, it would buy them several days. However, unfortunately, during the recent relocation of the Spirit Wood Realm, its position shifted, severing the passages to the affiliated small worlds. At this point, the only possible direction for escape was to break through the Myriad Immortals Alliance's encirclement with sheer force.

Chapter 1117: Revenge is Certain

"The branch we established at the Scarlet River has not yet been discovered."

"If we manage to escape, we can regroup there."

"The Scarlet River possesses a unique power that should effectively block the Myriad Immortals Alliance's tracking," Li Fan said to Liu Ruchen, Baihua Daoist, and other core members of the United Front, having already devised a plan for after their escape.

Li Fan already had a vague idea of how the Spirit Wood Realm's exact location was exposed.

However, it was not yet time for retribution.

Li Fan did not utter the cold words of preferring death to surrender.

Bound by the power of the Faceless True Immortal, even if they wished to surrender, they likely wouldn't be able to.

Just as the members of the Spirit Wood Realm were preparing for a desperate fight, the holy infant Li Fan quietly approached the statue of the Faceless True Immortal.

The statue was merely a vessel.

The True Immortal's power had long been revived through the growing network of United Front members.

"But without a doubt, compared to other ordinary members, He would pay more attention to His own statue."

"In fact, I could choose to discard the statue and let the Myriad Immortals Alliance directly confront the True Immortal's power. However…"

"This trick can only be used once. I'm still counting on Her to play chess with the Immortals of the Immortal Ruins later."

Under the solemn gaze of the holy infant Li Fan, the statue of the Faceless True Immortal slowly became transparent.

Then, it vanished.

In the Prison of Oblivion.

Li Fan watched as the statue materialized out of thin air before him, his expression unreadable.

Where the True Immortal's network extended, the True Immortal's power could flow freely.

Li Fan had previously bestowed cultivation and knowledge upon the United Front members through this very method.

However, this was his first attempt at transferring a physical object.

"If I were to truly choose to completely pledge allegiance to the Faceless True Immortal, to dedicate myself without reservation and become a true envoy of the True Immortal, perhaps with the vast power of the True Immortal, I could relocate the entire Spirit Wood Realm with a single thought," Li Fan mused, gazing at the statue.

The Prison of Oblivion remained unchanged by the arrival of the True Immortal statue.

After storing the statue, Li Fan refocused his attention on the Spirit Wood Realm.

The members of the United Front were hastily preparing for their evacuation.

The holy infant Li Fan, meanwhile, was calmly setting up a formation.

Sensing the figure appearing behind him, Li Fan paused his movements slightly.

"My Lord Envoy… must it truly be like this?"

The speaker was Lin Ling, the spirit of the great tree of the Spirit Wood Realm.

"Once this formation is activated, everything within the Spirit Wood Realm will be turned to ash," Lin Ling said, her face deathly pale, looking at the faintly appearing silver lines on the ground.

Li Fan smiled.

"We are undertaking a strategic relocation. This fertile land of the Spirit Wood Realm, why should we let the Myriad Immortals Alliance have it cheaply? Of course, we must destroy it. As for you…"

"You've made considerable progress in formations during this period without my notice. You can even discern the purpose of my formation?" Li Fan scanned Lin Ling.

Lin Ling pursed her lips.

"I don't have that ability. It's just that my heart is one with the Spirit Wood. Facing a life-or-death crisis, I could sense it."

"We will return one day, won't we? Even if we temporarily cede this place to the Myriad Immortals Alliance, what does it matter? I believe that under Your Excellency's leadership, that day will not be far off."

Who would have thought that the tree spirit, once naive and ignorant, would utter such eloquent words of persuasion?

The holy infant paused his formation-setting.

After a moment of silence, Li Fan asked, "The Myriad Immortals Alliance was able to lock onto the Spirit Wood Realm's location so quickly. Should it not be that there is a traitor among us? Do you have any leads?"

Lin Ling's body trembled violently, and she exclaimed, "It wasn't me!"

Li Fan glanced at her.

"If it were you, would you still be standing here talking to me so calmly?"

Lin Ling instantly felt a sense of relief and exhaled weakly.

Having witnessed the Spirit Wood Realm grow from nothing over the years and Li Fan's various schemes, she had absolutely no intention of betrayal.

Compared to Li Fan, the people of the outside Xuanhuang Realm seemed much simpler.

Offending the Myriad Immortals Alliance might not necessarily lead to death.

But offending Li Fan…

Lin Ling wiped the sweat from her brow and thought for a moment before replying quickly, "Actually, it's not necessarily that there's a traitor within our United Front. Although the entrance to the Spirit Wood Realm is hidden, it cannot fool everyone in the world."

"At the very least, I know of someone who is very clear about it. Moreover…"

Lin Ling cautiously glanced at Li Fan before speaking softly, "He seems to have some grievances with you."

Li Fan's eyes narrowed instantly.

"Are you referring to the Ancient Earth Vein Tree?"

Lin Ling nodded.

"When I was on good terms with him before, he saw all our frequent comings and goings into the Spirit Wood Realm. Although we lost contact later, the location of our Spirit Wood Realm never changed. And wherever the earth veins reach, his gaze is there…"

"More importantly, I could faintly sense the Earth Vein Ancient Tree's scrutinizing gaze before. But ever since the Myriad Immortals Alliance attacked us, his gaze has never appeared again, as if he felt guilty. If he hadn't leaked the information, and we had a grudge against him, he should be gloating at our misfortune right now, watching us die," Lin Ling reasoned logically.

Li Fan nodded slightly upon hearing this.

"You have done well. Let's leave the Spirit Wood Realm for now."

The holy infant Li Fan stopped setting up the formation.

"As the saying goes, 'even a rusty sword needs sharpening after three days.' If you had reminded me earlier, it would have been even better."

Looking at Lin Ling, Li Fan encouraged her.

Lin Ling's face flushed with excitement.

After dismissing Lin Ling and telling her to prepare for escape, Li Fan gazed toward the outside of the Spirit Wood Realm.

"Heh heh, like his ancestors, he's so vengeful."

"Coincidentally, so am I."

Li Fan conceded Lin Ling's deduction.

After all, the Spirit Wood Realm's entrance was extremely secluded, known only to a few.

Once all of them were ruled out, the target could be quickly identified.

As for the possibility that Lin Ling was the mole and had fabricated her entire deduction to clear herself…

Li Fan trusted his own judgment and his understanding of people.

"The Ancient Earth Vein Tree…"

"Relying on being integrated with the earth veins, he dares to be so presumptuous. Humph."

In an instant, Li Fan had devised a plan to deal with him.

"The Ruomu Tree is very interested in these descendants of the land. If I can present it with a great gift, perhaps our relationship can improve."

However, dealing with the Ancient Earth Vein Tree would have to wait for the next lifetime.

Li Fan put aside this grievance for the moment and, once the inhabitants of the Spirit Wood Realm were adequately prepared, convened Liu Ruchen and the others again.

"After we break out, follow behind Heavenly Sun."

"Form this formation."

Li Fan passed down the formation to the people of the Spirit Wood Realm in a deep voice.

Chapter 1118: The Heavenly Venerate's Puppet Strings

Although it was merely a formation recently deduced by Li Fan, it was tailor-made for the inhabitants of the Spirit Wood Realm for their breakout. Centered around the Heavenly Sun immortal puppet, it leveraged its Longevity stage defensive capabilities to maximize the combat power of everyone else. This formation also had an effect similar to Soul Burning, capable of fully stimulating the potential of the cultivators within the formation for a short period, albeit at the cost of burning their souls.

Before gathering to form the array and evacuate, the holy infant Li Fan cast a final glance at the Spirit Wood Realm. "Next life's will be better." With not a trace of nostalgia, he led the group out of the Spirit Wood Realm. Initially, they expected to encounter heavy encirclement by the Myriad Immortals Alliance. However, to Li Fan's surprise, the void outside the Spirit Wood Realm was empty! Strangely, the pervasive feeling of being constantly monitored still lingered in everyone's hearts.

"Be careful!" Baihua Daoist was the first to cry out a warning. Her face was deathly pale, and cold sweat beaded on her forehead. Even when faced with Li Fan's coercion before, she had never been so flustered and discomposed. This was because the killing intent she had sensed from Li Fan previously was merely that of a conventional cultivator, whereas this…

"Pure malevolence…" Liu Ruchen of the Medicine King Sect and the others also adopted a grave stance, as if facing a formidable enemy. Despite the apparent emptiness ahead and no visible defenders, they all stopped their charge in unison. Including Li Fan, who was leading them. Their intuition told them that if they charged forward, they would die. As if targeted by a natural predator, their bodies stiffened, daring not to move.

At this moment, Heavenly Sun's voice reached Li Fan's ears. "Ahead. Longevity stage. Strange." Brief yet solemn. To the holy infant Li Fan, it was like a thunderclap.

"Longevity stage?"

"Has a Transmitter arrived?"

His heart felt as if it were being fiercely squeezed, even Li Fan's true body, hidden in the Prison of Oblivion, experienced a disturbance in his aura.

"It's possible. The Myriad Immortals Alliance already knew about the existence of a Longevity stage cultivator in the Myriad Realms United Front. After the initial probing, they wouldn't send more underlings to their deaths but would directly use decisive force to end it."

"But…"

"To personally intervene for the sake of avenging a few Transmitter Immortals? Isn't that beneath him?"

Li Fan was clearly caught off guard by the appearance of the Transmitter Heavenly Venerate. However, a multitude of doubts immediately arose in his mind. Judging by the Transmitter Heavenly Venerate's previous handling of the Transmitter Immortals, they were clearly treated as mere tools. Perhaps Transmitter Immortal Jiang had some special status, but other Transmitter Immortals were likely no different from ordinary cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm in his eyes. Would the Transmitter Sect personally descend to conquer for the sake of merely three Transmitter Immortals? Li Fan certainly didn't believe it.

Moreover, Li Fan had also experienced the vast might of the Transmitter Heavenly Venerate before. His aura was divine, boundless, and unfathomable. It was absolute that it had no connection to the "malevolence" that permeated their surroundings!

"If not the Transmitter, then who could it be?"

The Longevity Heavenly Venerates of the Xuanhuang Realm were few. Excluding the five Heavenly Venerates of the Five Elder Society, it couldn't be the newly ascended Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth. As his thoughts raced, a name, long buried deep in his memory and almost forgotten, suddenly surfaced in Li Fan's mind: the Eastern Extreme Heavenly Venerate!

Regarding the Eastern Extreme Heavenly Venerate, records in all the Myriad Immortals Alliance's scriptures mentioned only a few lines. His life seemed to have been deliberately erased. The only thing known was that the [Body Cleansing Spiritual Pool], used by the Myriad Immortals Alliance to remove the Immortal-Mortal Miasma from mortals, was invented by Him. Beyond that, there was nothing else. A generation's Longevity Heavenly Venerate, and the only Heavenly Venerate in the Myriad Immortals Alliance besides the Transmitter, was treated with such obscurity and incomprehensibility. If it wasn't His own request, then what happened to Him was indeed worth pondering.

Moreover, all the Longevity Heavenly Venerates of the Xuanhuang Realm were named after their paradoxical principles. Only this Eastern Extreme seemed to be merely His name.

… In a moment, countless thoughts flashed through Li Fan's mind. Meanwhile, the malevolent presence surrounding them, which had been watching intently, launched its attack on the people of the Spirit Wood Realm. The power of a Heavenly Venerate was truly different from ordinary cultivators. The Heavenly Sun immortal puppet, which originally emanated a pure white light, suddenly seemed to be stained with a hint of ominousness. Its light flickered unstably, and the Heavenly Sun's expression turned serious, as if struggling against that aura. Black spots appeared on the puppet's body, scattered here and there. The evil aura's attack bypassed Li Fan's formation's defenses, simultaneously striking every person in the Spirit Wood Realm.

Not everyone possessed the capital to contend with a Longevity Heavenly Venerate. In a flash, they were corrupted. Li Fan also witnessed the outcome of being completely corrupted by the evil aura: pupils vanishing, leaving only darkness in the eye sockets. Simultaneously, they launched attacks on their companions, having completely lost their minds. In an instant, the Spirit Wood Realm's team descended into chaos, showing signs of imminent defeat. And the enemy, still hidden in the darkness, had yet to reveal itself.

"Is this the combat power of a true Longevity Heavenly Venerate?"

"Defeat is acceptable. But to not even see His true form…"

Amidst the chaos, Li Fan's expression remained calm, and he focused his attention on Heavenly Sun. A dazzling crimson light suddenly erupted from within Heavenly Sun. Like a great sun in the heavens, it illuminated the surrounding dark space.

"Heavenly Sun's life…"

"Is no less than anyone else's!"

The Heavenly Sun immortal puppet's body instantly expanded by millions of times, becoming like a flame giant that split the heavens and earth, standing in the dark void. Circles of crimson flames erupted from its body, continuously spreading outwards, intending to incinerate the entire space. Under the scorching of Heavenly Sun's flames, the allied forces of the Spirit Wood Realm remained unharmed. Those corrupted cultivators, amidst piercing screams of horror, turned into black ashes. And the culprit, who had been hiding in the darkness all along, was finally forced to reveal its form!

The scene before them caused the holy infant Li Fan's eyes to narrow slightly. A tall, naked man stood in the air. His black hair cascaded to his ankles, and his body was covered in black patterns emanating an evil aura. Behind the naked man, countless threads could be vaguely seen emerging from the void and deeply embedding themselves into his body. The naked man's eyes were pure black, his expressionless. Just like those cultivators whose minds had been controlled.

"Longevity Heavenly Venerate, a Puppetry Strings puppet…"

This bizarre sight sent an uncontrollable chill through the hearts of everyone in the Spirit Wood Realm. Li Fan himself inhaled sharply.

"This is…"

"The Eastern Extreme Heavenly Venerate, who mysteriously disappeared, has become like this?"

"Although not dead, His existence is worse than death…"

"Who did this?"

"The Transmitter Immortals of the Myriad Immortals Alliance certainly don't have this capability."

"The only possibility is the Transmitter!"

In the Prison of Oblivion, Li Fan's true body instinctively clenched his fist.

Chapter 1119: Battle Between Two Heavenly Venerables

Regarding the horrors of the Prison of Oblivion, Zhang Fu had long heard of them. And after experiencing the brutal torture just now, he deeply understood the awfulness of the punishments here. Hearing Kou Hong's words and witnessing several cultivators driven mad and reduced to inhuman states, he knew he absolutely could not endure the tortures here. Thus, he decisively agreed to Kou Hong's proposal. "If all else fails, I can always betray this person and report him to earn merit," Zhang Fu thought.

However, all his schemes turned to naught after he followed Kou Hong in reciting an oath. "Compassionate True Immortal?" Zhang Fu initially didn't pay much attention to this so-called True Immortal. But later, whenever he harbored thoughts of betrayal, an inexplicable sense of impending disaster would arise. Zhang Fu finally realized that he had truly boarded a pirate ship.

Subsequently, Kou Hong and Zhang Fu slowly began their infiltration plan within the Prison of Oblivion. Every new prisoner, on the verge of their consciousness collapsing due to inhuman torture, would be approached by Kou Hong at the opportune moment. Under the illumination of the Compassionate True Immortal's divine power, these prisoners treated it as their last straw of hope, joining the prison break organization without hesitation.

As for the prisoners who had been confined for a long time but still retained basic self-awareness, they became Kou Hong's main targets for persuasion. However, these cultivators had been imprisoned for so long that some were suspicious and unwilling to trust anyone. Each persuasion required a significant amount of time and effort. Fortunately, the newly joined members also participated, so the progress of infiltrating the Prison of Oblivion was not too slow.

Three years later.

Amidst the echoing screams from the Prison of Oblivion, the private exchanges among the members of the prison break organization could be heard.

"Brother Kou, when will we act?"

"Yes, except for the deepest parts of the Prison of Oblivion, other areas have basically been conquered by our brothers. On the surface, this place still seems to be under the control of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. In reality, with just one command from Brother Kou, the Prison of Oblivion will change hands instantly."

"With the blessing of the Compassionate True Immortal's divine power over these years, we have all recovered our strength. Some brothers have even made further progress. One Dao Integration cultivator, sixteen Spirit Transformation cultivators, and over a hundred Nascent Soul cultivators… Compared to them, the guard force within the Prison of Oblivion is simply vulnerable."

"Heh heh, not only has our cultivation fully recovered. With the blessing of the Compassionate True Immortal's divine power, we can even stealthily bring in various external resources. I've been eating so much delicious food lately that I'm almost tired of it."

…

The crowd chattered, but they were all full of confidence in a collective escape from the Prison of Oblivion. Over the past three years, having witnessed the divine power displayed by the Compassionate True Immortal so many times, they had all become loyal believers of the True Immortal.

After a long discussion, Kou Hong finally spoke, "Initiating an uprising is easy, but what is more important is what happens after we get out. Once the Prison of Oblivion is breached, the Myriad Immortals Alliance will surely react immediately and launch a massive search. They won't give us much time to react, so we need to plan for the future before escaping."

Kou Hong's words stunned everyone.

"Future arrangements?"

"Could it be the sacred decree of the Compassionate True Immortal?"

Although they had joined the organization for three years, they only knew of the existence of the Compassionate True Immortal. They were completely unaware of the true name of the organization or its ultimate objective. Thus, they all looked towards Kou Hong with anticipation.

"Indeed, it is the True Immortal's trial. Only by completing the trial can one truly become a believer of the True Immortal and a member of the organization," Kou Hong's tone was filled with a sense of sacred mission. He then transmitted a grand formation and a map to everyone.

"Great Formation of All Spirits Under Heaven?" Upon seeing the name of the formation, the cultivators within the Prison of Oblivion were deeply shocked. According to the description, this formation had the ability to encompass heaven and earth and communicate with all realms. The crowd then studied the map.

The map depicted the territories within the Myriad Immortals Alliance, but marked with over a hundred small dots. Focusing their divine sense on these light dots, they were horrified to discover that they represented small worlds.

Kou Hong also spoke at this time: "The True Immortal's trial is not difficult. It just requires some time."

"Go to each small world and set up this [Great Formation of All Spirits Under Heaven]. Once each formation is completed, they will automatically connect, forming a formation network. Therefore, as soon as they are established, we will know of each other…" Kou Hong earnestly instructed.

At the same time, noticing the doubts of some cultivators in the group, he explained, "Do not worry. All the selected small worlds are worlds inhabited only by mortals. With your strength, you are more than capable of suppressing them within a short period. The Compassionate True Immortal has also bestowed the divine artifact [Heavenly Cauldron of All Creation] to help you transform the small worlds…"

"It can be said that the greatest test this time lies in your perseverance and faith."

Looking at the specific requirements of the trial, the cultivators each fell into contemplation. However, they had already been subtly influenced by the power of the Compassionate True Immortal, and considering that they would inevitably face pursuit from the Myriad Immortals Alliance after escaping the prison, hiding in mortal small worlds might not be a bad idea. Thus, without hesitation, they quickly accepted and began contemplating the details of their plans. After assigning each person their respective small world and discussing every minutiae of how to deal with unforeseen circumstances after escaping the prison, three months passed.

When the wardens of the Immortal Alliance escorted another escapee, preparing to cast him into the prison pillar for torment, they were horrified to see thousands of pillars in the Prison of Oblivion shattering in succession. Countless vicious prisoners, with ferocious eyes, locked onto him simultaneously. Under the overwhelming killing intent, he was instantly obliterated.

"Charge out, do not linger!" Kou Hong commanded in a low voice.

The crowd, like beasts released from their cages, rushed out of the Prison of Oblivion. All defensive formations were rendered useless as if they were mere decorations. Re-experiencing the sunlight, the prisoners roared, expressing their excitement. However, they did not linger there. After a simple directional identification, they swiftly shot towards their target small worlds. In the blink of an eye, the dark masses of felons vanished without a trace.

Not long after, the special envoy of the Myriad Immortals Alliance was alerted and led a team to investigate. Seeing the protective formations, which were not forcibly destroyed, they showed looks of rage. Squads of black-robed cultivators pursued the escaping felons, tracking their traces to hunt them down.

Chapter 1120: True Immortal's Faithful Disciple

Strictly speaking, Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi were not members of the Myriad Realms United Front. They were merely members of the precursor organization, the Congyun Mutual Aid Association. After the Congyun Mutual Aid Association was destroyed by the Transmitter Immortals, they lost contact with Li Fan. It was their unwavering faith in the Crimson Dust Compassionate Immortal that allowed them to vaguely sense the existence of the United Front. Now that the United Front was destroyed, as long as they themselves didn't reveal it, their past debt of gratitude to Li Fan would not be exposed.

Unfortunately, these two men were true to their nature. Upon hearing the Myriad Immortals Alliance's announcement regarding the extermination of the United Front, instead of hiding or fearing, they actively assassinated cultivators belonging to the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Although they knew that under the might of the Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth, cultivators could die and be reborn, they were determined to do so to repay Li Fan's kindness.

In this lifetime, guided by Li Fan, Dao Xuan Zi used the Canghai Pearl to establish his foundation, while Kou Hong used the Ten Thousand Mountains Cauldron. Their progress had been rapid over the years, and they had already reached the Golden Core mid-stage cultivation. However, in the face of the behemoth that was the Myriad Immortals Alliance, they were merely ants. After killing only a dozen or so insignificant Alliance cultivators, they were soon surrounded by the Myriad Immortals Alliance's Guardian Hall cultivators.

Dao Xuan Zi refused to be a prisoner and died laughing, self-detonating. Kou Hong had also intended to follow Dao Xuan Zi, but was stopped by the Alliance cultivators. His arms were severed, and one eye was destroyed before he was sent to the Prison of Oblivion by the Myriad Immortals Alliance for eternal suppression.

"You can only rely on your sharp tongue while you can still speak. I hope you can still be so tough after experiencing the torment of the formations here," the Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivator escorting him sneered coldly, unfazed by Kou Hong's continuous curses. Kou Hong, however, continued to curse incessantly.

To Li Fan's surprise, Kou Hong's subsequent performance exceeded his expectations. Li Fan knew too well the power of the formations within the prison pillars. Ordinary people could not endure such endless torment for long; they would instinctively cry out for mercy. Yet, Kou Hong, even when tortured to the brink of death and his consciousness blurred, never stopped cursing, albeit softly. "This is partly due to the brainwashing of the Faceless True Immortal, but it's also related to Kou Hong's own resolute will. Once he decides on something, he must complete it, even if it means death without regret."

Li Fan's first encounter with them involved being offered a Golden Core cultivation method for ten years of hard labor in the Myriad Immortals Alliance, but they refused. They were willing to risk their lives exploring sect ruins instead. Later, after finding the Nascent Soul True Scripture, the two brothers, as close as kin, fought to the death for a sliver of opportunity to attain Dao. And in this lifetime, after being saved from the mutated Immortal-Mortal Miasma by Li Fan, they joined the Mutual Aid Association and became devout seekers of the Crimson Dust Compassionate Immortal. These instances perfectly illustrated their personalities.

"He is a moldable talent, capable of being used. At the very least, he is more practical than those so-called geniuses," Li Fan thought, observing Kou Hong, who lay unconscious nearby with a resolute expression. His eyes showed a hint of approval.

As the Spirit Wood Realm faced imminent destruction and Li Fan led the United Front members in their escape, he had observed everyone's reactions. The prodigies of the Mountain and River Xuan Heavenly Sect, who had been swayed by Shang Tian, despite having sworn oaths before the statue of the Faceless True Immortal, showed no intention of fighting alongside the United Front at the moment of crisis. Instead, they exhibited regret and contemplated escape or surrender. In terms of loyalty alone, they were far inferior to Kou Hong.

Thinking this, a barely noticeable beam of light penetrated the prison pillar and flew towards the unconscious Kou Hong. Kou Hong's ferocious expression instantly softened somewhat. When Kou Hong woke up and realized something had appeared in his mind, his eyes flashed with surprise. However, he continued to feign defiance, denouncing the shameless actions of the Myriad Immortals Alliance while secretly studying the knowledge he had just acquired.

"This is… "

"A detailed explanation of formations?"

"And it's even the formation that constructs these prison cages in the Prison of Oblivion?"

"How could this appear in my mind?"

After a long while, Kou Hong's heart was greatly shaken, and he suppressed the urge to investigate further, deciding to first study the detailed explanation of the formation. Although he had only learned formations superficially before, this detailed explanation was profound yet simple, easy to understand. Coupled with Kou Hong's decent aptitude, within seven days, Kou Hong had barely grasped the basics.

At the same time, a thought flickered in his mind: "Could this be a trap?" "This is clearly a place where the Myriad Immortals Alliance imprisons serious offenders. Why would the overseeing formation be so simple? As a beginner, after only a few days of study, I can break it?"

Kou Hong secretly attempted to break the formation. Currently, his body was extremely weak, and his spiritual energy was suppressed, rendering him unable to use it. Yet, Kou Hong, by exerting all his strength to generate spiritual energy fluctuations, managed to cause a slight impact on the prison formation. The change was that when the Prison wardens activated the formation to torment Kou Hong again, the pain he felt was reduced by a few points!

"It's actually real?" Kou Hong, enduring the pain, was overjoyed. But he quickly calmed down and began to ponder the origin of the detailed explanation of formations in his mind. "I am merely a minor Golden Core cultivator. The Myriad Immortals Alliance has no reason to play games with me." "Moreover, the level of expertise displayed in this formation's explanation far exceeds that of the Myriad Immortals Alliance…" A divine name instantly appeared in Kou Hong's mind. "Crimson Dust Compassionate Immortal."

At the same time, a surge of warmth emerged from Kou Hong's body, circulating through his limbs and bones. It instantly broke through the Myriad Immortals Alliance's restrictions, nurtured and repaired Kou Hong's damaged body, and rapidly improved his cultivation. Sensing the earth-shattering changes within his body, Kou Hong stiffened, daring not to show any abnormality for fear of being discovered by others. In reality, his heart was already overflowing with tears. The great and benevolent Crimson Dust True Immortal had indeed not abandoned him!

"The United Front has been destroyed, and now there are probably not many True Immortal believers left in the world." "I am deep within this prison, and yet the True Immortal has suddenly bestowed a method of escape upon me…" Thinking this, Kou Hong's eyes lit up. He quickly lowered his head to conceal his inner excitement: "I understand. The Myriad Immortals Alliance destroyed the United Front. This is an irreconcilable hatred!" "An enemy of my enemy is my friend. Those imprisoned here are all mortal enemies of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. If I release them all…"

Chapter 1121: Immortal Alliance Overthrown In Prison

"Furthermore, perhaps I can even convert them into believers of the Compassionate True Immortal!" Looking at the countless prisoners around him, groaning in pain under the formation's torture, Kou Hong empathized and mused.

"However, this is a strictly guarded prison. Achieving this will require careful planning." Kou Hong's eyes flickered, and he once again used his usual angry shouts to conceal his true intentions. However, this time, he deliberately adopted a hesitant and weak tone, as if he was nearing his limit.

For the next period, Kou Hong used his superficial compliance to divert the wardens' attention from himself. Meanwhile, he frantically studied the detailed explanation of formations and secretly accumulated strength.

He had now realized that the miraculous bestowal of the Compassionate True Immortal, the stream of warmth that inexplicably appeared within his body, was actually the cultivation that cultivators yearned for. In conventional understanding, cultivation was accumulated only through day and night of arduous training, serving as the driving force for advancement. However, now, it was like water from an inexhaustible source, ceaselessly irrigating his body. His strength was also increasing at an unimaginably terrifying speed.

In just over half a month, he had directly broken through to the peak of the Golden Core stage. This further convinced Kou Hong that the inexplicable miracles happening to him were definitely the bestowal of the Compassionate True Immortal! Keep in mind that it took him over two hundred years to cultivate from a mortal to the mid-Golden Core stage. Now, breaking through was instantaneous.

Kou Hong originally thought that the peak of the Golden Core stage was the limit. However, what happened next completely shattered his perception and made him understand the power of a True Immortal!
