As is well known, to break through from the Golden Core stage to the Nascent Soul stage, one needs to absorb the spiritual energy of a grotto-heaven in the Xuanhuang Realm. Currently, Kou Hong was still confined within the Prison of Oblivion, naturally unable to meet this condition.

However, three days later, something that made Kou Hong tremble with astonishment occurred. When he circulated his spiritual energy to inspect his body, he discovered that a phantom grotto-heaven had faintly appeared in his Dantian! Upon sensing further, Kou Hong confirmed that this phantom grotto-heaven was not an illusion. It was real! A grotto-heaven was being born within his body!

Naturally, he attributed this to the bestowal of the Compassionate True Immortal. Kou Hong quickly accepted this fact and, with the help of this nascent grotto-heaven, officially broke through to the Nascent Soul stage after one month!

The anomalies caused by breaking through the cultivation realm were perfectly concealed by the True Immortal power surging within him, preventing the wardens of the Prison of Oblivion from detecting anything.

Kou Hong looked at his hands, feeling as if he were in a dream. The Nascent Soul stage, a realm he had only dared to dream of before, was now easily attained.

"Supreme Compassionate True Immortal, I, Kou Hong, do not know what virtue or merit I possess to receive such favor from you."

"I will certainly complete your instructions, even at the cost of ten thousand deaths."

In the shadows, Kou Hong's gaze towards the countless towering pillars of the Prison of Oblivion gradually firmed. After entering the Nascent Soul stage, Kou Hong's strength continued to increase daily, but his primary focus shifted to breaking the formations and rescuing the prisoners within the Prison of Oblivion.

"It is still too difficult to accomplish this alone."

"But where can I find helpers in this prison?" Kou Hong quietly observed his "neighbors," selecting suitable partners for cooperation.

Thus, after an unknown period.

One day, Li Fan smiled slightly upon receiving the message from Kou Hong. However, he merely pretended not to see it and gave no response.

Kou Hong tried a few more times, feeling helpless and finally giving up.

"Did I misjudge?"

"It shouldn't be."

Just as Kou Hong was facing difficulties, a newly incarcerated prisoner caught his attention. This person was not a member of the Myriad Realms United Front but was imprisoned here for violating the laws of the Immortal Alliance. Given the severity of his crimes, he likely had no chance of ever leaving.

"Now, you insects, you want to die and erase your sins at the slightest provocation."

"It's not that easy!"

"I will make it so you cannot die, and you will rot and despair in this sunless Prison of Oblivion for the rest of your life!" The Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivator responsible for escorting him said through gritted teeth.

The prisoner, however, remained silent, only looking disdainfully and with killing intent at his captor. But soon, under the suppression of the cruel formations, all that remained were screams of agony.

In extreme pain, a person's subconscious words always reflect their true thoughts. Kou Hong listened for several days to the words of this new neighbor and confirmed that he was a potential collaborator.

One day, after waiting for him to be tortured to the brink of death, Kou Hong quietly pierced through the formation and transmitted his message. The other party instantly opened his eyes, trying to locate Kou Hong. This was clearly futile.

After some communication between the two parties, Kou Hong learned his name: Zhang Fu. His crime was not major, merely embezzling one-third of the annual profits of the Dan Hall in Mo Ling State. In the past, such an offense, even if discovered, could have been resolved by spending some contribution points and calling in favors to escape disaster. But this time, coincidentally, one of his arch-rivals somehow learned of the matter and reported it directly to the headquarters of the Immortal Alliance.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters reacted with unusual speed this time. Before Zhang Fu could even begin to grease any palms, an envoy from headquarters arrived. After a brief investigation, the evidence was conclusive, and he was apprehended on the spot. Without undergoing the usual review process, he was directly brought to the Prison of Oblivion for perpetual imprisonment.

Zhang Fu then realized that he had likely been framed. He had thought himself doomed forever, but unexpectedly encountered a turning point.

"Help release the prisoners in the Prison of Oblivion?"

"This is a capital offense. Although everyone can be reborn now, I heard before I came in that the Myriad Immortals Alliance seems to have reached some kind of agreement with that Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth. Those who commit unforgivable sins within the Alliance will lose the chance to reincarnate. True death!"

"For example, those members of the Myriad Realms United Front seemed to be like this."

Unaware of Kou Hong's body trembling nearby, Zhang Fu continued to speak to himself.

"Although I am imprisoned here with no hope of leaving, it is still better than true annihilation."

"Perhaps one day, a general amnesty will come from the Myriad Immortals Alliance?" Zhang Fu initially did not agree and even secretly contemplated reporting this subversive act to redeem himself.

However, the following words changed his mind.

"Here, death is a form of liberation."

"If you don't believe me, just look at the people around you."

Chapter 1122: The Great Array of All Realms

Although it was merely a formation recently deduced by Li Fan, it was tailor-made for the inhabitants of the Spirit Wood Realm for their breakout. Centered around the Heavenly Sun immortal puppet, it leveraged its Longevity stage defensive capabilities to maximize the combat power of everyone else.

This formation also had an effect similar to Soul Burning, capable of fully stimulating the potential of the cultivators within the formation for a short period, albeit at the cost of burning their souls.

Before gathering to form the array and evacuate, the holy infant Li Fan cast a final glance at the Spirit Wood Realm. "Next life's will be better." With not a trace of nostalgia, he led the group out of the Spirit Wood Realm.

Initially, they expected to encounter heavy encirclement by the Myriad Immortals Alliance. However, to Li Fan's surprise, the void outside the Spirit Wood Realm was empty! Strangely, the pervasive feeling of being constantly monitored still lingered in everyone's hearts.

"Be careful!" Baihua Daoist was the first to cry out a warning. Her face was deathly pale, and cold sweat beaded on her forehead. Even when faced with Li Fan's coercion before, she had never been so flustered and discomposed. This was because the killing intent she had sensed from Li Fan previously was merely that of a conventional cultivator, whereas this…

"Pure malevolence…" Liu Ruchen of the Medicine King Sect and the others also adopted a grave stance, as if facing a formidable enemy. Despite the apparent emptiness ahead and no visible defenders, they all stopped their charge in unison. Including Li Fan, who was leading them. Their intuition told them that if they charged forward, they would die. As if targeted by a natural predator, their bodies stiffened, daring not to move.

At this moment, Heavenly Sun's voice reached Li Fan's ears. "Ahead. Longevity stage. Strange." Brief yet solemn.

To the holy infant Li Fan, it was like a thunderclap. "Longevity stage?" "Has a Transmitter arrived?" His heart felt as if it were being fiercely squeezed, even Li Fan's true body, hidden in the Prison of Oblivion, experienced a disturbance in his aura.

"It's possible. The Myriad Immortals Alliance already knew about the existence of a Longevity stage cultivator in the Myriad Realms United Front. After the initial probing, they wouldn't send more underlings to their deaths but would directly use decisive force to end it."

"But…" "To personally intervene for the sake of avenging a few Transmitter Immortals? Isn't that beneath him?" Li Fan was clearly caught off guard by the appearance of the Transmitter Heavenly Venerate. However, a multitude of doubts immediately arose in his mind.

Judging by the Transmitter Heavenly Venerate's previous handling of the Transmitter Immortals, they were clearly treated as mere tools. Perhaps Transmitter Immortal Jiang had some special status, but other Transmitter Immortals were likely no different from ordinary cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm in his eyes. Would the Transmitter Sect personally descend to conquer for the sake of merely three Transmitter Immortals? Li Fan certainly didn't believe it.

Moreover, Li Fan had also experienced the vast might of the Transmitter Heavenly Venerate before. His aura was divine, boundless, and unfathomable. It was absolute that it had no connection to the "malevolence" that permeated their surroundings!

"If not the Transmitter, then who could it be?" The Longevity Heavenly Venerates of the Xuanhuang Realm were few. Excluding the five Heavenly Venerates of the Five Elder Society, it couldn't be the newly ascended Heavenly Venerate of Rebirth.

As his thoughts raced, a name, long buried deep in his memory and almost forgotten, suddenly surfaced in Li Fan's mind: the Eastern Extreme Heavenly Venerate!

Regarding the Eastern Extreme Heavenly Venerate, records in all the Myriad Immortals Alliance's scriptures mentioned only a few lines. His life seemed to have been deliberately erased. The only thing known was that the [Body Cleansing Spiritual Pool], used by the Myriad Immortals Alliance to remove the Immortal-Mortal Miasma from mortals, was invented by Him. Beyond that, there was nothing else.

A generation's Longevity Heavenly Venerate, and the only Heavenly Venerate in the Myriad Immortals Alliance besides the Transmitter, was treated with such obscurity and incomprehensibility. If it wasn't His own request, then what happened to Him was indeed worth pondering. Moreover, all the Longevity Heavenly Venerates of the Xuanhuang Realm were named after their paradoxical principles. Only this Eastern Extreme seemed to be merely His name.

…

In a moment, countless thoughts flashed through Li Fan's mind. Meanwhile, the malevolent presence surrounding them, which had been watching intently, launched its attack on the people of the Spirit Wood Realm.

The power of a Heavenly Venerate was truly different from ordinary cultivators. The Heavenly Sun immortal puppet, which originally emanated a pure white light, suddenly seemed to be stained with a hint of ominousness. Its light flickered unstably, and the Heavenly Sun's expression turned serious, as if struggling against that aura. Black spots appeared on the puppet's body, scattered here and there.

The evil aura's attack bypassed Li Fan's formation's defenses, simultaneously striking every person in the Spirit Wood Realm. Not everyone possessed the capital to contend with a Longevity Heavenly Venerate. In a flash, they were corrupted.

Li Fan also witnessed the outcome of being completely corrupted by the evil aura: pupils vanishing, leaving only darkness in the eye sockets. Simultaneously, they launched attacks on their companions, having completely lost their minds. In an instant, the Spirit Wood Realm's team descended into chaos, showing signs of imminent defeat. And the enemy, still hidden in the darkness, had yet to reveal itself.

"Is this the combat power of a true Longevity Heavenly Venerate?" "Defeat is acceptable. But to not even see His true form…" Amidst the chaos, Li Fan's expression remained calm, and he focused his attention on Heavenly Sun.

A dazzling crimson light suddenly erupted from within Heavenly Sun. Like a great sun in the heavens, it illuminated the surrounding dark space. "Heavenly Sun's life…" "Is no less than anyone else's!"

The Heavenly Sun immortal puppet's body instantly expanded by millions of times, becoming like a flame giant that split the heavens and earth, standing in the dark void. Circles of crimson flames erupted from its body, continuously spreading outwards, intending to incinerate the entire space.

Under the scorching of Heavenly Sun's flames, the allied forces of the Spirit Wood Realm remained unharmed. Those corrupted cultivators, amidst piercing screams of horror, turned into black ashes. And the culprit, who had been hiding in the darkness all along, was finally forced to reveal its form!

The scene before them caused the holy infant Li Fan's eyes to narrow slightly. A tall, naked man stood in the air. His black hair cascaded to his ankles, and his body was covered in black patterns emanating an evil aura. Behind the naked man, countless threads could be vaguely seen emerging from the void and deeply embedding themselves into his body. The naked man's eyes were pure black, his expressionless. Just like those cultivators whose minds had been controlled.

"Longevity Heavenly Venerate, a Puppetry Strings puppet…" This bizarre sight sent an uncontrollable chill through the hearts of everyone in the Spirit Wood Realm. Li Fan himself inhaled sharply.

"This is…" "The Eastern Extreme Heavenly Venerate, who mysteriously disappeared, has become like this?" "Although not dead, His existence is worse than death…" "Who did this?" "The Transmitter Immortals of the Myriad Immortals Alliance certainly don't have this capability." "The only possibility is the Transmitter!"

In the Prison of Oblivion, Li Fan's true body instinctively clenched his fist.

Chapter 1123: Myriad Spirits Mastering True Immortal

As for the Prison of Oblivion, after such large-scale escapes, it was merely a name.

After the transfer of the remaining prisoners was completed, even the entrance to the Prison of Oblivion was no longer concealed.

It was thus abandoned.

Time flowed slowly, and no one came here anymore. It was as if the world had forgotten it.

After an unknown period, Li Fan's figure slowly emerged.

"Suppressed in the deepest part of the Prison of Oblivion, even I cannot discern his face."

"It requires three Law Transmitters to personally transfer him..."

"Interesting."

Instead of fleeing with the escaped cultivators immediately, Li Fan hid near the entrance. His purpose was to thoroughly explore the target imprisoned in the deepest part of the Prison of Oblivion, which he had been unable to approach for the past three years.

It wasn't that the formations in the deepest part were too advanced for Li Fan to break, but that the prison guards responsible for suppressing that prisoner were three combined Dao cultivators.

It seemed their sole purpose was to suppress that one prisoner. Even when the upper Prison of Oblivion was breached and countless fierce criminals escaped, they remained indifferent and did not intervene.

When the reception team from the Myriad Immortals Alliance arrived and was transferring prisoners, Li Fan managed to catch a glimpse of the prisoner.

It vaguely felt familiar to Li Fan.

However, it was obscured by secret techniques, so he couldn't be entirely sure.

"Before the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation is completed, it is not advisable to create further trouble."

"I will wait for the next life to investigate thoroughly."

"Now, all that needs to be done is to wait for the opportune moment and witness the world turned upside down!"

Li Fan looked toward the distant horizon, as if seeing the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation lighting up across thousands of mortal worlds.

The Myriad Spirits Grand Formation displayed to the multitude of villains was not its complete name.

This formation was deduced by the Ultimate Dissolution Disk within three years.

It represented the highest level of formation that the Dissolution Disk could deduce in its current state.

Based on the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation that once covered the Spirit Wood Realm, the Empire, and the Beastkin Realm as a prototype, it was further deduced and created into a world-shattering formation.

The full name of the formation is [Myriad Spirits of Heaven and Earth, Refining Gods of All Beings].

The primary function of this formation, and the goal Li Fan painstakingly pursued by freeing these prisoners from the Prison of Oblivion and making them work for him, was the four characters [Refining Gods of All Beings].

It was similar in principle to the Refining Gods of All Beings Formation displayed by Song He Song in Ningyuan City when fighting against Senior Brother Zhang in the Immortal Subjugation Illusionary Realm.

The killing power of the formation used the thoughts and will of the myriad spirits of heaven and earth and countless beings.

However, Li Fan's improved version...

Was hundreds of billions of times stronger.

Because the materials required to be consumed were hundreds of billions of times more.

At that time, with the power of a single city's mortals, Song He Song could almost force Senior Brother Zhang into a desperate situation, forcing him to reveal the secret of his Violet Core Immortality.

As for Li Fan, he used thousands of small worlds and trillions of living beings in the Xuanhuang Realm, all for the purpose of briefly holding back the Faceless True Immortal.

During the three years of hiding in the Prison of Oblivion after the Spirit Wood Realm was destroyed by the Myriad Immortals Alliance, Li Fan had been constantly contemplating and reviewing his final world-destroying plan.

After all, it was his first engagement with True Immortal power. Even if he was borrowing strength to fight, or watching from the sidelines as immortals battled, it still meant infinite risk.

After all, these two were truly transcendent immortals, not mere Foundation Establishment cultivators.

If they could be so easily manipulated, how could they be worthy of the name True Immortal?

Failure would result in eternal damnation.

Especially after experiencing the encirclement by the Myriad Immortals Alliance, which revealed unexpected trump cards and directly annihilated the Spirit Wood Realm, Li Fan became unprecedentedly cautious about his world-destroying plan.

He accounted for every possibility.

Thus, he discovered a problem he had previously taken for granted and overlooked. In Li Fan's original plan, he would first incite the power of the Immortal Ruins Immortals, and then, by virtue of this transcendent power, provoke a reaction from the Faceless True Immortal.

Indeed, living beings always subconsciously react to threats.

In simulated predictions, the Faceless True Immortal and the Immortal Ruins Immortals should first notice each other and fight amongst themselves, while overlooking Li Fan, the instigator of all this.

But this was only under ideal circumstances.

What if, after ascending to immortality, their thought processes were no longer the same as mortals?

Or, what if they sensed the [Return to Truth] on Li Fan's person?

Instead of immediately locking onto an equally matched opponent, what if they first focused on Li Fan?

If he made no preparations, being targeted by a True Immortal would likely leave him no time even to flee to the Netherworld and forcefully return to truth.

The more he thought about it, the more restless Li Fan became.

Thus, he finally decided that he had to find a way to at least buy himself a sliver of time.

And the [Myriad Spirits of Heaven and Earth, Refining Gods of All Beings] Grand Formation was the final answer provided by the Dissolution Disk.

The gap between cultivators and mortals, and between True Immortals and cultivators, was like a chasm.

But when numbers reached a certain point, a terrifying qualitative change could occur.

"Falling into the endless sea of the will of trillions of beings, even a True Immortal would surely have a moment of wavering."

"That moment of stunned confusion, bought for me, is the only chance of survival."

The power of a True Immortal could indeed instantly destroy Xuanhuang.

However, if things developed as Li Fan predicted, after being targeted, the True Immortal, in order to capture this ant secretly plotting, would not directly destroy the Xuanhuang Realm.

This offered Li Fan an opportunity.

"Heh heh, thousands of mortal worlds, countless beings' thoughts and wills."

"What an immense power this is. Yet, no matter how I deduce it, I can only impede them for a moment."

"This gap in absolute strength..."

"It truly makes one yearn for it."

Li Fan stood with his hands behind his back, silent.

Constrained by the power of the Faceless True Immortal, those vicious prisoners would obediently complete the construction of the Grand Formation.

Li Fan did not need to worry about this.

And once the formation was built, it would no longer be under their control.

"The day the Refining Gods Formation is complete, will be the day Xuanhuang is destroyed."

"It's close, perhaps within a year."

And during this period, Li Fan only needed to wait patiently.

At this final moment of this lifetime, Li Fan still had some finishing touches to make.

He first went to Tianling State, to the original location of the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven.

Since the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven, which had been developing for an unknown number of years, was devoured by Li Fan, a new Five Elements Grotto-Heaven began to form in this place called the [Root of Heaven and Earth], an intangible void.

However, this process was particularly long.

And it was only now that a nascent form of the grotto-heaven was vaguely appearing.

Li Fan ambled through the void, circulating his Fate Twisting Heavenly Dao divine ability, observing the principles of heaven and earth.

Feeling the rhythm like a beating heart, Li Fan narrowed his eyes, carefully awaiting the hint from Return to Truth.

From this innate treasure of his, Li Fan vaguely sensed a hint of dissatisfaction.

Chapter 1124: The Blood-Red Great Array Rises

Li Fan had felt the emotions of [Return to Truth] to varying degrees before. The tremor when he first encountered an Eternal Relic, and the desire when facing Mr. Bai's skull. Now, when Li Fan attempted to "feed" the nascent Five Elements Grotto-Heaven to Return to Truth, Return to Truth again provided feedback. "Not very satisfied. Meaning, it's barely acceptable."

A cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. Countless red threads flew out from within his grotto-heaven, like billions of tentacles, plunging into the void of the [Root of Heaven and Earth]. From this mother body, he seized ownership of the nascent grotto-heaven. The Root of Heaven and Earth was only responsible for passively nurturing the grotto-heaven. Therefore, when the creation, destined to leave it, was slowly stripped away by Li Fan, it did not provoke much violent resistance.

Instead, the nascent grotto-heaven itself seemed to sense something. It unleashed waves of resistance, trying to prevent Li Fan's devouring. But how could a newborn infant compare to a robust adult sibling? Without suspense. The nascent grotto-heaven, amidst continuous faint rumbling sounds, was pulled into the illusory projection of the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, which resembled a background painting. Until it was completely swallowed and disappeared.

"Hum hum hum..." A sharp ringing sound pulsed in Li Fan's ears, and the scene before him seemed to dim for a moment. After everything returned to normal, Li Fan looked at his Return to Truth panel.

"Current usable anchor count: 3"

"One was added. Indeed, it was feasible. After the Golden Core laws could no longer satisfy Return to Truth's appetite, it could only seek higher-grade Nascent Soul Grotto-Heavens next." Although he had verified his guess and increased the usable anchor point for Return to Truth by one, Li Fan did not feel particularly happy. Instead, he was constantly recalling the emotion Return to Truth had just expressed. Bland, yet he couldn't bear to discard it. But under Li Fan's insistence, Return to Truth ultimately devoured the nascent grotto-heaven.

"Now it's a grotto-heaven, but what will it desire in the future? A small world, a cultivation world? Or the upcoming changes in the new law system, the 'Soul of Heaven and Earth'?"

"However, regardless of what it is, it's time to tease its appetite a little. Being picky is not a good habit."

Li Fan stood alone in the dark void. After pondering for a long time, he slowly departed.

Emerging from the [Root of Heaven and Earth], Li Fan then went to the location of the Blood-Colored River. Due to the protection of the remaining power of the Fishing Pond, this place had still not been discovered by the Myriad Immortals Alliance. The surviving cultivators in the outpost were the last remaining foundation of the Myriad Realms United Front. They already knew the news of the annihilation of the Spirit Wood Realm headquarters. While filled with sadness and anger, not a single person's faith in the Crimson Dust Compassionate True Immortal wavered. Because they could still feel the Compassionate True Immortal's omnipresent divine power in their meditations.

The cultivators Li Fan sent to the Blood-Colored River to search for historical fragments were basically young people filled with fervent passion. Their cultivation did not exceed the early Golden Core stage at most. The Myriad Immortals Alliance was powerful, and although their desire for revenge was intense, they knew they were no match for them. Thus, they could only lie low for now and secretly accumulate strength. Without support from headquarters, and having lost their original backing, they could only place their hope for revenge on that vast blood-colored river. With steadfast faith, disregarding their depleting lifespans, they repeatedly threw themselves into it, attempting to explore its mysteries. Over three years, out of the original more than a hundred people, only thirty-three survived. And these survivors had all suffered great damage to their lifespans. Despite their young age, they had all turned white-haired, appearing like elderly individuals. However, they were not without gains.

Li Fan studied the insights they had summarized.

"Compared to pure profit-driven motives, those bearing bone-deep hatred can maintain greater clarity of mind when exploring the Blood-Colored River."

"Projecting the Blood-Colored River seems to have a similar attraction. For example, we avengers are more likely to observe cultivators in history who also harbored immense hatred."

"Besides merely recording images, perhaps we can even bring back actual things that existed in history. It seems to be a manifestation of the power of the [Blood-Colored River]. However, the probability of triggering it is too low. Since the creation of [Seeking the Profound], this phenomenon has only occurred once. We are currently researching the conditions required to achieve this goal..."

Li Fan diligently noted down all this valuable research material. He also remembered the names of the cultivators responsible for diligently compiling and recording these results. Chen Chen.

"Not bad. Previously, he didn't seem to stand out among the crowd. Only now, in the desperate situation of the United Front's destruction, has he finally displayed his leadership potential."

"He is a talent worth cultivating. He can be utilized earlier in the next life. Hmm, let me see which small world he comes from..."

After achieving his goals at the Blood-Colored River, Li Fan did not reveal himself or disturb them. Instead, he let these people continue their mission. In any case, after a year, the outcome would be the same.

Li Fan quietly departed and then visited numerous other locations such as the Boundary-Leaving Realm, the Empire, and the Netherworld. He completed the harvesting of achievements and repeatedly tested and verified his escape plan.

...

The river of time flowed forward. On this day, Li Fan, who was tinkering with a Heavenly Profound Mirror, suddenly looked up and gazed into the distance. The first Myriad Spirits Grand Formation had been completed. Li Fan's gaze instantly penetrated layers of spatial obstruction, reaching the mortal world where the formation was located.

The cultivator responsible for building this formation felt the reward of increased cultivation bestowed by the Crimson Dust Compassionate True Immortal, his face filled with excitement. Guided by the unseen hand, he immediately activated the Grand Formation.

This mortal world was larger than Li Fan's homeland, Great Xuan. However, as the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation activated, the originally clear blue sky was suddenly stained with a trace of eerie crimson. The crimson color spun back and forth in the sky, like a paintbrush, eventually transforming into a grotesque and terrifying blood-colored giant eye. The giant eye coldly gazed at the sentient beings below, like the eye of a god.

All living beings in heaven and earth felt an inexplicable sense of extreme dread in their hearts at this moment. Under instinctive fear, their bodies trembled uncontrollably and they collapsed to the ground. Although nothing had happened yet, the emotion of despair had already spread across the land. Of course, there were beings who dared to resist this blood-colored giant eye. But all they could do was curse the heavens in a futile rage.

The cultivator who had personally built the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation of this world stared blankly at the blood-colored giant eye in the sky. He muttered, "No, no, how could this happen?"

Chapter 1125: Crossing the Tribulation to Save Oneself

"The Myriad Spirits Grand Formation connects all the heavens and myriad realms. Why would such a strange change occur after the formation was completed? Something must have gone wrong."

An extreme sense of unease welled up in his heart, and the cultivator was about to shut down the formation.

But...

It was already too late.

The formation inexplicably began to operate on its own.

The blood-colored giant eye slowly opened, revealing a bizarre vertical pupil.

Boom!

The entire mortal world began to tremble violently.

Countless beams of blood-red light rose from the land, like pillars of light, converging into the blood-colored giant eye in the sky.

After a moment of stupefaction, once he understood what had just happened, the cultivator's face was instantly filled with despair and terror.

Because the instant the blood-colored vertical pupil appeared, all living beings in this mortal world were instantly killed.

They turned into blood-red light and were absorbed by the blood-colored pupil.

The cultivator's body trembled incessantly, and an endless chill enveloped his heart.

Although he had committed no small sins himself, compared to the act of instantly killing a world's inhabitants, they were of a different order of magnitude.

"We were all deceived. What compassionate True Immortal..."

"This is clearly an incomparably terrifying evil god!"

The scenes from the past four years came to mind, and unspeakable fear gradually consumed the cultivator.

But at this moment, the last shred of conscience remaining in his heart suddenly awakened him from his despair.

A beam of hope erupted in the cultivator's eyes. He suddenly remembered something: "No, I can't let others repeat the same mistake as me. I must quickly notify them..."

Just as the cultivator was about to flee this place in disarray, he discovered that the blood-colored vertical pupil in the sky had, at some unknown time, locked onto him.

And just as the cultivator's body turned cold, thinking he would die under the blood-colored giant eye.

It was as if a gentle breeze swept through heaven and earth, and then a phantom figure inexplicably materialized.

Instantly, it drew the attention of the blood-colored vertical pupil in the sky.

And far away in the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan narrowed his eyes slightly.

He was not unfamiliar with the phantom figure.

"Mr. Bai?"

"This is caused by killing too many beings at once, leading to a sudden resurgence of the Mortal-Immortal Miasma, triggering a countermeasure?"

The phantom figure stood between heaven and earth. Although its facial expression could not be seen, an boundless rage could be felt from its being.

The phantom figure's gaze swept across this land and then locked onto the only survivor in this place, the cultivator who had set up the formation.

The cultivator immediately felt he could not move, and a sense of mortal danger surged in his heart. He struggled to say something.

The phantom figure did not listen to his explanation at all.

A wave of energy instantly crossed a thousand miles, descending from the phantom figure to the cultivator.

The cultivator's body stiffened abruptly.

Then, streaks of hair turned from black to white, his skin wrinkled, like dead wood...

In the blink of an eye, the cultivator transformed from a middle-aged appearance into an elder on the verge of death.

Then, he completely turned into a skeleton.

And fell from the air.

After completing this act of vengeance, Mr. Bai's phantom figure looked at the now blank world with no other living beings, a hint of sadness appearing on his face.

With a final, reluctant glance, he dissipated with the wind.

...

In the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan shook his head slightly.

"I didn't expect the Mortal-Immortal Miasma to have such a form."

"No wonder the cultivators of the Xuanhuang Realm so quickly agreed to the proposal for mortal migration back then; they must have discovered this secret."

"Revenge has its due, and accounts must be settled. Whoever set up the formation, go find them. It has nothing to do with me," Li Fan said with a cold smile.

"It conveniently saved me the trouble of dealing with it."

The demise of one wicked individual did not attract the attention of the other wicked individuals.

As more and more formations were built and integrated into the Refining Gods network, Li Fan drew closer to his final goal of this lifetime.

He looked at the countless consciousnesses of beings within the Refining Gods formation. Even as the mastermind behind it all, and considering himself qualified to disregard all worldly matters after obtaining Return to Truth, he still felt a prickle of unease and dared not look directly at it for too long.

"The power of infinite beings is truly terrifying and awe-inspiring."

"I think even True Immortals would pale in comparison in this sea of beings."

Li Fan's heart, as cold as ten thousand years of ice, was actually stirred by a faint tremor at this moment.

However, soon, his gaze became firm again.

"All of this is necessary."

"The immortal path is severed. Even figures like Heavenly King of Rebirth, King Xuan Tian, and Mr. Bai are trapped here for eternity."

"Only by finding a true method of liberation can everything be resolved in the end."

"Otherwise, even if I do nothing, the entire Xuanhuang Realm will ultimately face destruction."

...

Li Fan's gaze became cold once more.

Under his instruction, the construction speed of the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation accelerated again.

Finally, this supreme Grand Formation covering numerous mortal worlds was meticulously completed.

And at this very moment, five paper figures from the Tribulation Crossing Sect, who had been by Li Fan's side, reappeared.

This time, they did not nag Li Fan.

Instead, they all looked up at the sky of the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Strange, strange. Why is it that after just a nap, the Xuanhuang Realm seems to be accelerating its change somewhat uncontrollably?"

"Could it be that the suction of the Immortal Ruins has intensified?"

"Such strange things have not happened for many years. The magnitude of the change was limited, and we didn't notice it immediately..."

The five small figures bickered amongst themselves, completely ignoring Li Fan's presence.

After Li Fan's careful observation, he realized that they were not the same ones who had occasionally advised him before.

Instead, they were figures who had never appeared before.

It seemed they held quite high positions in the Tribulation Crossing Sect and were responsible for monitoring the crisis in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Li Fan had no intention of communicating with them.

Instead, he directly activated the formation and forcibly recalled them into the Book of Tribulation Crossing.

"Hmm?"

Such a drastic action quickly alerted the five small figures.

They stared at Li Fan, their expressions slowly turning to fear.

"So you were always..."

"Not good!"

The Book of Tribulation Crossing trembled violently, its pages flipping autonomously without any wind.

It seemed as if a large number of paper figures were about to surge out from within.

However, before they could achieve anything, under the restraint of invisible power, the five small figures were forcibly pulled into the Book of Tribulation Crossing.

The book then slowly closed.

But it continued to twitch and struggle non-stop.

Li Fan's expression remained unchanged, as he continuously reinforced the sealing formation.

Until the Book of Tribulation Crossing finally became still.

"Since you choose to be a turtle hiding in its shell, then continue to be one."

"The Xuanhuang Realm does not need you to save it."

Li Fan said lightly, suppressing the Book of Tribulation Crossing in the deepest part of the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven.

The Myriad Spirits Grand Formation, Refining Gods of All Beings, had been fully deployed.

Li Fan's final failsafe had been put in place. Next, he would prepare to launch his ultimate plan.

"After my observation over the past year, I have confirmed that the Law Transmitter is not in the Xuanhuang Realm."

"Just like before."

Chapter 1126: Still Truly Before the Immortal

Headed towards the Jiu Shan Prefecture.

"Today is a good day." Zhao Xian wrote his name on the golden contract. After a stream of golden light entered his body, establishing the contract, he laughed heartily.

The group from the Five Elder Society in the shop also put away their contracts, their faces beaming with joy, and echoed his sentiments.

For the rest of the afternoon, Zhao Xian engaged in more detailed negotiations with the Five Elder Society regarding the trade agreement. Only after escorting them to the designated guest dwellings in the city for rest did Zhao Xian heave a sigh of relief.

Instead of returning to his own dwelling, he turned back into the shop and descended into the underground secret chamber.

Looking at the Faceless stone statue hidden in the darkness, Zhao Xian's expression was complex, and his thoughts churned.

Ever since the Myriad Realms United Front was annihilated by the Myriad Immortals Alliance and listed as a permanent target for extermination, Zhao Xian, as the secret agent of the United Front in Jiu Shan Prefecture, had been living in fear.

He was restless every day, often hallucinating that the Myriad Immortals Alliance had found him and arrested him.

Without supplies from the United Front, the shop's inventory was severely affected. Customer traffic declined daily, and it was almost unsustainable. Finally, after begging and borrowing, and using all his accumulated wealth from the past few years, he managed to rebuild the supply chain.

"Fortunately, it's all over now." Zhao Xian thought to himself.

The turmoil surrounding the United Front had subsided.

During the period when the Myriad Immortals Alliance's search was most intense, they had not discovered Zhao Xian's true identity. There should be no more danger in the future.

After several years of diligent management, the shop's business had returned to normal. Recently, he had even reached a commercial agreement with a merchant caravan from the Five Elder Society. The fixed trade goods alone were worth tens of millions of contribution points annually.

"Although I no longer receive True Immortal rewards, the profits from the shop alone are enough to support my cultivation to the Nascent Soul realm."

"With the destruction of the United Front, I don't have to hand over profits and can keep them all for myself. I'm actually living more comfortably than before..." Zhao Xian thought with some pride.

"Indeed, fortune and misfortune are intertwined, and life is unpredictable."

Taking one last look at the Faceless stone statue, Zhao Xian had already decided to permanently seal this underground secret chamber.

From now on, no one would ever know his secret of once being a member of the Myriad Realms United Front.

"True Immortal's compassion, I believe He will not blame me." Zhao Xian respectfully bowed one last time before sealing the secret chamber.

Having completed all this, Zhao Xian felt as if he had been reborn, shedding a heavy burden.

However, on his way back to his dwelling, he looked up at the azure sky of the Xuanhuang Realm and, for some reason, a sense of unease suddenly surged within him.

Zhao Xian had always been confident in his intuition, and he immediately stopped in his tracks.

Carefully recalling every detail of his recent life and pondering for a long time, Zhao Xian could not find anything amiss.

"Strange..."

The chaotic feeling in his heart intensified. Zhao Xian suddenly felt something and looked at the people around him.

Upon seeing this, he immediately broke out in a cold sweat.

It turned out that it wasn't just him.

In the free trade city of Jiu Shan Prefecture, all the cultivators strolling on the streets at this moment seemed to vaguely sense something was wrong. Their hearts were in turmoil, and their expressions were nervous.

Some even broke out in cold sweat on their foreheads, their steps faltering.

"This..." Zhao Xian's mind suddenly flashed with the image of ants collectively moving house before a rainstorm.

"Could it be that a disaster of unimaginable proportions is about to occur?"

Zhao Xian suddenly and inexplicably remembered the origin of the Nine Mountains Trade Prefecture.

Originally, this place had been a chaotic region with mixed factions and nine mountains standing tall. Due to the battles between the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elder Society, the mountains and rivers were flattened into plains under the gaze of the Heavenly Venerates' manifestations.

Thus, the current prosperous Jiu Shan Prefecture came into being.

"Could it be that what happened that day is about to happen again?" The thought surfaced in Zhao Xian's mind, causing him to shudder involuntarily.

Although logic told him that neither the Myriad Immortals Alliance nor the Five Elder Society would go to war in Jiu Shan Prefecture again for their mutual benefit, the current anomaly made him certain that a catastrophe was imminent!

"Flee!"

In just a moment, Zhao Xian made his decision.

That's right, he was greedy.

He also wanted to become a great cultivator of Golden Core stage and rule a region.

But the prerequisite for all this was to save his own life.

With the skills he had honed in Jiu Shan Prefecture over the years, even if he returned to being penniless, he could rise again in another place.

Moreover, the most valuable items in the shop were always kept on his person.

With this in mind, Zhao Xian immediately changed direction. Disregarding the city's prohibitions, he sped toward the border of Jiu Shan Prefecture.

His abnormal behavior naturally attracted the attention of the cultivators in Jiu Shan City. As if triggering a chain reaction, they also began to flee without any reason.

It was like the instinctive struggle of wild beasts sensing a life-or-death crisis.

And the facts proved that these cultivators' premonitions were not wrong.

They had not fled very far when a terrifying fluctuation descended from behind them.

The sky instantly darkened.

Countless cultivators were swallowed by an unknown terrifying existence without even a chance to scream.

Sensing the disappearance of tens of thousands of lifeforces behind him in an instant, extreme fear overwhelmed his mind.

At this moment, his thoughts also began to race at an unprecedented speed.

"Something terrible must have befallen Jiu Shan Prefecture."

"My strength, clearly, cannot survive this disaster."

"There is still a long distance to the border of Jiu Shan Prefecture. There is simply not enough time to escape to a safe place."

"The reason Jiu Shan Prefecture does not have a Law Transmission formation is because the spatial structure here is extremely unstable. Activating a teleportation formation rashly will not only fail to reach the target location but may also result in being randomly teleported to other places, or even getting lost in the void..."

"But there is still hope of survival..."

Zhao Xian's thoughts raced, and his body responded instinctively.

He directly activated the random teleportation formation diagram stored in his spatial ring.

The surrounding scene became distorted and blurred.

After a brief dizziness, Zhao Xian escaped Jiu Shan Prefecture and arrived at an unfamiliar place.

But the scene before his eyes gave him no joy of escaping death.

Instead, he felt as if he had fallen into an ice cellar, his mind completely blank.

It was as if he were floating high in the sky, looking down upon the Xuanhuang Realm.

Thousands of black dots densely appeared on the ground.

Like black abysses, devouring everything around them.

The entire world seemed to be torn apart by these black dots, forming curled-up pieces of parchment.

The cultivators on the ground, no matter how they struggled, could not last even a moment in the black domain.

They all turned into distorted beams of light and disappeared into the black dots.

...

"So the disaster is not just happening in Jiu Shan Prefecture?"

"What is this?"

"Is the end of the world coming? Is the world about to be destroyed?" Zhao Xian was stunned.

But soon, his attention was drawn to another wondrous sight that complemented this apocalyptic scene.

Above the Xuanhuang Realm, which had been torn into thousands of twisted parchment-like fragments, a painting resembling spilled ink appeared.

In the ink painting, countless scenes shifted rapidly at every moment.

And before this bizarre painting stood a figure with his hands behind his back.

As if sensing Zhao Xian's gaze from afar, the figure turned its head.

Before he could even clearly see the other party's face, Zhao Xian's body and soul exploded into countless fragments due to the inability to withstand the immense pressure.

He died without a complete corpse.

"Hmm?"

A moment later, Li Fan already knew why this unlucky fellow had come here.

He shook his head slightly, no longer paying attention to him, and focused his attention on the myriad changes in heaven and earth erupting from the Xuanhuang Realm before him.

Those countless black dots were naturally the power of the Immortals from the Immortal Ruins, triggered by the bait puppets flying towards the Immortal Ruins after he launched his world-destroying plan.

The power of the Immortal Ruins Immortals, guided by the sense of connection established by those puppets, was transmitted into the Xuanhuang Realm, causing immense world-destroying calamities.

And as Li Fan had expected, the moment the power of the Immortal Ruins appeared, it triggered a spontaneous reaction from the Faceless True Immortal statues he had arranged beside the bait puppets.

These Faceless True Immortal statues had no physical form; they were condensed purely from the essence of the Faceless True Immortal's source power by Li Fan.

As the world-destroying power of the Immortal Ruins swept towards them, an indescribable force inexplicably emerged from the source power essence.

Like a butterfly breaking out of its cocoon, or a flower falling and a fruit appearing.

The source power essence melted away like ice and snow, disappearing directly, replaced by power that mortals could not comprehend, colliding with the power of the Immortal Ruins.

It was like two giant waves crashing into each other, creating countless splashes.

In an instant, the Xuanhuang Realm was torn into thousands of fragments.

But it seemed that it was precisely due to the struggle between the two that the Xuanhuang Realm, already riddled with holes, did not completely shatter immediately.

"It seems my concerns were unnecessary."

"The Faceless True Immortal does not seem to have noticed my existence."

Li Fan thought to himself.

"Extracting the essence of heaven and earth to obtain its spirit."

Muttering to himself, he absorbed the bizarre ink painting before him into the illusory projection of the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven behind him.

Before Li Fan's eyes, scenes of the Xuanhuang Realm's past, present, and future based on its original trajectory played out like a revolving lantern.

In addition, Li Fan sensed a strong desire for survival and unwillingness to cooperate within it.

The scene spun rapidly like a vortex, as if something was about to be born from within.

Upon careful consideration, Li Fan actually sensed the Xuanhuang Realm's intention to seek cooperation.

"A world on the verge of death is no different from a person."

"Although it discovered I was falsifying the Heavenly Dao, for the sake of a slim chance of survival, it not only did not blame me but was even willing to cooperate with me..."

"This is something I did not anticipate before."

Li Fan snorted coldly and did not agree to the Xuanhuang Realm's request.

Nor did he directly refuse.

Instead, he accelerated the speed of extracting the essence of heaven and earth.

As countless potential future changes were integrated into his body, the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven also began to undergo earth-shattering changes.

In stark contrast to the Xuanhuang Realm, which was at its end, the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven presented an unprecedented scene of prosperity.

The five elements circulated and tended towards fusion.

Gold, wood, water, fire, and earth reunited, and the boundaries within each cave-heaven, which were originally very distinct, slowly disappeared.

A new world, full of infinite vitality, was taking shape.

...

At this moment, Li Fan, who was on the verge of successfully advancing to the Nascent Soul stage, inexplicably felt a sense of danger.

A beam of light instantly arrived from beyond the void.

"No!"

After clearly seeing the current appearance of the Xuanhuang Realm, he let out a roar.

Then, in an instant, he traversed the vast spatial distance and locked onto Li Fan.

Their eyes met, and both appeared somewhat stunned.

Li Fan was stunned because he had originally expected the Law Transmitter to return.

He never expected that the figure appearing in this lifetime...

Was the Heavenly Doctor.

And the Heavenly Doctor was stunned as to why Li Fan, the nominal last inheritor of the Heavenly Law Realm, would appear here.

And furthermore, he was mercilessly extracting the essence of the Xuanhuang Realm's heaven and earth.

"He returned quite quickly." Li Fan sighed inwardly.

"Return to Truth."

Without any hesitation, Li Fan silently chanted in his heart.

Influenced by the power of the Immortal Ruins, Li Fan's senses indicated that the restraint of the True Immortal Net on him had loosened.

The Heavenly Doctor had also discovered him.

So, he stopped being greedy and directly activated Return to Truth.

The surrounding scene instantly became illusory.

At this very moment, Li Fan clearly saw the shock on the Heavenly Doctor's face, and the sudden burst of light from his cloudy eyes.

"What did he discover?" Li Fan's heart tightened abruptly.

But the surrounding scenery had almost come to a standstill.

Even for the powerful Heavenly Doctor, his movements appeared incredibly slow in Li Fan's eyes.

A thick mist enveloped all scenes, as if everything in the world was about to transform from reality to illusion, and substance to void.

At this moment...

From those myriad black dots in the Xuanhuang Realm, brilliant light suddenly erupted.

The power of the Immortal Ruins, capable of easily tearing apart the Xuanhuang Realm, was actually suppressed at this moment.

Among all the frozen scenes, only this radiance was least affected.

Even in Li Fan's eyes, it was still in slow motion.

But it was still rushing towards Li Fan at an incredibly fast speed.

"Faceless True Immortal!"

Li Fan's heart felt as if it were being squeezed by a hand.

The threat of the Heavenly Doctor was instantly cast aside.

"He finally found me..."

"Myriad Spirits of Heaven and Earth, Refining Gods of All Beings!"

A blood-colored giant net unfurled around Li Fan.

Layer upon layer, densely packed.

It was clearly made of countless ferocious human faces.

The red giant net emanated from Li Fan, expanding wildly outwards.

The beings within the net, trillions upon trillions, simultaneously let out their dying screams.

The brilliant light ignored the red giant net and firmly moved towards Li Fan.

Li Fan had never felt that the activation of Return to Truth was so slow.

As the brilliant white light was about to reach him, his body instinctively became stiff and cold.

Even his thoughts began to freeze.

Fortunately...

The red giant net, after all, provided a slight obstruction.

Just as the brilliant light locked onto Li Fan, Li Fan successfully activated Return to Truth.

All scenes became illusory.

Only that trace of brilliant white light remained dazzling.

...

Anchor: 1 year.

Desolate Mountain Peak.

Li Fan, having narrowly escaped death, was soaked in sweat, panting heavily.

"Is this the might of a True Immortal?"

"The will of trillions of beings is so powerless before him."

As Li Fan was thinking this, he suddenly felt something unusual about his body.

He was not seeing with his eyes at this moment, because...

Li Fan reached out to touch his face, and his body trembled slightly.

His face had disappeared.

Chapter 1127: Immortal Power Turns to Nothingness

[This simulation has ended]

[You can choose one of the following options to retain:

1. One item held by yourself in this simulation.

2. Your cultivation realm in this simulation.

3. The simulated memories of a person closely related to you in this simulation. This memory can be inherited by that person.

4. Forgo the above options and accelerate the charging progress.]

...

The prompt from Return to Truth appeared "before" Li Fan's eyes, but he was in no mood to make a choice.

Instead, he focused on the changes happening to his body.

Just like when he encountered the power of the Immortal Ruins before, even after returning through Return to Truth, he still felt an intense hunger. This time, after being forced to return through Return to Truth under the dazzling Immortal power of the Faceless True Immortal, Li Fan had not completely escaped the corrosion of True Immortal power with just one activation of Return to Truth.

"The side effect brought by the Immortal Ruins Immortals was an insatiable hunger for everything around. As for the Faceless True Immortal..."

Li Fan carefully felt his face.

It was as if a layer of skin had been draped over it, obscuring all his features.

Only the sense of touch remained.

Although he had divine sense to assist in perception, which did not affect his normal actions and life, it still sent a slight chill through Li Fan's heart.

"Not only has my face disappeared, but..."

Li Fan "looked" at his body with his divine sense.

It actually exhibited a faint transparency from time to time, like a ghost.

"My [existence] is also gradually disappearing."

He had just returned to the Anchor point of 1 year, and Return to Truth was still charging. If he died now, he would truly be dead, with no chance to try again.

Facing such a desperate situation, Li Fan did not panic.

Instead, he calmly and rapidly pondered.

From his past experiences of weakening the influence of the Immortal Ruins power through multiple activations of Return to Truth, Li Fan understood that the influence the Faceless True Immortal had imposed on him this time could likely also be resolved through repeated activations of Return to Truth.

This did not mean that Return to Truth's ability was beginning to falter when facing True Immortals, but rather that Li Fan himself was too weak.

However, there were several key issues before Li Fan now.

"First, Return to Truth needs to charge. And before that, if I don't do anything, I'm afraid I won't last that long."

"Second, under the influence of the Faceless True Immortal's dazzling Immortal power, I have become like this. Compared to when I was the True Immortal's envoy in the previous lifetime, His influence on me now is even deeper. This means..."

"From the beginning of this lifetime, I have already fallen into the True Immortal Net. Based on my last experience, even if I incite the myriad changes of Xuanhuang, it might not attract the attention of the Faceless True Immortal. But once I activate Return to Truth, it will inevitably attract Him."

...

Li Fan walked out of the wooden house on the mountain peak and arrived outside the boundless sea of clouds.

He looked at the rising sun on the horizon. Although the sunlight shone down, Li Fan felt no warmth at all.

Instead, a hint of coolness uncontrollably welled up in his heart.

Li Fan sat calmly on the edge of the cliff, deep in thought.

At the same time, he seemed to be waiting for something.

Until the sun reached its zenith, after a full half-day had passed, the Desolate Mountain of Great Xuan remained peaceful. Nothing unexpected happened.

Only then did Li Fan heave a sigh of relief, a feeling of having narrowly escaped death washing over him.

"The Faceless True Immortal did not come."

He stood up, dusted off his clothes, and felt his increasingly ethereal body. Li Fan looked at the Return to Truth prompt still flashing "before his eyes."

He still did not make any choice, temporarily ignoring it.

Returning to the wooden house on the mountain peak, Li Fan lay on the bed and pondered.

"What is the essence of Return to Truth?"

"When truth becomes falsehood, and falsehood becomes truth."

"For me, a bug that suddenly appeared in the True Immortal Net without any warning, the Faceless True Immortal chose to ignore it. Either it means He cannot perceive the specific situation in the small worlds of the Xuanhuang Realm. Or..."

"Before this, the world did not exist. The moment I returned, time began to flow, and everything truly gained meaning. From my perspective, it was due to the karmic causality of the previous lifetime that I suddenly appeared in the True Immortal Net. But from the Faceless True Immortal's perspective, I have always existed on the True Immortal Net. So, there is nothing unusual about it. This is also why He did not descend."

Numerous thoughts churned in Li Fan's mind.

"If this is time reversal, then the Faceless True Immortal at this current point in time should be able to keenly perceive the changes happening to himself. For a True Immortal, experiencing something beyond his control, He would surely not let such a anomaly pass but would follow the causal chain and come looking for me."

"But none of this has happened."

Li Fan repeated the seven words that accompanied the appearance of [Return to Truth] in his mind.

"When truth becomes falsehood, and falsehood becomes truth."

"Transforming emptiness into substance, and reconstructing all things. Possessing such a divine object, yet finding myself in such a desperate predicament, truly makes no sense." Li Fan shook his head and ridiculed himself.

Ultimately, he had still underestimated the power of a True Immortal.

He had not expected that even with the activation of Return to Truth, that dazzling Immortal power could still trace back to its source.

Moreover, it seemed the more powerful the existence, the more sensitive it was to the power of [Return to Truth].

The sudden explosive action of the Faceless True Immortal, suppressing the power of the Immortal Ruins and rushing towards him, clearly indicated that He knew something about Return to Truth.

"The performance of Return to Truth is directly related to my strength. Before I advance to the Longevity realm, I should avoid provoking them."

Li Fan thought so.

After making estimations and summaries regarding True Immortals and Return to Truth, Li Fan finally began to consider how to resolve the current predicament.

"I am currently at the third anchor point. [Return to Truth] is a Foundation Establishment wondrous item with a late-stage Foundation Establishment cultivation. If I choose to inherit my cultivation from the previous lifetime, I will instantly complete the transformation from the Foundation Establishment stage to the Nascent Soul stage."

"But I am currently within the True Immortal Net. Currently, I have not attracted the attention of the Faceless True Immortal because my own strength is negligible. However, if a Foundation Establishment ant instantly becomes a Nascent Soul ant, it might attract His attention..."

"Therefore, the method to resolve the crisis in this lifetime is clear: Hide in the Netherworld, and upon activating Return to Truth to inherit the cultivation from the previous lifetime, activate Return to Truth again to prevent further contamination by the Faceless True Immortal, and use Return to Truth to cleanse the imprint He left on me. Repeat this process."

"But before that..."

Li Fan reached out to pick up a teacup placed in the wooden house.

Initially, there was no problem. But as his body became somewhat transparent, the teacup actually slipped from his hand and fell to the ground.

"Is this the power of the Faceless True Immortal? Existence being stripped away..."

The first thing Li Fan needed to solve was finding a way to stabilize his own existence before Return to Truth finished charging.

Otherwise, all efforts would be in vain.

And judging by his current physical condition, Li Fan did not have much time left.

Chapter 1128: Heavenly Emperor Qi as Anchor

Fortunately, Li Fan was no longer the Grand Tutor who had just entered the cultivation world back then.

Having gone through multiple reincarnations, he had mastered too many secrets of the cultivation world.

Scenes from the past flashed rapidly in his mind, and he quickly found a feasible solution.

"To minimize the possibility of the Faceless True Immortal noticing, my own realm should ideally not change drastically. But I need to increase my strength as much as possible, that is, my [existence] in this world..."

"Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex."

A secret manual that did not belong to the Xuanhuang Realm instantly appeared in Li Fan's sea of consciousness.

This was a peerless divine technique that Senior Stone Slab had fished out from the Fishing Pond.

Senior Stone Slab was not interested in it and had casually given it to Li Fan at the time.

Now, it had become the most suitable life-saving straw for Li Fan.

The Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex allowed one to achieve the status of an Earthly Emperor and condense the destiny and luck of all beings and dynasties. One could become a powerhouse comparable to the Longevity realm without cultivation.

Although achieving the highest realm of the Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex required hundreds of years and the relentless efforts of multiple generations, Li Fan did not expect to reach the highest realm.

He only needed to condense the destiny and luck of all beings to help him overcome the current predicament.

"There's no time to delay. Late-stage Foundation Establishment cultivation is enough to pacify the world."

Li Fan stood on the Desolate Mountain Peak, gazing at Xuanjing City.

His figure floated gracefully as he executed the Extreme Escape technique and flew away.

...

Three days later, a piece of news spread like wildfire throughout the land.

The Emperor of Great Xuan was tyrannical and corrupt, incurring the wrath of heaven and earth.

Fortunately, a destined Holy Emperor descended, slew the corrupt ruler and treacherous officials, reopened a golden age, and created a new universe.

The stories were told with great embellishment, but the officials and commoners of Great Xuan knew at a glance that a regime change had occurred.

Although it was indeed a shocking event, after a few days of chaos, everyone quickly calmed down.

After all, imperial power had never truly reached the villages since ancient times. No matter who was in charge above, the real power was still held by those people.

The commoners of Great Xuan initially thought this.

However, it wasn't long before the extraordinary nature of this destined Holy Emperor began to manifest.

Overnight, tall platforms sprang up all over Great Xuan.

No one knew how these hundred-zhang-tall structures were born, but these existences called [Holy Emperor's Seat] completely changed the official hierarchy ecology of the Great Xuan Empire.

Because these Holy Emperor's Seats could project the image of the destined Holy Emperor onto the heavens.

Every commoner, even those living in remote mountain villages, could listen to the Holy Emperor's teachings through these Holy Emperor's Seats scattered throughout the empire.

What further alarmed officials in various regions was that these Holy Emperor's Seats also had the function of connecting to the capital.

In Qingzhou, there was a drought that lasted for three months, resulting in no harvest and widespread famine.

However, shortly after the construction of the Holy Emperor's Seat, a team of Imperial Guards emerged from it, bringing a large amount of grain for disaster relief.

While saving countless commoners, this event was instantly broadcast throughout the land through the Holy Emperor's Seat.

Subsequently, Holy Emperor's envoys continued to emerge from the Holy Emperor's Seats, summoning officials from various regions, which also confirmed the authenticity of the disaster relief.

And the deeds of the destined Holy Emperor, a reincarnated immortal, displaying various divine abilities in the imperial court, quickly became known to all.

"All the people in various regions can pray to the great destined Holy Emperor through the Holy Emperor's Seat. Any incompetent or corrupt officials in their jurisdiction will be severely punished once confirmed." This was the teaching of the Holy Emperor's envoys to the people of Great Xuan.

"Don't think you can simply die to escape punishment. The methods of the destined Holy Emperor are beyond your imagination. The seventy or so fat pigs tied up in the execution ground of Xuanjing City are officials who previously preyed on the people. They are now writing confessions on the ground with their pig trotters every day. I have come to show you all." This was a warning from the Holy Emperor's envoys to the officials of Great Xuan.

And after the officials of Great Xuan collectively visited the execution ground in the capital, they all turned deathly pale. Upon returning to their respective regions, they all became upright and diligent in a short period.

Xuanjing City.

Li Fan floated above the capital, watching the imperial destiny of the Great Xuan Dynasty transform from black to green, nodding slightly.

"By leveraging the Holy Emperor's Seat to achieve strong centralized power, the Great Xuan Dynasty has transformed in a short period. Next, we will slowly consolidate the hearts of the people and elevate the imperial destiny."

Li Fan observed his own body.

The hundreds of millions of beings in Great Xuan were now tied to him.

It was equivalent to a substantial "anchor," fixing his existence.

His body was no longer ethereal and transparent like a ghost.

However, he still experienced moments of voidness from time to time.

Clearly, he had not yet completely stabilized.

"It's not a big problem. As long as Great Xuan remains stable and becomes increasingly prosperous, in another three years, I should be able to completely shake off the side effects of [Voidness]."

"But this only resolves the side effects. To truly break free from the True Immortal Net, I still need to go to the Netherworld to perform Return to Truth."

Li Fan waved his hand slightly forward.

Without mobilizing his late-stage Foundation Establishment spiritual energy, he used only the destiny of the dynasty condensed by the Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex.

A whistling sound tore through the air, and the white clouds in the distance were split apart.

A phantom image of a green dragon faintly appeared in the sky, roaring upwards.

"White, green, red, purple, gold."

"In just one month, I have mastered the second level of the five realms of the Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex."

"Currently equivalent to a late-stage Golden Core cultivator. Such rapid cultivation is first because Great Xuan already had a decent foundation, barely considered to be in a flourishing golden age. Second..."

Li Fan looked at the towering Holy Emperor's Seat below.

"The methods of immortals are a dimensionality reduction attack for mortal dynasties. Punishing corrupt officials severely and resolving local disasters, then announcing it to the world through the Holy Emperor's Seat, has almost instantly condensed the hearts of the people."

"If it were an ordinary mortal emperor of a feudal dynasty, it would take at least a decade to achieve what I have, and they would still have to face the backlash from officials and local powers."

"I do not need to worry about these things."

Thinking this, Li Fan slowly descended from the clouds and landed inside the palace.

"Greetings, Holy Emperor!"

"Greetings, Teacher!"

The guards in the courtyard immediately knelt.

"Rise." Li Fan raised his hand, helping them all up.

The faces of these young people instantly flushed red with excitement.

They were all personally selected by Li Fan from various parts of Great Xuan. Besides undertaking guard duties in the imperial palace, their main task was to eliminate corrupt officials everywhere and deter petty criminals, maintaining the prosperity and invincibility of the Great Xuan Dynasty's destiny.

Among them, the ones who called Li Fan 'Teacher' were two exceptionally talented youths from below Desolate Mountain, named Sun Erlang and Wang Xuanba.

They bore even more important missions.

"Erlang, how is your cultivation of the [Immortal Sitting Technique] I taught you?"

After dismissing the others, Li Fan looked at Sun Erlang and asked in a deep voice.

Chapter 1129: The Meaning of the Anchor Point

Wearing black robes embroidered with nine intertwined golden dragons.

The beaded crown hung down, obscuring his face, making it impossible to see.

"As expected of the destined Holy Emperor, mortals cannot hope to behold the Dragon Countenance."

Sun Erlang felt Li Fan's gaze, his body trembled slightly, and he instinctively lowered his head.

At the same time, he spoke with difficulty, "Reporting to Teacher, your disciple is incompetent. Yesterday, I just broke through to the first level of Qi Refining."

"It is not easy to achieve Qi Transformation within such a short period, relying solely on the spiritual energy gathered within the imperial palace," Li Fan did not chide him but nodded and comforted him.

Upon hearing this, Sun Erlang's face showed even more guilt. "If not for the [Great Xuan Immortal Heart Incantation] that Teacher taught me, I am afraid I would still be affected by the miasma within my body and unable to embark on the path of immortality."

After speaking, Sun Erlang kowtowed several times filled with gratitude.

Li Fan did not stop him.

When Sun Erlang stood up again, he asked indifferently, "What is the overall progress of the Imperial Guards learning the Immortal Heart Incantation?"

"As of yesterday, one hundred and sixty soldiers successfully entered the initial stage and shed their mortal bodies. The rest who failed the test have all been dealt with cleanly," a hint of reluctance flashed in Sun Erlang's eyes, but he quickly concealed it.

"You will all be the main force for the conquest of the myriad realms in the future. You must cultivate diligently day and night and not slack off."

"As for the spiritual energy problem, you need not worry. In three days, you will personally pilot this immortal boat and head to the Eastern Abyss."

Li Fan casually flicked his finger, and a ten-zhang-long wooden boat appeared before Sun Erlang.

Silver lines were engraved all over the wooden boat, emitting an aura of profound mystery.

"This is truly an immortal treasure. How can Master entrust such a treasure to me so casually?" Sun Erlang's heart tensed, and he quickly nodded in agreement.

The immortal boat then flew into his embrace.

A feeling of commanding it as if it were an extension of his own arm instantly surfaced in Sun Erlang's mind.

"You may go." Just as he was experiencing the wonders of the immortal boat, Li Fan's voice sounded at the right moment.

Sun Erlang bowed and took his leave.

The entire imperial palace garden was suddenly left with only Li Fan.

His face, hidden in the shadows beneath the beaded crown, appeared strange and sinister.

"Heh heh, if it weren't for the fact that this lifetime is destined to be short, and I was trying out the method of passing down techniques to others, I might have taken a long time to discover that the [Great Xuan Immortal Heart Incantation] is not restricted by the taboo of not being able to cultivate multiple techniques."

"Is it that the Immortal Heart Incantation does not fall under the category of cultivation techniques, or is it a special favor from the Great Xuan Heavenly Dao for the Great Heavenly Venerate of Xuan Tian?"

"Regardless, the plan to select a suitable successor for the Great Heavenly Venerate of Xuan Tian in the future will be much easier than I imagined."

Li Fan's thoughts turned slowly. With a flash, he appeared on the [Holy Emperor's Seat] standing in Xuanjing City.

Traces of thin spiritual energy nourished Li Fan's body.

This allowed his current late-stage Foundation Establishment realm to not regress due to lack of spiritual energy.

Having reincarnated over a hundred times, and reaching the Nascent Soul realm at his peak, capable of rivaling Combined Dao cultivators, Li Fan, despite having returned to the Foundation Establishment realm, saw the world differently than before.

For example: mortal small worlds like Great Xuan were not entirely devoid of spiritual energy, as they were still connected to the Xuanhuang Realm.

However, due to the special structure of the small world itself, coupled with the blockade of the Immortal Severing Grand Formation, spiritual energy was extremely scarce, almost nonexistent.

Ordinary cultivators could not utilize it, and only long-lived animals could accumulate it bit by bit over time, acquiring limited amounts of spiritual energy.

Like the giant snake hundreds of feet long on Desolate Mountain.

"Even draining all the spiritual energy of an entire world can only sustain a Foundation Establishment cultivator's survival..."

"However, it's fine to borrow from the Xuanhuang Realm."

Li Fan added some new formations to the Taiyan Boat he gave Sun Erlang. Its purpose was to automatically fly to the Xuanhuang Realm, absorb spiritual energy, store it, and then return.

Sun Erlang, inside the Taiyan Boat, naturally could not see things outside the flying boat. All he needed to do was bring the flying boat near the Abyss.

Although with Li Fan's current level of formation attainment, his actions of stealing spiritual energy from the Xuanhuang Realm would be difficult for others to discover under the concealment of the formations, it was still not a long-term solution.

To create spiritual energy from nothing, he still needed the Dao Yi Insect.

The Dao Yi Insect was a peculiar exotic beast, and Li Fan could not create it himself. However...

Skipping the prompt for inheriting the previous lifetime's cultivation from Return to Truth, Li Fan looked at his panel.

Name: Li Fan

Realm: Late-stage Foundation Establishment

Physiological Age: 20/399

Psychological Age: 1399/9999

Void Transformation Charging Progress: 3%

Anchor Charging Progress: 0%

Current Anchor Count: 3

Current Usable Anchor Count: 1

Bound Items: Origin of the Sky Profound Mirror (Fragment), Taiyan Boat, Ten Thousand Beast Crystallization, Ten Thousand Men's Blood Essence, Dao Dissolution Stone, Ultimate Dissolution Disk

...

"Physiological age has returned to the 399 years expected of a Foundation Establishment realm, but there's no need to worry. Before my lifespan runs out, I should have already performed Return to Truth."

"The upper limit of psychological age, even after reaching the Nascent Soul stage, has not increased accordingly, so it seems there's a bottleneck..."

Li Fan glanced at these points and then moved on.

He focused his attention on the anchor count and bound items.

The original usable anchor count was 2. After absorbing the nascent Five Elements Grotto-Heaven, it became 3.

As for now, only one remains.

This was because Li Fan had used a blank anchor to replace a bound item.

"Thousand Mechanisms Jade Halo Golden Chapter" had become the Origin of the Sky Profound Mirror.

The Unstable Stone Tablet (Damaged) had become the Ten Thousand Beast Crystallization.

Anchors were hard-won, but after absorbing the nascent Five Elements Grotto-Heaven and generating anchors, Li Fan gained new insights into the essence of anchors.

Heavenly and earthly wonders, Golden Core laws, and Nascent Soul Grotto-Heavens.

The reason Return to Truth needed to absorb these items as anchors was likely because Return to Truth was supplementing its knowledge of [external objects].

Just as the Heavenly Profound Mirror sublimated itself by measuring heaven and earth, Return to Truth simply and crudely absorbed experience through devouring.

"So it's the opposite of what I thought."

"The closer to the essence of the world something is, the more charging progress it provides. Foundation Establishment wondrous items and Law Golden Cores are too superficial and cannot satisfy Return to Truth's needs."

"Therefore, the number of anchors generated is limited."

"On the other hand, Nascent Soul Grotto-Heavens, the birth mutations, and even the Soul of Heaven and Earth will provide a large amount of charging progress."

"With the Xuanhuang Realm as a massive source of nourishment, the anchor count is not a particular concern for now."

Therefore, Li Fan did not hesitate to use the anchor replacement function.

The Origin of the Sky Profound Mirror was obtained by chance in the previous lifetime.

As for the Ten Thousand Beast Crystallization...

In the previous lifetime, before finally launching the world-destroying plan, Li Fan had traveled to various small worlds to conduct a final inventory.

The Myriad Beast Samsara was a harvest from the Empire and from Xu Ke.

Li Fan's thoughts drifted back to that time.

"Myriad Immortals Alliance's surprise attack? The United Front headquarters wiped out?" Xiao Qing's face turned deathly pale upon hearing Li Fan's words.

"If I hadn't severed the connection between the Spirit Wood Realm and you in time, the Empire would likely have turned into ruins by now," Li Fan sighed faintly.

The Empress and Xiao Hong exchanged glances, their hearts filled with lingering fear.

"However, you don't need to worry too much. Although the Spirit Wood Realm was destroyed, the vast majority of the headquarters' members managed to escape safely and have temporarily gone into hiding. Once the storm passes, the United Front can rise again in an instant," Li Fan lied with a straight face.

Upon hearing this blatant lie, the people of the Empire and others felt reassured.
