While listening to the reports from the Empire and others about current events, Li Fan entered the Empire's treasury.

Chapter 1130: Inferior Version of the Sky Patrol Arrow

All the research results of the Empire were backed up here.

Li Fan strolled through the vast treasury, and only when he reached the location of the Myriad Beast Furnace at the end did he turn around.

He took out an item and showed it to the two of them.

It was only a palm-sized disk, but the pressure it inadvertently emitted made Xiao Qing and Xiao Hong tremble, and they felt an irresistible urge to kneel.

"This is?"

They forced themselves to resist their bodies' instincts and looked at the disk in Li Fan's hand, their faces filled with horror: "Myriad Beast Samsara?"

With their life and death in his hands, this feeling instantly reminded them of this legendary treasure of the beast race.

However, after staring intently at the disk for a long time, they still found something amiss.

As members of the beast race, their bloodline memories contained ancestral memories of the Myriad Beast Samsara.

But it was clearly different from the item Li Fan held.

The true Myriad Beast Samsara exuded a more ancient and primordial aura.

As for this one before them...

It did have a certain control effect on them.

But even if they fought with all their might, they might not be able to break free. It was still quite different from the legends of life and death being beyond one's control.

"A replica?"

The thought simultaneously arose in Qing and Hong's minds as they looked at Li Fan, their faces filled with shock.

"You guessed correctly. It is indeed a replica created by the elders of the United Front based on the research materials of the Myriad Beast Samsara you provided earlier."

"Besides being able to control myriad beasts, it has another function, which is the main purpose of my visit here."

Li Fan suddenly sighed, "The Spirit Wood Realm was destroyed. Although the personnel losses were not significant, we escaped in such a hurry that many precious materials and research data could not be brought out."

"Therefore, after painful reflection, the elders decided to activate the backup plan for the myriad realms, replicating and preserving all valuable items from each small world..."

Before Li Fan finished speaking, Xiao Qing and Xiao Hong's expressions changed.

Then Li Fan continued, "This is also for your own good. After all, your Empire's self-defense capabilities are too weak. The Myriad Immortals Alliance only needs to dispatch one or two Combined Dao cultivators to completely destroy you."

"It is best to leave a seed of civilization in the United Front. Even if something unexpected happens, you can rebuild quickly."

Li Fan fiddled with the disk in his hand and looked at the countless frozen exotic beast specimens in the Empire's treasury. "Your greatest wealth is actually the various exotic beasts you have cultivated over the years. I know you all have more than one backup. I will only take one of them."

With that, he ignored Xiao Qing and Xiao Hong's reactions. A beam of light shone from the disk, sweeping across these frozen exotic beasts.

All those that were illuminated instantly vanished on the spot.

And in Li Fan's disk, phantom images of those exotic beasts seemed to faintly appear.

It looked as if these frozen exotic beasts were being stored within, but in reality, they had already been decomposed by the disk's beam of light. Simultaneously, the information regarding the structure, bloodline, and tissues of these exotic beasts was all recorded into the disk.

"All beasts under heaven originate from [Di Yi]."

"And the exotic beasts of this Empire are all evolved from the beasts of the past. As the saying goes, all changes stem from the same origin. As long as this information is mastered, all exotic beasts can be 'created out of thin air'."

As more information about exotic beasts was collected, the phantom images on the disk became more numerous.

Not only did the aura it exuded become more majestic and powerful, but even the appearance of the disk itself changed.

It became increasingly similar to the true Myriad Beast Samsara in the bloodline memories of Xiao Qing and Xiao Hong.

And while Li Fan was collecting backup information on exotic beasts, he couldn't help but marvel at the wonders of creation.

Besides some exotic beasts that were specifically cultivated and bred, the birth of most exotic beasts in the Empire was basically due to various coincidences.

Different bloodlines intertwined and mutated, and new species mutated into different offspring.

It seemed endless.

"Infinite possibilities." The phrase spoken by the Di Yi beast in the Immortal Subjugation Illusionary Realm suddenly reappeared in Li Fan's mind.

As Li Fan was about to absorb the information of a frozen exotic beast as usual, he suddenly stopped.

Because he felt a familiar aura from this exotic beast.

"Sky Patrol Arrow..."

Xiao Qing and Xiao Hong saw Li Fan's movement pause and his gaze fall upon a certain spot, and they immediately understood.

They quickly explained, "This exotic beast is the core of the arrow that the superior envoy instructed us to research, and we named it [Sky Splitter]. Back then, in the Beast Taming Sect, we had seen similar demonic beasts, but they were far less ferocious and swift than the current ones. Moreover, they had strong self-awareness and were difficult to control."

"The offspring cultivated so far are still far from the main body that the superior envoy gave us, so we have not reported it yet."

After a search, Li Fan indeed found similar species around the Sky Splitter exotic beast.

"If the core is insufficient, I can compensate with formations. Even if it doesn't match the destructive power of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's true Sky Patrol Arrows, half of it would be very practical." Thinking this, Li Fan absorbed the information of these Sky Splitter exotic beasts into the disk.

...

His thoughts returned to the present.

The disk, which carried the essence of the Empire's research, was naturally the [Ten Thousand Beast Crystallization].

With the artifact refining level of the Heavenly Mystery Realm combined with the detailed and specific information about the Myriad Beast Samsara obtained from Xu Ke, creating a replica was not a difficult task.

"Condensing physical exotic beasts from the Ten Thousand Beast Crystallization requires a massive amount of spiritual energy. My current late-stage Foundation Establishment cultivation cannot support it. However, once Sun Erlang pilots the Taiyan Boat back from the Xuanhuang Realm, it will be fine."

"With the Dao Yi Insect and Sky Splitter, Great Xuan will possess the capital to conquer other small worlds."

To go to the Netherworld, the Nether race would need to perform a special ritual.

Although Li Fan easily subdued the Nether race in the previous lifetime, it was because he possessed the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, and his true combat power was above that of ordinary Combined Dao cultivators.

In this lifetime, Li Fan, who was already within the True Immortal Net, could not easily increase his realm.

Relying solely on the Great Xuan Realm, the Nether race was not easy to deal with.

Therefore, it was necessary to improve the combat power of Great Xuan's army and civilians as much as possible, and also to improve Li Fan's own [Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex] level.

Li Fan stood on the [Holy Emperor's Seat] and began to consider suitable targets for conquest.

A month later, Sun Erlang successfully returned piloting the Taiyan Boat.

The first step in the sublimation of Great Xuan into a spiritual energy world began.

As the first Heaven and Earth Furnace was successfully forged, spiritual energy began to diffuse within the Xuanjing City area.

The Great Xuan Imperial Guards were the first to sense the presence of spiritual energy.

Overnight, the hundred Imperial Guards who possessed the [Great Xuan Immortal Heart Incantation] all successfully introduced Qi into their bodies, thus embarking on the path of cultivation.

And among them, Sun Erlang, as the leader, advanced directly to the Great Perfection of Qi Refining, thanks to the power of the [Immortal Sitting Technique].

Chapter 1131: Great Xuan Conquers Myriad Realms

If it weren't for the requirement of a heavenly terrestrial treasure to advance further, Sun Erlang would have directly leaped to the mid-stage Foundation Establishment.

Sun Erlang was also steady in his temperament. He did not show excessive joy but actively reported the matter to Li Fan.

"The Great Xuan Imperial Guards, and in the future, the army and civilians who conquer the myriad realms, will all become your assistance in cultivating the [Immortal Sitting Technique]."

"Within five years, I need you to help me forge an army that is capable of fighting and conquering."

Li Fan sat suspended above the [Holy Emperor's Seat], looking at Sun Erlang kneeling below, and said indifferently.

"As for the necessary items for your advancement, you need not worry."

Sun Erlang was filled with emotion, his blood boiling, and he retreated in response.

He went to train his subordinates and the Imperial Guards.

Meanwhile, Li Fan took out a Heavenly Profound Mirror and probed it with his divine sense.

This Heavenly Profound Mirror was an unexpected harvest from the Taiyan Boat's trip to the Xuanhuang Realm.

As the Taiyan Boat was absorbing spiritual energy from the Xuanhuang Realm, a Golden Core cultivator happened to pass by.

Whether by coincidence or because this cultivator had extraordinary talent, he was able to vaguely sense the anomaly of the Taiyan Boat under the concealment of the formation.

This person thought he had discovered some hidden treasure and excitedly explored it.

As a result, he triggered the Taiyan Boat's defensive formation, was unfortunately taken into the boat, and suppressed.

Li Fan currently imprisoned him in the Great Xuan dungeon, letting him simmer for the time being.

"It's a pity that it's just an ordinary Heavenly Profound Mirror and doesn't have a direct item transmission function."

Even though he had not yet joined the Myriad Immortals Alliance in this lifetime, and even though this Heavenly Profound Mirror did not belong to him, Li Fan could still access the Heavenly Profound Mirror unimpeded.

This was precisely because of the Origin of the Sky Profound Mirror.

In the previous lifetime, upon initiating the world-destroying plan, Li Fan had used a blank anchor to exchange the [Thousand Mechanisms Jade Halo Golden Chapter] for the Origin of the Sky Profound Mirror.

On the Return to Truth panel, it became [Origin of the Sky Profound Mirror (Fragment)].

The Heavenly Profound Mirror did not seem to notice this mysterious origin that had appeared in the world.

And in this lifetime, as the true owner of this origin, when Li Fan entered the Heavenly Profound Mirror again, he felt things were different from the previous lifetime.

In the previous lifetime, the Origin of the Sky Profound Mirror was given by the human avatar of the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Although it indeed possessed all sorts of permissions specific to the Heavenly Profound Mirror, its fundamental source of authority belonged to the Heavenly Profound Mirror itself.

If the Heavenly Profound Mirror wished, it could recall the gifted origin at any time and invalidate the permissions.

But in this lifetime...

Li Fan roamed through the countless pieces of information in the Heavenly Profound Mirror and felt true [freedom].

He possessed completely independent authority.

He could even do things that the Heavenly Profound Mirror itself could not.

For example, deleting certain transaction data.

Perhaps influenced by Xuan Tian Wang's past refinement, the Heavenly Profound Mirror could not perform actions like forgery or deception.

And to maintain the stable operation of the Immortal Alliance, all data in the Heavenly Profound Mirror was unalterable and traceable.

Mo Ru Bin's actions in the previous lifetime, using the Heavenly Profound Mirror to deduce Xuan Tian Wang's whereabouts, were eventually discovered by the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

This was not a betrayal by the Heavenly Profound Mirror, but rather its inherent characteristic.

But now, empowered by this newly appeared origin force, Li Fan could achieve this.

He erased the information of the original owner of this Heavenly Profound Mirror, and then registered a completely new blank identity for himself.

By selling crucial information, he earned tens of thousands of contribution points in a short period.

Then, using this as seed capital, and engaging in high-frequency transactions, within half a month, the contribution points in Li Fan's account had ballooned to hundreds of thousands.

He purchased the necessary resources in large quantities.

The agreed-upon trading location was set in the sea area near the Great Xuan exit.

Li Fan remotely controlled the Taiyan Boat to retrieve the items.

...

Although it seemed troublesome, Li Fan operated with ease and grace.

All the resources required for the Great Xuan Imperial Guards' advancement were purchased.

Without the constraint of heavenly terrestrial artifacts, the strength of the Great Xuan Imperial Guards ushered in its first surge.

Foundation Establishment cultivators appeared one after another, and Sun Erlang, as the leader among them, advanced to the Great Perfection of Foundation Establishment in a short period.

He was even slightly stronger than Li Fan currently was.

However, with the blessing of Great Xuan's imperial destiny, if they were to truly fight Li Fan, he would not be able to withstand even one move.

Sun Erlang's realm advanced too quickly. Li Fan ordered him to suppress his strength for the time being.

And he taught him the [Calamity Body Method] from the Supreme Sect, storing all the excess feedback cultivation.

Anchor Point 3 years. The Great Xuan Imperial Guards had fifty-six Foundation Establishment cultivators and eight hundred and forty-two Qi Refining cultivators.

On this day, Li Fan preached in Xuanjing City.

His image was transmitted throughout the land via the Holy Emperor's Seat.

As Li Fan's words, seemingly containing infinite Great Dao, resonated, various strange phenomena appeared in the Great Xuan sky.

Flowers rained down from the sky, accompanied by countless golden dragons flying.

The Heavenly and Earth Furnaces, which had been sealed by Li Fan with formations earlier, began to radiate the spiritual energy they had generated over the past three years.

Even mortals could feel the wonderful changes happening in the world at this moment.

Not to mention the cultivators in Xuanjing.

Among the fifty-six Foundation Establishment cultivators, three directly had epiphanies and advanced to the Golden Core realm.

Sun Erlang was naturally among them.

However, it was merely a simple advancement in realm.

In terms of actual combat effectiveness, he was still far inferior to ordinary Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators.

But for Li Fan, it was enough.

Li Fan did not expect them to fight enemies directly; they only needed to function as spiritual energy refiners for the operation of the formations.

He taught the formation to Sun Erlang and ordered the Great Xuan Imperial Guards to practice diligently day and night, ensuring seamless cooperation.

Great Xuan's strength increased day by day.

Anchor Point 5 years. Great Xuan, having accumulated strength for a long time, finally launched its first offensive battle.

The target was the Spirit Wood Realm, which Li Fan was very familiar with.

Due to the absence of Combined Dao cultivators, direct connection of the Spirit Wood Realm's entrance to Great Xuan was impossible.

Therefore, the route for this conquest was to pass through Xuanhuang and then attack the Spirit Wood Realm.

To prevent detection by the Myriad Immortals Alliance, the expeditionary force consisted of only fifty cultivators led by Sun Erlang.

Riding the Taiyan Boat, they silently entered the Spirit Wood Realm.

Upon seeing the sky-high giant tree in the middle of the world, all the Great Xuan Imperial Guards couldn't help but be slightly dazed.

However, their years of rigorous training quickly allowed them to focus.

The formation was instantly set up, and an afterimage whistled away, heading towards the Spirit Wood.

It was none other than a Sky Patrol Arrow!

The flight of the Sky Patrol Arrow naturally angered the Treant race.

They wanted to intercept it.

But even Treant elders with Nascent Soul stage cultivation were as fragile as paper before the Sky Patrol Arrow.

Screams echoed continuously as the Treants used their lives to try and stop it, but they were unable to prevent the Sky Patrol Arrow from ultimately landing within the Spirit Wood.

Boom!

A terrifying great hole was pierced through the center of the Spirit Wood.

The constantly pulsating Heart of the Spirit Wood was faintly visible within.

Sun Erlang, clad in black and gold armor, flew forward.

Before him, as many as ninety Sky Patrol Arrows circled.

"Submit, or die."

Chapter 1132: Furnace of Fortune Transformation

Ninety Sky Patrol Arrows, only half were actual lethal objects.

As for the remaining half, they were illusions created by formations, possessing only an imposing appearance.

However, the Treants of the Spirit Wood Realm were already terrified by the destructive power displayed by the first Sky Patrol Arrow, rendering them unable to distinguish between reality and illusion.

The central giant tree was intimately connected with the Spirit Wood Realm.

When the tree flourished, the realm prospered; when the tree was destroyed, the realm perished.

With the massive hole in the trunk of the giant tree, the Treant race of the Spirit Wood Realm had no will to resist.

The female patriarch of the Treants led the entire tribe, kneeling in humiliation before the Great Xuan Imperial Guards, expressing their submission.

Then, Sun Erlang, following the instructions of the destined Holy Emperor, carved numerous formations onto the Heart of the Giant Tree.

He did not understand the meaning of these formations, but executing orders was the heavenly duty of the Great Xuan Imperial Guards.

With Sun Erlang's current Golden Core Great Perfection strength, activating the formations was still somewhat strenuous.

And he also had to guard against a counterattack from the Treant race.

Fortunately, the deterrence of the Sky Patrol Arrows was too great, and ultimately the Treant race did not dare to risk a desperate struggle.

Once the formation was completed, a brilliant green light erupted from the Heart of the Giant Tree.

The wounds of the Spirit Tree began to slowly heal, and a figure was born from the light.

"Spirit of the Giant Tree..." Sun Erlang mused thoughtfully.

Just as he had expected, the Spirit of the Giant Tree, upon appearing, did not side with the Treants.

Instead, it transmitted its voice to communicate with Sun Erlang: "Are you Senior Brother Sun? Teacher asked you to leave half of the Imperial Guards here to assist in building the formation."

"By the way, my name is Lin Ling."

Lin Ling transmitted an image. Sun Erlang heard the familiar voice of the destined Holy Emperor in the picture and nodded slightly.

Without losing a single soldier and only consuming one Sky Patrol Arrow, Sun Erlang successfully conquered the Spirit Wood Realm. However, Sun Erlang also knew that this had nothing to do with the actual combat strength of the Great Xuan Imperial Guards. It was entirely due to the terrifying, world-destroying power of the Sky Patrol Arrow.

Sun Erlang shook his head slightly, dispelling the sense of frustration in his heart. He led the remaining personnel towards the second target small world.

"Great Li? Humph..." A murderous glint flashed in Sun Erlang's eyes.

...

After the Great Xuan Imperial Guards departed, Lin Ling, following the formation taught by Li Fan, began to direct the Treant race.

Lin Ling did not have much affection for these Treants.

Instead, the one who lectured, taught, and enlightened him upon his initial awakening, Li Fan, was the person Lin Ling felt closest to in this world.

"Myriad Spirits Grand Formation?"

"Upon completion, it will open a passage to the world where Teacher resides, and it will also increase the overall spiritual energy concentration of the Spirit Wood Realm, leading to its sublimation."

"First, complete the basic formation construction. The remaining crucial materials will be delivered by the Great Xuan Imperial Guards later."

Recalling the formation instructions taught by Li Fan, and remembering Li Fan's promise that he could go to see the destined Holy Emperor once he completed the construction of the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation, Lin Ling became enthusiastic and once again urged the dull Treants.

...

In Great Xuan.

Sensing the somewhat blurry images from the Spirit Wood Realm, Li Fan nodded inwardly.

Although he intended to perform Return to Truth in the Netherworld in this lifetime, using the power of the Netherworld to reduce the Faceless True Immortal's perception.

Li Fan could not predict how much this reduction would be.

Therefore, the [Myriad Spirits of Heaven and Earth, Refining Gods of All Beings] Grand Formation was still necessary to build, in case of unforeseen accidents.

If Li Fan had felt some emotional stirrings the first time he witnessed the death of billions of beings.

Then the second time, and after the second time...

Li Fan truly felt no psychological pressure at all.

He collected his thoughts and looked at his nominal second disciple in this lifetime.

Wang Xuanba.

Unlike Sun Erlang, Li Fan did not teach him the new cultivation methods.

Instead, he taught him the [Creation Furnace Technique] he had researched.

This version had undergone a complete transformation compared to the initial version, which simply leveraged the body's hidden potential to crudely strengthen the physical body.

In the previous lifetime, after receiving guidance from the Heavenly Doctor and mastering the fusion of the "Heavenly Doctor Immortal Scripture" and the "Heaven Mending Record," Li Fan gained new insights into how to stimulate human potential.

However, turning theory into practice still required experimentation.

Wang Xuanba's special physique was the perfect experimental subject.

"The Xuanhuang heaven and earth, at the moment of imminent destruction, burst forth with myriad miraculous changes."

"Humans should also be the same."

"In a normal state, the human body is in balance. Only when invaded by foreign objects and facing a life-threatening crisis will it mobilize its own potential."

Before Li Fan, Wang Xuanba, only seventeen years old, slept with his eyes closed.

His height had already reached nearly thirty feet, his muscles bulged, and his skin was covered with a layer of golden keratin, resembling armor.

Although the human form could still be vaguely discerned, at first glance, he looked like an ancient ferocious beast.

"Eighteen types of exotic beast flesh and blood have already been implanted. Only seven of them have been fused and absorbed by him. The rest have all produced severe rejection reactions. If I hadn't intervened to save him, he would likely have died from bloodline exhaustion by now."

"However, as his physique continues to strengthen, perhaps we can try again."

Thinking this, Li Fan injected a mass of flesh and blood from the exotic beast [Heavenly Silk Fox] into Wang Xuanba's body.

Solely strengthening his power seemed to have caused his physical development to become unbalanced and on the verge of collapse. He needed to be strengthened in terms of agility.

Li Fan was very curious to see where the limit of the human body lay.

...

Boundary-Leaving Realm.

The conquest of Great Li was even easier than that of the Spirit Wood Realm.

They didn't even need to use the Sky Patrol Arrows. The Great Xuan Imperial Guards flying in the sky alone made the Emperor and the civil and military officials in the capital kneel down.

Adhering to the principle that there should only be one destined Holy Emperor, Sun Erlang ruthlessly executed the Emperor of Great Li.

He then selected King Zhennan, Xiao Tianyou, as his proxy.

As the Holy Emperor's Seats appeared throughout Great Li, people quickly accepted the fact of the sudden regime change.

And the existence of the destined Holy Emperor.

Great Li also gradually transformed into a small world infused with spiritual energy.

Anchor Point 8 years.

"85%."

"Compared to before, it has actually slowed down."

"Is it because of my current physical condition?"

Li Fan pondered as he looked at the number on the Return to Truth panel.

Over three years, as numerous small worlds such as Spirit Wood, Beast Taming, and Great Li were incorporated into Great Xuan's territory, his [Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex] successfully advanced to the third level.

Great Xuan's destiny shone like the rising sun, emitting a fiery red light and vigorous vitality.

His actual combat power was equivalent to the early-stage Nascent Soul level of the Xuanhuang Realm.

However, Li Fan already felt the bottleneck of the Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex.

To advance further to the fourth level, the Violet Qi realm.

Based on the current development speed, it would take decades to achieve.

Chapter 1133: Dark Faith Power

The dark faith

To achieve the highest realm of the Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex and become a peerless emperor comparable to a Longevity realm powerhouse, Li Fan estimated that it would at least require building a vast dynasty whose sphere of influence encompassed the entire Xuanhuang Great World.

"Hmph, if I had that kind of strength, why would I still need to cultivate the Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex?"

However, since it was merely a temporary measure to anchor himself, Li Fan did not harbor too many illusions about it.

In fact, his goal had already been achieved.

As the Great Xuan Dynasty became increasingly prosperous, the strange phenomenon of his body intermittently disappearing had almost completely ceased.

Even his face, which had originally lost all features, showed signs of reappearing.

"Faceless True Immortal, His power seems to be to sever all connections with the mortal world."

"And I, as the destined Holy Emperor of Great Xuan, with hundreds of millions of lives bound to me. To some extent, this has influenced the power of the True Immortal Net."

Li Fan carefully savored the entanglement of these two forces within himself and suddenly had a realization.

"The correct way to use the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation might not be simple obstruction."

"It's to throw that cauldron of dog blood, made from the lingering wills of billions of beings, right at them!"

"To put it simply, to forcibly associate those lingering wills with the Faceless True Immortal."

"For example, by making those who died unjustly believe that the Faceless True Immortal is the culprit."

Li Fan's thoughts raced, and after a bout of deduction with the Ultimate Dissolution Disk, he quickly made minor adjustments to the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation.

He then summoned Lin Ling.

"Master."

Soon, Lin Ling, clad in armor and looking valiant, appeared before Li Fan.

Unlike in his previous life, in this lifetime, Lin Ling had shouldered the heavy responsibility of leading the Great Xuan Imperial Guards to conquer myriad realms since awakening her consciousness.

She was constantly on the move, and especially under Li Fan'sinstruction, she had not established any connection with the Earth Vein Ancient Tree.

Her temperament had also become bold and uninhibited, like a seasoned soldier.

After Li Fan explained the subtle modification method for the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation, Lin Ling was about to leave to execute the mission when she suddenly remembered something.

"Hmm?" Li Fan looked at Lin Ling.

"Master, while I was fleeing through the Xuanhuang main world, a thought-sense discovered me and has been trying to communicate. "

"Is it the Earth Vein Ancient Tree?" Li Fan frowned slightly.

"No. But it's very similar..." Lin Ling replied truthfully.

Seeing Li Fan's expression, she quickly added, "However, I have always abided by your teachings and ignored it."

"That thought-sense is acting crazy and doesn't even say who it is. It just wants me to go see it..."

Upon hearing this, Li Fan immediately understood.

He just didn't know why the Eastern Wood would discover Lin Ling's whereabouts.

After inquiring in detail about the location of the encounter, Li Fan designed a formation for Lin Ling to shield her from external perception.

Only then did he dismiss her.

He mused that the mission for this lifetime was primarily to escape the influence of the Faceless True Immortal.

Li Fan merely noted down the time and location of the Eastern Wood's appearance, having no intention of further contact with it.

"Later, I can give the Earth Vein Ancient Tree a surprise."

Li Fan snorted coldly.

His figure flickered, and he arrived in the secret chamber beneath the Holy Emperor's Seat.

It was pitch black, and more than a dozen Netherworld race members were imprisoned there.

After Great Xuan had initially established its combat capabilities, Li Fan had ordered Sun Erlang and Wang Xuanba to attack the Netherworld race members.

Even with the assistance of the Sky Patrol Arrows, the battle was hard-won.

The Great Xuan Imperial Guards suffered hundreds of casualties, but they also captured some Netherworld race members alive. After some "persuasion," they recognized reality and agreed to open a passage to the Netherworld for Li Fan.

However, the "Return to Truth" charging process was not yet complete, so Li Fan was not in a hurry to enter.

Seeing Li Fan arrive, these Netherworld race members hastily knelt down.

Li Fan stood motionless, sensing a statue of himself not far away in the darkness.

After becoming the destined Holy Emperor of Great Xuan, Li Fan had also considered replicating a power similar to the Origin Power Essence.

Because it was somewhat similar to faith power, Li Fan had ordered the construction and erection of his statues in various locations, hoping to condense the Origin Power Essence through the sheer number of his populace.

But it was clear that he had been a bit naive.

Although the Origin Power Essence was an abandoned existence by True Immortals, it was still subtly a step above ordinary spiritual energy. Relying solely on the collective prayers of mortals without special means would clearly not be enough to condense it.

However, things changed after these Netherworld race members were captured and brought back.

Perhaps it was due to the Netherworld race members' innate and extremely strong faith in the Netherworld, but almost the moment they surrendered, Li Fan vaguely sensed a peculiar aura appearing within him.

It was crimson, similar to the Imperial Destiny of the Great Xuan Dynasty, and Li Fan's feeling was...

It was extremely similar to the golden Origin Power Essence of the Crimson Dust Compassionate True Immortal from his previous life!

Later, Li Fan even moved a statue of himself into this dungeon and ordered these dozen or so Netherworld race members to pray day and night.

The effect was also very significant.

The Origin Power Essence generated by these Netherworld race members was actually more abundant than that of hundreds of millions of Great Xuan citizens combined!

Li Fan studied their prayer methods and had the Great Xuan Imperial Guards learn and imitate them, but they all failed without exception.

After much thought, Li Fan could only attribute it to the special physique of the Netherworld race members.

"It seems to be related to the Netherworld's dark power. King Xuan Tian..."

The Netherworld, capable of interfering with the True Immortal Net to a certain extent, clearly harbored many secrets.

However, this was not something that could be explored in this lifetime.

"It's a pity that the Netherworld race members' reproductive capacity is not very strong."

"Otherwise, without the Faceless True Immortal statue, I could also weave a faith network."

The ability to bestow, strip away, and even transmit abilities remotely was truly too powerful and convenient.

Having tasted the benefits, Li Fan naturally found it difficult to abandon it.

Therefore, even though "Return to Truth" was not far off, Li Fan had not given up on researching this kind of power.

Clearly, Li Fan did not possess talent in this area.

"I'll have to wait until it's completely safe and let those guys research it."

Li Fan sighed slightly.

"Great Holy Emperor..." Just then, one of the Netherworld race members, who was kowtowing and praying, suddenly trembled and spoke, as if he had something to say.

"Hmm?" Li Fan's interest was piqued.

This was the first time they had actively tried to communicate with Li Fan.

After receiving Li Fan's permission, the Netherworld race member tremblingly continued, "While praying, I discovered that the master I originally served..."

He cautiously glanced at Li Fan, "that is, the Netherworld, does not seem to be very angry about our rebellion."

He swallowed his saliva, "The ancestral teachings passed down through generations in our clan always said not to betray the darkness, otherwise you would surely incur divine punishment."

"But I have tried it now, and it's all nonsense."

Chapter 1134: The Change of Divine Transformation

The Transformation of Deification

The young Netherworld race member, trembling, explained to Li Fan while occasionally glancing at Li Fan's expression.

But how could the face of the destined Holy Emperor be discerned by such a vulgar person?

Growing increasingly fearful, he poured out all his recent discoveries, "Holy Emperor, please enlighten me. Since I defected, I have been absolutely loyal. However, praying to the darkness has become as instinctive as breathing. So, during this time, while praying to you, the Holy Emperor, I couldn't help but naturally seek the darkness again."

"The darkness, as usual, responded to me..."

At this point, all the more than ten Netherworld race members in the secret chamber knelt down in extreme fear.

It was clear that this phenomenon had occurred to all of them.

Li Fan waved his hand gently, helping them all up.

In this lifetime, Li Fan was actually not very concerned about these Netherworld race members serving two masters.

Because in his plan, these individuals were merely tools for him to research "faith power" during the short period before "Return to Truth."

Once he initiated "Return to Truth," everything in the Xuanhuang Realm would be annihilated, let alone these Netherworld race members.

He was more interested in why the "darkness" would tolerate such duplicitous behavior.

If they were believers of the Faceless True Immortal and dared to serve two masters, they would likely have been torn to shreds by the True Immortal's power long ago.

"Either the power behind the darkness, the sovereign, is so noble that it is unbelievable, tolerating its believers to such an extent."

"Or..."

Li Fan's heart surged momentarily. "It has another motive. It wants to use the betrayal of its believers to infect beings of the same rank."

Thinking of this, Li Fan became vigilant.

He had always speculated about powerful beings in the world with the greatest malice.

He carefully discerned the trace of crimson power within him—though not much, it was extremely potent.

But after repeated confirmation, he found no connection to the dark power.

"Am I perhaps overthinking it?"

After a brief contemplation, Li Fan made his decision.

He would not allow any variables to affect the "Return to Truth" process of this lifetime.

First, he verbally praised the Netherworld race members for their honesty.

After leaving the underground secret chamber, Li Fan ordered Wang Xuanba to grant them a peaceful slumber.

Not a symbolic gesture, but a true slumber.

Li Fan was unwilling to be tainted by such impure faith power, yet he was afraid that directly slaughtering the Netherworld race members might attract the attention of the dark sovereign.

Therefore, he simply turned them into living corpses.

"It seems I need to find a way to solve the Netherworld race members' fertility problem. Cultivating believers must start with the new generation."

Wang Xuanba quickly completed the task and returned to report to Li Fan.

After years of continuously devouring and integrating exotic beast tissues, combined with practicing the enhanced version of the "Creation Furnace Technique," Wang Xuanba had transformed from the previous three-zhang giant into a normal-sized human.

He merely appeared somewhat robust and sturdy.

Possessing the abilities of numerous exotic beasts and an incredibly fast physical healing rate, even Sun Erlang, who was at the Great Perfection of Golden Core, would not be a match for Wang Xuanba in a fight to the death.

"Xuanba, have you encountered any confusion or difficulties in your recent cultivation?" Li Fan asked.

This was both to help Wang Xuanba resolve his doubts and to understand his physical condition, intending to improve the Creation Furnace Technique.

"Master. My body is indeed growing stronger by the day, and I feel as if I have inexhaustible energy. But..."

Wang Xuanba organized his thoughts, scratched his head, and said, "I've gradually developed two feelings. One is an inexplicable sense of crisis, as if there's a natural predator existing in the world. This feeling is particularly strong when passing through the Xuanhuang main world."

"The second is that I occasionally hear whispers. I don't understand what they're saying, but they give me a sense of familiarity and closeness."

After listening, Li Fan said calmly, "Although you have achieved a body like a furnace, your mind is not yet in that state. The residual thoughts of the exotic beasts you've devoured still linger in your heart. Refrain from cultivating for now and focus on recuperating."

Li Fan naturally understood the reason for Wang Xuanba's abnormal physical condition but did not explicitly state it. He merely let him rest in the small world of Great Xuan.

As the deadline for "Return to Truth" drew closer, Li Fan needed to eliminate all unstable factors.

Consequently, under his will, Great Xuan's pace of conquest of various realms halted.

Under the guise of "rest and recuperation, preparing for battle," the people of Great Xuan praised the destined Holy Emperor's great benevolence and wisdom. Time flew by rapidly.

By the end of Anchor Year 8, Li Fan looked at the fully charged progress bar and rose resolutely from the Holy Emperor's Seat in Xuanjing.

Without alerting anyone, he quietly went to the underground secret chamber.

He awakened the slumbering Netherworld race members and opened the passage to the Netherworld.

In the depths of the dark sea.

Li Fan opened the "Return to Truth" panel.

[You can choose one of the following options to retain:

1. One item held by yourself in this simulation.

2. Your cultivation realm in this simulation.

3. The simulated memories of a person closely related to you in this simulation. This memory can be inherited by that person.

4. Forgo the above options and accelerate the charging progress.]

...

The flashing light symbols had been present for eight years.

"Inherit cultivation."

Li Fan chanted silently in his heart, simultaneously reaching the peak of his vigilance.

At the same time, on the firmaments of Great Xuan, the Boundary-Leaving Realm, the Beastkin Realm, and other conquered small worlds, streaks of silver lines crisscrossed.

Like a giant net, it enveloped all living beings.

Few beings within the net could sense the impending fatal crisis; some looked up at the sky in surprise.

Only those with some cultivation, the "strong ones," felt a vague sense of unease.

The eternally unchanging dark sea seemed to suddenly stir with imperceptible waves.

A storm-like fluctuation descended upon Li Fan, creating a violent vortex around him.

Foundation Establishment, Golden Core, Nascent Soul...

Earth-shattering changes suddenly occurred within Li Fan's body.

Li Fan saw his cloud-like "Return to Truth" foundation instantly transform into a Golden Core.

Then, in an explosion that devoured all light, it evolved into the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven.

The Grotto-Heaven instantly completed an evolution that would normally take millennia.

The majestic Five Elements presented a grand spectacle.

Subsequently, the boundaries between the Five Elements became blurred.

Various changes unfolded rapidly within the Grotto-Heaven, dazzling to behold.

"The Xuanhuang world-destroying change."

The Five Elements merged into one. All changes within the newly born Grotto-Heaven were aimed at countering the non-existent world-destroying crisis of this world.

The giant tree in the original Wood-element Grotto-Heaven's leaves fell, leaving only bare branches.

However, its trunk gradually turned as hard as gold and iron.

The boundless sea of the Water-element Grotto-Heaven began to freeze for thousands of miles.

The scorching flames of the Fire-element Grotto-Heaven dimmed.

But they did not extinguish.

Instead, they continuously shrank and condensed.

Transforming into peculiar wisps of free-floating flame.

...

Various unbelievable changes occurred sequentially within Li Fan.

His realm also broke through Nascent Soul, rapidly advancing into the Deification stage.

Early Deification, Mid-Deification, Late Deification...

It only stopped upon reaching the Great Perfection of Deification.

Powerful.

Vibrant.

Dominated by aggression.

This was how Li Fan felt about himself at this moment.

But Li Fan had no time to savor it.

As he predicted, his transformation within the True Immortal Net had, after this round of "Return to Truth," quickly attracted the attention of the Faceless True Immortal beyond the high wall.

The surroundings no longer seemed entirely dark but were dotted with points of light.

Waves seemed to ebb and flow; uninvited guests had arrived in the silent dark sea.

"Return to Truth." Li Fan stated decisively.

The surrounding scene became still.

Then it rapidly misted over.

Perhaps it was because the Faceless True Immortal had not fully investigated the anomaly within the net, or perhaps the dark sea had shielded most of the Faceless True Immortal's power.

In any event, this "Return to Truth" process went very smoothly.

The void-like white mist did not last long before dissipating with a boom.

Light reappeared.

Anchor Year 1, Desolate Mountain Peak!

"Safe return."

"Proving my method is feasible."

Li Fan breathed a sigh of relief, temporarily ignoring the "Return to Truth" prompt.

He carefully examined his own face.

The influence of the Faceless True Immortal's power, after another "Return to Truth," had indeed weakened to a certain degree.

Li Fan's face was no longer a smooth, featureless expanse.

Instead, faint outlines of facial features had slightly protruded.

However, this appearance looked even more unsettling than being completely faceless.

But Li Fan did not care.

"Next, I just need to repeat the process."

He skillfully flew towards the capital city of Great Xuan.

Subsequently, what happened in Great Xuan and several other small worlds was almost identical to the previous lifetime, the 120th iteration.

The only possible difference was that Li Fan was more proficient and skipped many trial-and-error steps.

To be safe, Li Fan did not deviate from the plan; he even stopped researching the use of faith power from the Netherworld race members.

Minimizing all variables.

In the 121st iteration, the "Return to Truth" charging progress accelerated.

The charging was completed three months ahead of schedule.

Hiding in the dark sea, inheriting cultivation, returning to truth.

A seamless sequence.

Next, the 122nd iteration, the 123rd iteration...

All the way to the 125th iteration.

In early Anchor Year 8, Li Fan once again arrived at the dark sea.

He had a premonition that after this "Return to Truth," he would finally completely escape the influence of the Faceless True Immortal.

His face now looked like that of a normal person.

However, he still sensed certain imperfections, imperceptible to the naked eye or divine sense.

The influence of the True Immortal Net still existed.

But it was as fragile as brittle paper.

Li Fan suppressed the urge to take a reckless action.

Taking a deep breath, he silently chanted in his heart.

"Return to Truth!"

The scene instantly shifted between illusion and reality. Mist condensed and then scattered in an instant.

In the 126th iteration, Anchor Year 1, Desolate Mountain!

"Hoo!"

A feeling completely different from the previous lifetimes washed over Li Fan.

It was genuine freedom, unbridled and unrestrained.

"Long confined in a cage, I now return to nature."

Li Fan softly murmured, then slowly walked to the edge of the cliff.

"Xuanhuang Realm, I have returned!"

Facing the boundless sea of clouds, Li Fan chose to inherit his cultivation.

Above the Great Xuan, the sky and clouds churned instantly.

The entire world seemed to groan under the unbearable pressure, making creaking sounds as if on the verge of collapse.

However, this change was fleeting.

The immense aura radiating from Li Fan quickly subsided.

The sky returned to normal.

"Great Perfection of Deification. The Great Xuan world is already struggling to bear it."

"If I were at the Great Perfection of Dao Integration, the world would likely shatter the moment I inherited my cultivation."

"But it matters not. I can inherit my cultivation within the Xuanhuang Realm then, or upgrade the Great Xuan world first."

Li Fan shook his head slightly, then shifted his thoughts to the plan for this lifetime.

"In this lifetime, I will remain behind the scenes."

"My true self will never make an appearance unless absolutely necessary."

"Everything else is secondary, merely to verify my previous conjecture."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, gazing into the distance, as if seeing the sky of the Xuanhuang Great World.

"The transmission of dharma, what is its true connection to the Heavenly Doctor..."

Setting aside the argument that Dharma Transmission and the Heavenly Doctor had never appeared simultaneously, Li Fan's suspicion about their relationship stemmed from the "Record of Mending the Heavens" passed down by the Heavenly Doctor.

At the end of the "Record of Mending the Heavens," a theoretical method for saving worlds was described: "Borrowing a shell for reincarnation, breaking and then being reborn."

Worlds, even the most powerful cultivation worlds, like living beings, had an end to their existence.

When a world inevitably moved towards decay and demise, even the most skillful physicians would be powerless to reverse its fate, merely watching it perish.

This was the normal, theoretical situation.

However, the Heavenly Doctor proposed a possibility for saving worlds: finding another cultivation world in its prime and performing a "soul transference."

"The Heavenly Dao changes, and the world transforms."

"Although it seems absurd and incredible, for the Heavenly Doctor, it might not be impossible."

"Moreover..."

As Li Fan recalled the scenes witnessed since entering the Xuanhuang Realm, they flashed rapidly before his eyes.

"The phenomena predicted in the Record of Mending the Heavens during world reincarnation strongly resemble the current state of the Xuanhuang Realm."

"Anomalies arise, and the Heavenly Dao undergoes sudden changes."

"More importantly..."

"The Heavenly Doctor is from the Heavenly Law Realm, yet attaches such importance to the Xuanhuang Realm, desperately wandering the bleakest reaches of the sea, collecting fragments of other worlds."

"Coupled with the Heavenly Doctor's previous actions..."

Li Fan's eyes flickered.

"The accuracy of the Heavenly Doctor's 'World Mending Plan' is almost certain."

"The only chilling aspect is the attitude of Dharma Transmission."

"If he knew that the Heavenly Doctor was from another world and intended to 'borrow' the Xuanhuang Realm for rebirth, yet Dharma Transmission did not interfere at all."

"Instead, like the Heavenly Doctor, he also went out to collect world fragments in the star sea..."

"... "

Li Fan's heart felt heavy.

"Either it's possible that Dharma Transmission, lacking any better method to save the Xuanhuang Realm, was forced to act this way."

"Or..."

"Dharma Transmission and the Heavenly Doctor are actually the same person!"

"Or rather, Dharma Transmission is a clone of the Heavenly Doctor!"

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

In the Xuanhuang Realm, countless cultivators harbored a question:

Why did Dharma Transmission, while roaming the heavens, not leave behind a clone?

If there were only a clone, it would be enough to suppress all scoundrels in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Chapter 1135: Six Lives of Immortal Power Expulsion

The Power of the Six-Life Immortal Expulsion

If Dharma Transmission had a clone to suppress the Xuanhuang Realm, the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elders Society would never have engaged in large-scale warfare.

Perhaps the Five Elders Society was deliberately tolerated by Dharma Transmission as a tool to maintain the delicate balance of the Xuanhuang Realm. Dharma Transmission might not have cared about their conflicts, and might have even welcomed them.

However, the Xuanhuang Realm harbored too many lurking demons and ghosts, and the Immortal Ruins loomed in the distance.

With the potential to destroy the Xuanhuang Realm with a single word, leaving behind a clone in the Xuanhuang Realm would undoubtedly be more prudent.

Yet, Dharma Transmission, who cherished the Xuanhuang Realm, had specifically not done so.

In Li Fan's two experiences of world destruction, Dharma Transmission had either arrived late from beyond the heavens, letting out useless roars, or had not appeared at all, with only the Heavenly Doctor appearing.

This appeared highly suspicious.

Was refining a clone difficult for Dharma Transmission?

Although clone techniques were rare in the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan himself had repeatedly caused trouble using them.

How much more so for this progenitor of new dharma?

He could have easily done so, yet chose not to...

In fact, Xuanhuang Realm cultivators, while not daring to discuss it openly, often speculated privately about why Dharma Transmission had not left a clone to suppress the realm.

The common consensus was that Dharma Transmission had transcended worldly affairs and no longer cared about the Xuanhuang Realm.

Clearly, they understood neither the Xuanhuang Realm nor Dharma Transmission.

However, in Li Fan's view, if Dharma Transmission himself was a clone...

Then everything would become logical. Not that he couldn't, but that he was unable to!

In the 119th iteration, Li Qing's clone's strength had approached the original body, reaching the peak of Nascent Soul, just one step away from surpassing the original body.

At that time, Li Fan had wondered if a clone's strength could surpass the original body.

Later, by leveraging the Origin permission of the Heavenly Profound Mirror and consulting various ancient texts, Li Fan gained some insight.

A clone's strength surpassing the original body, and a clone further refining its own clone.

The latter should be more difficult to achieve.

Because if a clone could refine its own clone, it could theoretically extend infinitely, leading to a scenario where only one person existed in the entire world.

This was not absolutely impossible but exceeded the limits of mortal dharma.

Relatively speaking, a clone's strength surpassing the original body was easier to achieve.

"Heavenly Doctor, Dharma Transmission..."

Two faces flashed through Li Fan's mind. He then recalled seeing the illusory image of Dharma Transmission in the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters for the first time.

At that time, his body's instincts had spontaneously warned him due to a sense of familiarity.

And before that, the only existence above Dao Integration in the Xuanhuang Realm that he had encountered was the Heavenly Doctor.

"Although their appearances are not the same, there is a subtle resemblance between them."

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters retain a trace of Dharma Transmission's aura. Upon first entering, cultivators would have a sense of this, leading to hallucinations. My main body saw the image of Dharma Transmission, while the clone Li Qing saw..."

The Dao Dissolution Stone emitted a faint white light, faithfully reproducing the recorded images from that time.

Within a blurry light cluster, several figures stood.

Fragmented dialogue could be heard.

"Regarding this journey, how much confidence do you have?"

"Do my best, and leave the rest to fate."

"This doesn't sound like you."

"The disparity in strength is too great; we can only fight with our lives."

"Enough, you may go. Who knows if it's a blessing or a curse."

...

Li Fan recalled the scene in his chaotic consciousness when he was treating Han Hai in the 119th iteration.

"Venerable Heavenly Doctor has been gone for a long time; I wonder if this will succeed."

Han Hai sat at the main hall of the sect, while Gui She Tai Yi, as small as an ordinary turtle, spoke dejectedly from beneath his feet.

"Venerable Heavenly Doctor said before leaving that there is at least a ninety percent chance of success. We should have confidence in Him." Unlike Tai Yi's gloomy expression, Han Hai seemed relaxed, smiling and comforting him.

...

Li Fan stroked his chin.

Under the hypothesis that "Dharma Transmission is a clone of the Heavenly Doctor," all the fragmented clues obtained in the past instantly connected.

Li Fan reread his past memories.

He indeed found more traces.

...

Yinyin Island.

Elder Yin pointed to two human skeletons he had been treasuring and brought them close to Li Fan, whispering, "These two people are not of the same kind."

"Not of the same kind?" Li Fan was surprised. "What do you mean?"

Elder Yin gestured with his hands, pondered for a while, and seemed unable to find suitable words to describe it.

After much hesitation, he suddenly clenched his fist, his face contorted with frustration. "It's just a feeling, you know? They're both human, but these two humans lived in different eras and different regions. Perhaps they looked similar, and I dug them up from the seabed of Congyun, but there's an extremely special demarcation line that distinguishes these two skeletons..."

Elder Yin spoke cryptically, rambling for a long time without getting to the point.

...

During the second simulation of Tian Yang's eternal lingering thought.

To escape Tian Yang's frail body as much as possible and recover from his coma quickly, Li Fan studied the "Heavenly Doctor Immortal Scripture," prescribed a medicinal formula, and instructed his senior brother to refine it.

It was indeed effective, but when he woke up later, his second senior brother, Ling Xiao, told him:

"Junior brother, you are really lucky. Several of the medicinal ingredients in the formula you gave are unheard of. We searched all the surrounding markets and couldn't find anyone selling them. Some even said these herbs don't exist in the cultivation world."

"Heh heh, I don't believe it. How could a medicinal formula have all other ingredients but these few are non-existent?"

"We argued heatedly with the other party."

"Fortunately, a disciple from the Medicine King Sect happened to pass by and overheard our argument. Out of curiosity, he asked for the specific formula."

"Then, based on the principles of medicine, he selected a few common herbs as substitutes."

"Only then could junior brother drink this medicine!"

...

When he met the Ultimate Immortal and received the reward of the Jinfeng Jade Token.

The Ultimate Immortal pointed to a [Green Cloud Willow] in his courtyard and asked him, Han Yi, and Xi Men Yue if they knew the specifics of this tree.

Han Yi and Xi Men Yue both did not know, but only Li Fan, who had read the "Heavenly Doctor Immortal Scripture" thoroughly, could identify it.

Later, the Ultimate Immortal gave Li Fan much guidance because of this.

Li Fan was initially puzzled, but after further investigation, he realized.

Ink Ancient Bamboo, Green Field Wood, Unmoved Flower, Hundred Spirits Hawk, Nine Refinements Deer, and the hundreds of plants and creatures recorded in the "Heavenly Doctor Immortal Scripture." These plants and animals, which should have been common, had become scarce in the current Xuanhuang Realm.

Green Cloud Willow currently had only a small distribution in some areas of Luoyan State. The Ultimate Immortal's hometown was also in Luoyan State. At that time, the Ultimate Immortal mistook Li Fan for a fellow townsman and gave him special attention. ...

"The Heavenly Doctor is a cultivator from the Heavenly Law Realm. Different cultivation worlds have subtle differences in species. That's why many of the spiritual herbs I saw in the 'Heavenly Doctor Immortal Scripture' are not found in the ancient Xuanhuang Realm. The disciples of Shenhua Dao naturally searched all the surrounding cultivators and received answers that those medicinal herbs did not exist."

"But the Green Cloud Willow, originally only found in the Heavenly Law Realm, has now appeared in some regions years later. This is precisely a sign of the Heavenly Law's integration into the Xuanhuang Realm."

"Intermingling of the two realms."

"The two human skeletons at the bottom of Congyun Sea, one is a native of Xuanhuang, and the other belongs to the Heavenly Law Realm. Although both are human, they have subtle differences due to belonging to different cultivation worlds. These differences are so small that even Elder Yin's abilities could not discern them."

"It's not just the Congyun Sea that originated from the Heavenly Law Realm; many other regions in the Xuanhuang Realm also come from the Heavenly Doctor's hometown."

"Xi Men Yu's 'Record of Ancient and Modern Rivers and Mountains' deduces the changes in ancient and modern geography. The Xuanhuang Realm does not expand outward like it absorbs other small worlds and grotto-heavens, but rather seems to be dismembered and segmented, with fragments of other worlds inserted into the gaps."

Li Fan's thoughts churned.

"In the Immortal Subjugation Illusory Realm, Ningyuan City and the Purple霄 Sect were not far apart. But in the real world, Mr. Bai's underground secret chamber in Ningyuan City was buried deep beneath Mount Taixu, while the ruins of the Purple霄 Sect were in Linlang State, in the central region of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Both were in the same state, but thousands of years later, they were worlds apart."

"Integration, transformation."

"It's like performing precise surgery..."

"Heavenly Doctor..."

"The Xuanhuang Realm has undergone such earth-shattering changes over thousands of years. Ordinary cultivators are completely unaware. Even those with extraordinary talent like Xi Men Yu, who can discern the truth from the mist, have their works suppressed by the Myriad Immortals Alliance and unable to be disseminated."

Piecing together all the clues, Li Fan roughly reconstructed a possible vague truth.

After King Xuan Tian's disappearance and the annihilation of the Xuan Tian Sect, the Xuanhuang Realm entered an era ruled by the Ten Immortal Dao Sects.

However, the threat from the Immortal Ruins did not change with the change in power in the Xuanhuang Realm.

The Ten Immortal Dao Sects still had to solve the crisis of falling into the Immortal Ruins.

The Xuan Tian Sect's [Floating Crossing the Starry Sky Grand Formation] was clearly the most effective method among them.

Thus, the Ten Immortal Dao Sects continued to push the grand formation, capturing other worlds in the void.

Finally, one day, they unexpectedly encountered the Heavenly Law Realm.

From the combat power of Tian Jue, Tian Yu, and others, it could be seen that the overall strength of the Heavenly Law Realm back then was not much weaker than the Xuanhuang Realm.

Especially since the Xuanhuang Realm had already experienced internal strife, with the ultimate powerhouse King Xuan Tian and his twelve Law Kings all having unknown fates.

The Heavenly Law Realm naturally would not sit idly by.

A large-scale bloody battle erupted between the two sides.

The Cloud Water Heavenly Palace in the Heavenly Law Realm, and the Shenhua Dao in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Neither were particularly powerful sects, yet they had still expended almost all their disciples in this war.

"Perhaps the Floating Crossing the Starry Sky Grand Formation was also damaged at that time."

"In the later stages of the war, both sides were trapped and a stalemate ensued."

"At this moment, the Heavenly Doctor planned to use the 'Dharma Transmission' to infiltrate the Xuanhuang Realm, shake its foundation with new dharma, and disintegrate the Xuanhuang from within."

"But for some unknown reason, by the time Dharma Transmission appeared on the Xuanhuang land, a considerable amount of time had passed."

"And by the time the Ten Immortal Dao Sects were destroyed and the Xuanhuang Realm's strength was greatly diminished..."

"When the Heavenly Doctor returned to the Heavenly Law Realm, he found a scene of ruins and devastation."

...

Li Fan did his best to reconstruct the history shrouded in mist.

After a while, he frowned slightly.

Although most of it seemed to fit together, he still felt a few points that were not quite right.

"Firstly, the timing of Dharma Transmission and the Heavenly Doctor's appearance in the Xuanhuang Realm. Or rather, there was a time lag in the Heavenly Doctor's journey between the two realms."

Recalling the peculiar journey of the Medicine King Sect, Li Fan couldn't help but glance towards the Immortal Ruins outside the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Could it be the influence of the Immortal Ruins' celestial power?"

"Besides that, there's another point of confusion. The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao should naturally generate some form of rejection response towards outsiders and foreign objects, similar to how anomalies arise during the integration of worlds due to differences in laws."

"If Dharma Transmission were truly an outsider, then when he widely propagated his teachings and attempted to subvert the world's foundation, heavenly wrath would surely have erupted. Moreover, I recall the Ten Immortal Dao Sects once investigated Dharma Transmission's background..."

"Although his true identity might not have been clearly ascertained, they should have at least figured out whether he was a Xuanhuang Realm cultivator or not."

"Dharma Transmission's identity seems peculiar as well."

...

On Desolate Mountain Peak, Li Fan stood for a long time, his thoughts undisturbed.

After half a month, he finally emerged from his meditation.

He began to prepare for the plans of this lifetime.

"Since I am to remain behind the scenes, my true self will not reveal himself under any circumstances."

"Using a clone to create a decoy to attract attention would be ideal."

"Heh heh, the Faceless Holy Emperor who unified tens of thousands of small worlds..."

Li Fan gracefully descended the mountain and refined a clone using the vital blood of his young disciples Sun Erlang and Wang Xuanba.

"The Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex does not have any requirements for talent. Besides, the cultivation aptitude of these two is not too poor."

"Completely severing all memories related to 'Return to Truth' and my own..."

As a faceless figure slowly took shape before Li Fan's eyes, Li Fan nodded with satisfaction after observing it for a long time.

"Destined Holy Emperor, conquer all heavens, and let myriad realms submit."

"You shall be named Li Ping!"

As Li Fan thought this, his figure gradually faded.

When the clone Li Ping woke up, he first scanned his surroundings.

Then, as if contemplating something, he headed straight for the capital of Great Xuan.

Not long after, Li Fan's true self slowly reappeared.

"Although he possesses the Nascent Soul realm, he lacks actual combat power. However, for the mortals of Great Xuan, it is more than enough."

"The trajectory of Great Xuan in this lifetime should be the same as before."

"However, I will make minor adjustments."

...

Li Fan gazed into the distance towards the Eastern Ruins Abyss of Great Xuan.

In fact, with his current strength of Great Perfection of Deification, unmatched below the Longevity realm, and capable of contending with ordinary Longevity realm cultivators, even if he went to the Xuanhuang Realm before the "Return to Truth" charging was complete, as long as he didn't court death, he should not encounter any fatal dangers.

But after thinking about it...

Li Fan shook his head and did not act impulsively.

"No need to rush."

He turned back to his thatched hut on the mountain peak and sat in meditation.

Chapter 1136: Heavenly Doctor Transmits Dharma Mystery (Combined Chapter)

If the Heavenly Venerate of Dharma Transmission had a clone to suppress the Xuanhuang Realm, the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elder Society would never have engaged in large-scale warfare. Perhaps the Five Elder Society was deliberately tolerated by Dharma Transmission as a tool to maintain the Xuanhuang Realm's delicate balance. Dharma Transmission might not have cared about their conflicts, and might have even welcomed them.

However, the Xuanhuang Realm harbored too many lurking demons and ghosts, and the Immortal Ruins loomed in the distance. With the potential to destroy the Xuanhuang Realm with a single word, leaving behind a clone in the Xuanhuang Realm would undoubtedly be more prudent. Yet, the Heavenly Venerate of Dharma Transmission, who cherished the Xuanhuang Realm, deliberately did not do so.

In Li Fan's two experiences of world destruction, Dharma Transmission had either arrived late from beyond the heavens, letting out useless roars, or had not appeared at all, with only the Heavenly Doctor appearing. This seemed highly suspicious. Was refining a clone difficult for Dharma Transmission? Although clone techniques were rare in the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan himself had repeatedly caused trouble using them. How much more so for this progenitor of new dharma? He could have easily done so, yet chose not to...

In fact, Xuanhuang Realm cultivators, while not daring to discuss it openly, often speculated privately about why Dharma Transmission had not left a clone to suppress the realm. The common consensus was that Dharma Transmission had transcended worldly affairs and no longer cared about the Xuanhuang Realm. Clearly, they understood neither the Xuanhuang Realm nor Dharma Transmission.

But in Li Fan's view, if Dharma Transmission himself was a clone... then everything would become logical. Not that he couldn't, but that he was unable to!

In the 119th iteration, the clone Li Qing's strength had approached the original body, reaching the peak of Nascent Soul, just one step away from surpassing the original body. Li Fan had wondered then if a clone's strength could surpass the original body. Later, by leveraging the Origin permission of the Heavenly Profound Mirror and consulting various ancient texts, Li Fan gained some insight.

A clone's strength surpassing the original body, and a clone further refining its own clone. The latter should be more difficult to achieve. Because if a clone could refine its own clone, it could theoretically extend infinitely, leading to a scenario where only one person existed in the entire world. This was not absolutely impossible but exceeded the limits of mortal dharma. Relatively speaking, a clone's strength surpassing the original body was easier to achieve.

"Heavenly Doctor, Dharma Transmission..." Two faces flashed through Li Fan's mind. He then recalled seeing the illusory image of Dharma Transmission in the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters for the first time. At that time, his body's instincts had spontaneously warned him due to a sense of familiarity. And before that, the only existence above Dao Integration in the Xuanhuang Realm that he had encountered was the Heavenly Doctor.

"Although their appearances are not the same, there is a subtle resemblance between them."

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters retain a trace of Dharma Transmission's aura. Upon first entering, cultivators would have a sense of this, leading to hallucinations. My main body saw the image of Dharma Transmission, while the clone Li Qing saw..."

The Dao Dissolution Stone emitted a faint white light, faithfully reproducing the recorded images from that time. Within a blurry light cluster, several figures stood. Fragmented dialogue could be heard from within.

"Regarding this journey, how much confidence do you have?"

"Do my best, and leave the rest to fate."

"This doesn't sound like you."

"The disparity in strength is too great; we can only fight with our lives."

"Enough, you may go. Who knows if it's a blessing or a curse."

...

Li Fan then recalled the scene in his chaotic consciousness when he was treating Han Hai in the 119th iteration.

"Venerable Heavenly Doctor has been gone for a long time; I wonder if this will succeed."

Han Hai sat at the main hall of the sect, while Gui She Tai Yi, as small as an ordinary turtle, spoke dejectedly from beneath his feet.

"Venerable Heavenly Doctor said before leaving that there is at least a ninety percent chance of success. We should have confidence in Him." Unlike Tai Yi's gloomy expression, Han Hai seemed relaxed, smiling and comforting him.

...

Li Fan stroked his chin. Under the hypothesis that "Dharma Transmission is a clone of the Heavenly Doctor," all the fragmented clues obtained in the past instantly connected. Li Fan reread his past memories. He indeed found more traces.

...

Yinyin Island. Elder Yin pointed to two human skeletons he had been treasuring and brought them close to Li Fan, whispering, "These two people are not of the same kind."

"Not of the same kind?" Li Fan was surprised. "What do you mean?"

Elder Yin gestured with his hands, pondered for a while, and seemed unable to find suitable words to describe it. After much hesitation, he suddenly clenched his fist, his face contorted with frustration. "It's just a feeling, you know? They're both human, but these two humans lived in different eras and different regions. Perhaps they looked similar, and I dug them up from the seabed of Congyun, but there's an extremely special demarcation line that distinguishes these two skeletons..."

Elder Yin spoke cryptically, rambling for a long time without getting to the point.

...

During the second simulation of Tian Yang's eternal lingering thought. To escape Tian Yang's frail body as much as possible and recover from his coma quickly, Li Fan studied the "Heavenly Doctor Immortal Scripture," prescribed a medicinal formula, and instructed his senior brother to refine it. It was indeed effective, but when he woke up later, his second senior brother, Ling Xiao, told him:

"Junior brother, you are really lucky. Several of the medicinal ingredients in the formula you gave are unheard of. We searched all the surrounding markets and couldn't find anyone selling them. Some even said these herbs don't exist in the cultivation world."

"Heh heh, I don't believe it. How could a medicinal formula have all other ingredients but these few are non-existent?"

"We argued heatedly with the other party."

"Fortunately, a disciple from the Medicine King Sect happened to pass by and overheard our argument. Out of curiosity, he asked for the specific formula."

"Then, based on the principles of medicine, he selected a few common herbs as substitutes."

"Only then could junior brother drink this medicine!"

...

When he met the Ultimate Immortal and received the reward of the Jinfeng Jade Token. The Ultimate Immortal pointed to a [Green Cloud Willow] in his courtyard and asked him, Han Yi, and Xi Men Yue if they knew the specifics of this tree. Han Yi and Xi Men Yue both did not know, but only Li Fan, who had read the "Heavenly Doctor Immortal Scripture" thoroughly, could identify it. Later, the Ultimate Immortal gave Li Fan much guidance because of this. Li Fan was initially puzzled, but after further investigation, he realized.

Ink Ancient Bamboo, Green Field Wood, Unmoved Flower, Hundred Spirits Hawk, Nine Refinements Deer, and the hundreds of plants and creatures recorded in the "Heavenly Doctor Immortal Scripture." These plants and animals, which should have been common, had become scarce in the current Xuanhuang Realm. Green Cloud Willow currently had only a small distribution in some areas of Luoyan State. The Ultimate Immortal's hometown was also in Luoyan State. At that time, the Ultimate Immortal mistook Li Fan for a fellow townsman and gave him special attention. ...

"The Heavenly Doctor is a cultivator from the Heavenly Law Realm. Different cultivation worlds have subtle differences in species. That's why many of the spiritual herbs I saw in the 'Heavenly Doctor Immortal Scripture' are not found in the ancient Xuanhuang Realm. The disciples of Shenhua Dao naturally searched all the surrounding cultivators and received answers that those medicinal herbs did not exist."

"But the Green Cloud Willow, originally only found in the Heavenly Law Realm, has now appeared in some regions years later. This is precisely a sign of the Heavenly Law's integration into the Xuanhuang Realm."

"Intermingling of the two realms."

"The two human skeletons at the bottom of Congyun Sea, one is a native of Xuanhuang, and the other belongs to the Heavenly Law Realm human remains. Although both are human, they have subtle differences due to belonging to different cultivation worlds. These differences are so small that even Elder Yin's abilities could not discern them."

"Not only did the Congyun Sea originate from the Heavenly Law Realm; more regions of the Xuanhuang Realm also come from the Heavenly Doctor's hometown."

"Xi Men Yu's 'Record of Ancient and Modern Rivers and Mountains' deduces the changes in ancient and modern geography. The Xuanhuang Realm does not expand outward like it absorbs other small worlds and grotto-heavens, but rather seems to be dismembered and segmented, with fragments of other worlds inserted into the gaps."

Li Fan's thoughts churned.

"In the Immortal Subjugation Illusory Realm, Ningyuan City and the Purple Heaven Sect were not far apart. But in the real world, Mr. Bai's underground secret chamber in Ningyuan City was buried deep beneath Mount Taixu, while the ruins of the Purple Heaven Sect were in Linlang State, in the central region of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Both were in the same state, but thousands of years later, they were worlds apart."

"Integration, transformation."

"It's like performing precise surgery..."

"Heavenly Doctor..."

"The Xuanhuang Realm has undergone such earth-shattering changes over thousands of years. Ordinary cultivators are completely unaware. Even those with extraordinary talent like Xi Men Yu, who can discern the truth from the mist, have their works suppressed by the Myriad Immortals Alliance and unable to be disseminated."

Piecing together all the clues, Li Fan roughly reconstructed a possible vague truth. After King Xuan Tian's disappearance and the annihilation of the Xuan Tian Sect, the Xuanhuang Realm entered an era ruled by the Ten Immortal Dao Sects. However, the threat from the Immortal Ruins did not change with the change in power in the Xuanhuang Realm. The Ten Immortal Dao Sects still had to solve the crisis of falling into the Immortal Ruins. The Xuan Tian Sect's [Floating Crossing the Starry Sky Grand Formation] was clearly the most effective method among them. Thus, the Ten Immortal Dao Sects continued to push the grand formation, capturing other worlds in the void. Finally, one day, they unexpectedly encountered the Heavenly Law Realm.

From the combat power of Tian Jue, Tian Yu, and others, it could be seen that the overall strength of the Heavenly Law Realm back then was not much weaker than the Xuanhuang Realm. Especially since the Xuanhuang Realm had already experienced internal strife, with the ultimate powerhouse King Xuan Tian and his twelve Law Kings all having unknown fates. The Heavenly Law Realm naturally would not sit idly by. A large-scale bloody battle erupted between the two sides. The Cloud Water Heavenly Palace in the Heavenly Law Realm, and the Shenhua Dao in the Xuanhuang Realm. Neither were particularly powerful sects, yet they had still expended almost all their disciples in this war.

"Perhaps the Floating Crossing the Starry Sky Grand Formation was also damaged at that time."

"In the later stages of the war, both sides were trapped and a stalemate ensued."

"At this moment, the Heavenly Doctor planned to use the 'Dharma Transmission' to infiltrate the Xuanhuang Realm, shake its foundation with new dharma, and disintegrate the Xuanhuang from within."

"But for some unknown reason, by the time Dharma Transmission appeared on the Xuanhuang land, a considerable amount of time had passed."

"And by the time the Ten Immortal Dao Sects were destroyed and the Xuanhuang Realm's strength was greatly diminished..."

"When the Heavenly Doctor returned to the Heavenly Law Realm, he found a scene of ruins and devastation."

...

Li Fan did his best to reconstruct the history shrouded in mist. After a while, he frowned slightly. Although most of it seemed to fit together, he still felt a few points that were not quite right.

"Firstly, the timing of Dharma Transmission and the Heavenly Doctor's appearance in the Xuanhuang Realm. Or rather, there was a time lag in the Heavenly Doctor's journey between the two realms." Recalling the peculiar journey of the Medicine King Sect, Li Fan couldn't help but glance towards the Immortal Ruins outside the Xuanhuang Realm. "Could it be the influence of the Immortal Ruins' celestial power?"

"Besides that, there's another point of confusion. The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao should naturally generate some form of rejection response towards outsiders and foreign objects, similar to how anomalies arise during the integration of worlds due to differences in laws."

"If Dharma Transmission were truly an outsider, then when he widely propagated his teachings and attempted to subvert the world's foundation, heavenly wrath would surely have erupted. Moreover, I recall the Ten Immortal Dao Sects once investigated Dharma Transmission's background..."

"Although his true identity might not have been clearly ascertained, they should have at least figured out whether he was a Xuanhuang Realm cultivator or not."

"Dharma Transmission's identity seems peculiar as well."

...

On Desolate Mountain Peak, Li Fan stood for a long time, his thoughts undisturbed. After half a month, he finally emerged from his meditation. He began to prepare for the plans of this lifetime.

"Since I am to remain behind the scenes, my true self will not reveal himself under any circumstances."

"Using a clone to create a decoy to attract attention would be ideal."

"Heh heh, the Faceless Holy Emperor who unified tens of thousands of small worlds..." Li Fan gracefully descended the mountain and refined a clone using the vital blood of his young disciples Sun Erlang and Wang Xuanba.
