"The Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex does not have any requirements for talent. Besides, the cultivation aptitude of these two is not too poor."

"Completely severing all memories related to 'Return to Truth' and my own..."

As a faceless figure slowly took shape before Li Fan's eyes, Li Fan nodded with satisfaction after observing it for a long time.

"Destined Holy Emperor, conquer all heavens, and let myriad realms submit."

"You shall be named Li Ping!"

As Li Fan thought this, his figure gradually faded. When the clone Li Ping woke up, he first scanned his surroundings. Then, as if contemplating something, he headed straight for the capital of Great Xuan. Not long after, Li Fan's true self slowly reappeared.

"Although he possesses the Nascent Soul realm, he lacks actual combat power. However, for the mortals of Great Xuan, it is more than enough."

"The trajectory of Great Xuan in this lifetime should be the same as before."

"However, I will make minor adjustments."

...

Li Fan gazed into the distance towards the Eastern Ruins Abyss of Great Xuan. In fact, with his current strength of Great Perfection of Deification, unmatched below the Longevity realm, and capable of contending with ordinary Longevity realm cultivators, even if he went to the Xuanhuang Realm before the "Return to Truth" charging was complete, as long as he didn't court death, he should not encounter any fatal dangers. But after thinking about it... Li Fan shook his head and did not act impulsively.

"No need to rush." He turned back to his thatched hut on the mountain peak and sat in meditation.

Chapter 1137: The Sacred Dynasty Displays Its Power

The Willful Inheritance

Li Fan lay on the bed with his eyes closed, seemingly oblivious to Wu Ninglu's words.

Wu Ninglu's beautiful eyes darted around, about to shed her clothes and climb onto the bed herself.

However, just as her body was about to approach Li Fan, an bone-chilling coldness made her instinctively shiver and retreat.

Upon closer inspection, Wu Ninglu was horrified to discover that a layer of frost had inexplicably formed on her skin at that very moment.

If she hadn't instinctively dodged, Wu Ninglu had no doubt that her husband would have frozen her into an ice sculpture!

She was both pleased and angered.

Though she had a thousand unsaid words, Li Fan suddenly spoke softly, "I just broke through and cannot yet perfectly control my power. It's best if you don't approach me casually for now."

Rejected in her attempt to offer warmth, Wu Ninglu was no longer angry.

Her face lit up with joy, and she nodded repeatedly. "Okay, okay. I didn't expect you, Sun Lang, to give me such a big surprise after disappearing for over half a year. This is a major event, and the clan must be informed!"

Just as Wu Ninglu was about to leave, an ice wall inexplicably appeared, blocking the door and obstructing her path.

Turning back, she looked at Li Fan.

Li Fan still had his eyes closed, but he spoke a seemingly unrelated sentence.

"Regarding the matter of which of the three elders in the clan will take up the post at the Law Enforcement Hall, has a decision been made?"

Wu Ninglu paused for a moment, then immediately understood.

"The Patriarch naturally cannot leave. Elder Uncle and Third Uncle have been pushing the responsibility back and forth for a while, but recently, it's said that Elder Uncle finally relented and compromised..."

Saying this, Wu Ninglu couldn't help but retract her foot.

"Our branch is not exactly well-regarded in the clan. If my promotion to Dao Integration becomes known, they might send me to the Law Enforcement Hall in their stead. At least three hundred years of confinement outside..."

"Hmph."

"If it weren't for the fact that I sustained injuries during my breakthrough and my realm is unstable, fearing that outsiders might detect it and reap the rewards. I wouldn't have returned prematurely."

Li Fan sighed slightly.

"Although taking up a position at the Law Enforcement Hall will come with certain material compensation from the clan and the Immortal Alliance, most of that is already useless to me. Moreover, three hundred years is far too long."

Li Fan suddenly opened his eyes and looked at Wu Ninglu.

"Therefore, my advancement must be kept secret for now."

When their eyes met, Wu Ninglu's body trembled violently, and she subconsciously nodded.

Li Fan closed his eyes again to recuperate.

Silence descended upon the room once more.

The faint ice-sealing field caused Wu Ninglu to operate her spiritual energy at full capacity just to maintain her body temperature.

Curled up in a corner of the room, Wu Ninglu felt both wronged and envious.

"Is this the might of Dao Integration? I never thought he would actually reach Dao Integration. I originally thought Sun Weizhou would be the first among the younger generation to break through."

Wu Ninglu looked at her husband, who was recuperating and cultivating, her mind racing with thoughts.

Only when the fluctuations of his aura gradually subsided did she realize he was still meditating with his eyes closed.

Feeling sulky, Wu Ninglu quietly left the room.

...

"If I'm not mistaken, this foolish woman will soon leak the news that her dao companion is a Dao Integration expert."

"It's all for a little benefit promised by Sun Lushang. "

"It's not that she's truly foolish. After all, benefits held in hand are real. As long as Sun Ang is a Dao Integration expert, no matter where he is, people will treat her, the wife of a Dao Integration expert, with respect." Li Fan's gaze was profound, as if he could see through time.

Just as Li Fan predicted.

Half a month later, when Wu Ninglu personally witnessed the generous offers made by her Elder Uncle and Third Uncle to avoid serving at the Law Enforcement Hall, she couldn't help but feel tempted.

After all, her life with Sun Ang had not been particularly smooth in the past. They had no say in the clan's decisions, and good fortune always went to others first.

However, due to Li Fan's previous instructions, she did not speak directly.

But Wu Ninglu's unusual expression did not escape the eyes of the Sun family's several Dao Integration elders.

Coupled with the subtle fluctuation that Li Fan had deliberately emitted upon his return earlier, it led them to have implicit suspicions.

After some inquiries, Wu Ninglu reluctantly revealed the matter.

Sun Lushang was overjoyed and immediately dragged his two brothers to visit.

Li Fan feigned helplessness and anger, looking at Wu Ninglu.

The three elders at the Dao Integration stage took the initiative to intercede for her.

Then, appealing to reason and emotion, they persuaded Li Fan one after another.

For the overall benefit of the clan, he finally had to agree to go to the Law Enforcement Hall in their stead.

"Don't worry, Lu'er. During your absence, we will take good care of Ninglu and ensure she doesn't suffer any grievances." Sun Lushang promised.

Lu'er was Sun Ang's given name.

Logically speaking, as fellow Dao Integration cultivators, even as elders, calling him by his given name was inappropriate. However, Sun Lushang continued to use it, perhaps to remind "Sun Ang" of his status as a disciple of the Sun family.

To ensure that "Sun Ang" could pass the Myriad Immortals Alliance's review, the three Sun family Dao Integration elders jointly tested "Sun Ang's" actual combat strength.

Li Fan mainly focused on defense, occasionally unleashing one or two low-power techniques.

After persisting for hundreds of rounds, he gradually showed signs of faltering.

"Lu'er, the Essence of Heaven and Earth you absorbed is truly extraordinary. Although its offensive power is lacking, its field effect of freezing everything around can block most offensive maneuvers."

The three Sun family Dao Integration elders were quite satisfied with Li Fan's performance.

Even as a newly advanced Dao Integration cultivator, this level of strength was enough to satisfy the Immortal Alliance's requirements.

Before heading to the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters, Li Fan secretly called Wu Ninglu to his side.

"I know you've been avoiding me lately, afraid I'll blame you?"

"How could I?"

"Actually, I know that even if you didn't tell me, my breakthrough to Dao Integration couldn't be hidden for long. Some things are inevitable."

"Besides, we are one. If I work hard for three hundred years to gain some benefits for you, it's nothing."

Wu Ninglu was greatly surprised by Li Fan's words and was momentarily stunned.

She was even a little moved.

"While I'm away, you must be careful on your own."

"Those old guys in the family say nice things, but who knows what they're really like."

"During this trip, I made a friend who helped me greatly in my breakthrough."

As Li Fan spoke, he handed her a communication jade talisman.

"If you encounter any insurmountable problems, contact him."

"He should be able to help you resolve them."

"However, this person is also a Dao Integration cultivator and has a rather eccentric personality. Don't ask for his help unless absolutely necessary."

"Remember this, remember this."

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1138: Thermal Death and Ice Seal Transformation

"The changes of heaven and earth, the transformation of yin and yang, reside within a single heart..."

Li Fan's true form hovered above Mount Jieli, gazing down at the Great Xuan realm. As he sensed the impending changes within his body intertwining with the external world, he couldn't help but sigh inwardly.

"Perhaps the Heavenly Doctor used a similar method to dissect and alter the Xuanhuang Realm back then," he mused. "If he hadn't paved the way, with my current strength, I could have already begun modifying certain regions of the Xuanhuang Realm."

It was still Anchor Year 1.

His clone, Li Ping, followed the plan and headed to Xuanjing City. With lightning speed, he eliminated the corrupt ruler and, according to the mandate of heaven, established a new dynasty.

This dynasty was not merely a tool built in haste to escape the Faceless True Immortal. Instead, it was to prepare for investigating the true identity of the Dharma Transmitting Heavenly Venerate. Naturally, a formal approach was necessary, and the old dynasty's name could not be retained.

Thus, seven days later, Li Ping announced to the world through his techniques that the new dynasty would be named [启] (Qǐ) – Enlightenment.

As [Holy Emperor's Seats] sprang up across the Great Xuan, the Enlightenment Dynasty's absolute authority was rapidly established among the populace. Especially after the [Heaven and Earth Furnace] was forged and placed within the Holy Emperor's Seats, the concentration of spiritual energy in Great Xuan steadily increased.

Li Fan's true form, meanwhile, quietly utilized his own vast spiritual power within the midst of this spiritual energy resurgence, accelerating and transforming the process.

"What I am releasing in Great Xuan is one of the changes that naturally occurred in the last life after the Xuanhuang Realm faced an apocalyptic crisis."

In Li Fan's current view, the Great Xuan small world was like a raw stone embryo, its form constantly changing under the shaping hands of his power.

"When heaven and earth transform, heroes emerge. Because heroes are often born in accordance with the mandate of heaven and favored by it, their aptitude and talent usually far surpass ordinary people. In mortal folklore, there are tales of chaotic-era heroes being fallen celestial bodies, and the principle is essentially the same."

"This transformation is called [Heaven Bestows its Favor, Myriad Stars Descend]."

As the power of the world's impending transformation, residing within him, diffused outward, Li Fan could clearly feel the changes occurring in the Great Xuan world under this influence.

In the coming decades, true Child of Destiny individuals, like Mr. Bai and Su Yuqing, would emerge in droves, like bamboo shoots after a spring rain.

The actual innate talent of a Child of Destiny is closely related to the fortitude of the world. As Children of Destiny, Mr. Bai's innate talent naturally far surpassed that of Su Yuqing from the Mortal World Leaving Realm.

The initial batch of Children of Destiny born in Great Xuan might even be weaker than those in the Xuanhuang Realm. However, as Li Fan continuously reformed Great Xuan and the small world gradually ascended, the quality of Great Xuan's geniuses would eventually catch up to and surpass those of the Xuanhuang Realm!

"This is the transformation of heaven and humanity corresponding to each other, the way of nurturing man through heaven."

Li Fan carefully observed the subtle changes as the world was slowly shaped by his hands, a sense of pride and detachment washing over him.

"This is truly changing heaven and earth with a mere gesture. What I am changing now is merely a mortal small world. I wonder what it would feel like for someone like the Heavenly Doctor to casually knead the Xuanhuang Realm..."

World and man.

Vastness and insignificance.

Yet now, a minuscule human was reshaping the world.

The thrill derived from this stark contrast was even greater than the satisfaction of improving one's cultivation or realm, almost captivating Li Fan to the point of addiction.

Fortunately, the Great Xuan Immortal Heart Incantation operated autonomously, jolting Li Fan awake not long after.

"Hmm... this is the mental wandering that naturally occurs after mastering power that does not originally belong to one's own level."

"If one were to indulge in it continuously, there's a high probability of being assimilated by the world's Heavenly Dao, losing one's self-awareness and becoming a part of it."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, contemplating.

In the process of shaping the new mortal world of Great Xuan, Li Fan also discovered that the power of impending world transformation was not a perpetual force.

"As the world operates according to its transformations, this energy is consumed. For example, the [Heaven Bestows its Favor, Myriad Stars Descend] that I am currently activating, without further amplification, will likely only last for about fifty years based on the initial drive. It might even be shorter due to various unforeseen factors."

...

While waiting for the "Return to Truth" process to complete its charging, Li Fan constantly pondered and contemplated the principles of the world's Heavenly Dao and his future path.

Within the Great Xuan Dynasty, terrifying and rapid changes were occurring every moment.

Anchor Year 1: [Body Purifying Spirit Pools] were newly constructed in various locations. Accompanied by them was a cultivation technique called the [Heart Cleansing Incantation]. Citizens could visit the spirit pools and, with the aid of the incantation's power, expel the mortal miasma from their bodies.

Anchor Year 2: The spiritual energy concentration in Great Xuan had already reached the average level of the Xuanhuang Realm. The Destined Holy Emperor appeared in the sky, personally bestowing immortal techniques upon all beings, known as the [Enlightenment Spirit Yuan Technique]. Any citizen of Great Xuan who shed their mortal coil could cultivate it. Those who achieved minor success in the technique could proceed to the Sacred Capital to meet the Destined Holy Emperor for personal guidance.

Simultaneously, in a secret underground base within the Sacred Capital, tens of thousands of robust soldiers began tempering their physical bodies and absorbing the essence of exotic beasts through the [Creation Furnace Technique].

Anchor Year 3: The Destined Holy Emperor issued a policy encouraging childbirth. Families with three or more children would receive a fifty percent reduction in taxes. For more children, the court would provide additional rewards. To support this policy, [Sacred Medical Halls] were established throughout Great Xuan. The physicians in these halls were all cultivators who had embarked on the immortal path, personally taught by the Destined Holy Emperor. They possessed supreme medical skills. While they couldn't bring the dead back to life or regrow flesh and bone, they could easily resolve common ailments and the various dangers encountered during childbirth. Besides [Sacred Medical Halls], [Sacred Academies] and [Sacred Heart Halls] were gradually being constructed.

As the names suggested, Sacred Academies were places of learning. Through synchronized image transmission, citizens across Great Xuan could receive personal tutelage from renowned masters in the Sacred Capital within the Sacred Academies of their respective cities. The great Destined Holy Emperor himself would even lecture them from time to time.

The Holy Emperor's gaze seemed to encompass all living beings across heaven and earth simultaneously. When he lectured, he would also pose questions to students in various regions. Those who became overly nervous and couldn't answer were not reprimanded; instead, they received kind encouragement.

As time passed, the Destined Holy Emperor's status in the hearts of the populace became increasingly revered and unshakable. Consequently, more and more people visited the Sacred Heart Hall to offer prayers daily. Within the Sacred Heart Hall stood a towering statue of the Destined Holy Emperor. His face was obscured, but his aura was divine and inviolable. Citizens of Great Xuan with worries, desires, or regrets... could express anything to the Holy Emperor. The Holy Emperor accepted all, showing no blame. It was even rumored that he occasionally bestowed blessings, silently resolving the concerns of his devoted followers.

Aside from these sacred blessings, the dynasty did not lack necessary disciplinary institutions. The Sacred Supervisory Court monitored the realm, and any act that violated the dynasty's laws would receive the most severe punishment. The most terrifying punishment was not death, but the extraction of consciousness and eternal imprisonment within the Sacred Heart Hall, to forever face the scolding of the Great Xuan populace.

...

The entire Great Xuan Dynasty was like a flying boat with ever-increasing power, its strength surging forward and growing daily. Yet, it had not launched any external wars, merely accumulating strength.

By Anchor Year 8, Li Fan, seeing that the "Return to Truth" charging was complete, rose resolutely from the Holy Emperor's Seat in Xuanjing. Without alerting anyone, he quietly went to the underground secret chamber. He awakened the slumbering Netherworld race members and opened the passage to the Netherworld.

In the depths of the dark sea. Li Fan opened the "Return to Truth" panel.

[You can choose one of the following options to retain:

1. One item held by yourself in this simulation.

2. Your cultivation realm in this simulation.

3. The simulated memories of a person closely related to you in this simulation. This memory can be inherited by that person.

4. Forgo the above options and accelerate the charging progress.]

...

The flashing light symbols had been present for eight years.

"Inherit cultivation." Li Fan chanted silently in his heart, simultaneously reaching the peak of his vigilance.

At the same time, across the firmaments of Great Xuan, the Boundary-Leaving Realm, the Beastkin Realm, and other conquered small worlds, streaks of silver lines crisscrossed. Like a giant net, it enveloped all living beings. Few beings within the net could sense the impending fatal crisis; some looked up at the sky in surprise. Only those with some cultivation, the "strong ones," felt a vague sense of unease. The eternally unchanging dark sea seemed to suddenly stir with imperceptible waves. A storm-like fluctuation descended upon Li Fan, creating a violent vortex around him. Foundation Establishment, Golden Core, Nascent Soul... Earth-shattering changes suddenly occurred within Li Fan's body. Li Fan saw his cloud-like "Return to Truth" foundation instantly transform into a Golden Core. Then, in an explosion that devoured all light, it evolved into the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven. The Grotto-Heaven completed an evolution that would normally take millennia in an instant. The majestic Five Elements presented a grand spectacle. Subsequently, the boundaries between the Five Elements became blurred. Various changes unfolded rapidly within the Grotto-Heaven, dazzling to behold.

"The Xuanhuang world-destroying change." The Five Elements merged into one. All changes within the newly born Grotto-Heaven were aimed at countering the non-existent world-destroying crisis of this world. The giant tree in the original Wood-element Grotto-Heaven's leaves fell, leaving only bare branches. However, its trunk gradually turned as hard as gold and iron. The boundless sea of the Water-element Grotto-Heaven began to freeze for thousands of miles. The scorching flames of the Fire-element Grotto-Heaven dimmed. But they did not extinguish. Instead, they continuously shrank and condensed. Transforming into peculiar wisps of free-floating flame.

...

Various unbelievable changes occurred sequentially within Li Fan. His realm also broke through Nascent Soul, rapidly advancing into the Deification stage. Early Deification, Mid-Deification, Late Deification... It only stopped upon reaching the Great Perfection of Deification. Powerful. Vibrant. Dominated by aggression. This was how Li Fan felt about himself at this moment. But Li Fan had no time to savor it. As he predicted, his transformation within the True Immortal Net had, after this round of "Return to Truth," quickly attracted the attention of the Faceless True Immortal beyond the high wall. The surroundings no longer seemed entirely dark but were dotted with points of light. Waves seemed to ebb and flow; uninvited guests had arrived in the silent dark sea.

"Return to Truth." Li Fan stated decisively. The surrounding scene became still. Then it rapidly misted over. Perhaps it was because the Faceless True Immortal had not fully investigated the anomaly within the net, or perhaps the dark sea had shielded most of the Faceless True Immortal's power. In any event, this "Return to Truth" process went very smoothly. The void-like white mist did not last long before dissipating with a boom. Light reappeared.

Anchor Year 1, Desolate Mountain Peak!

"Safe return."

"Proving my method is feasible." Li Fan breathed a sigh of relief, temporarily ignoring the "Return to Truth" prompt. He carefully examined his own face. The influence of the Faceless True Immortal's power, after another "Return to Truth," had indeed weakened to a certain degree. Li Fan's face was no longer a smooth, featureless expanse. Instead, faint outlines of facial features had slightly protruded. However, this appearance looked even more unsettling than being completely faceless. But Li Fan did not care.

"Next, I just need to repeat the process." He skillfully flew towards the capital city of Great Xuan. Subsequently, what happened in Great Xuan and several other small worlds was almost identical to the previous lifetime, the 120th iteration. The only possible difference was that Li Fan was more proficient and skipped many trial-and-error steps. To be safe, Li Fan did not deviate from the plan; he even stopped researching the use of faith power from the Netherworld race members. Minimizing all variables. In the 121st iteration, the "Return to Truth" charging progress accelerated. The charging was completed three months ahead of schedule. Hiding in the dark sea, inheriting cultivation, returning to truth. A seamless sequence. Next, the 122nd iteration, the 123rd iteration... All the way to the 125th iteration. In early Anchor Year 8, Li Fan once again arrived at the dark sea. He had a premonition that after this "Return to Truth," he would finally completely escape the influence of the Faceless True Immortal. His face now looked like that of a normal person. However, he still sensed certain imperfections, imperceptible to the naked eye or divine sense. The influence of the True Immortal Net still existed. But it was as fragile as brittle paper. Li Fan suppressed the urge to take a reckless action. Taking a deep breath, he silently chanted in his heart.

"Return to Truth!" The scene instantly shifted between illusion and reality. Mist condensed and then scattered in an instant.

In the 126th iteration, Anchor Year 1, Desolate Mountain!

"Hoo!" A feeling completely different from the previous lifetimes washed over Li Fan. It was genuine freedom, unbridled and unrestrained.

"Long confined in a cage, I now return to nature." Li Fan softly murmured, then slowly walked to the edge of the cliff.

"Xuanhuang Realm, I have returned!" Facing the boundless sea of clouds, Li Fan chose to inherit his cultivation. Above the Great Xuan, the sky and clouds churned instantly. The entire world seemed to groan under the unbearable pressure, making creaking sounds as if on the verge of collapse. However, this change was fleeting. The immense aura radiating from Li Fan quickly subsided. The sky returned to normal.

"Great Perfection of Deification. The Great Xuan world is already struggling to bear it."

"If I were at the Great Perfection of Dao Integration, the world would likely shatter the moment I inherited my cultivation."

"But it matters not. I can inherit my cultivation within the Xuanhuang Realm then, or upgrade the Great Xuan world first." Li Fan shook his head slightly, then shifted his thoughts to the plan for this lifetime.

"In this lifetime, I will remain behind the scenes."

"My true self will never make an appearance unless absolutely necessary."

"Everything else is secondary, merely to verify my previous conjecture." Li Fan narrowed his eyes, gazing into the distance, as if seeing the sky of the Xuanhuang Great World.

"The transmission of dharma, what is its true connection to the Heavenly Doctor..." Setting aside the argument that Dharma Transmission and the Heavenly Doctor had never appeared simultaneously, Li Fan's suspicion about their relationship stemmed from the "Record of Mending the Heavens" passed down by the Heavenly Doctor. At the end of the "Record of Mending the Heavens," a theoretical method for saving worlds was described: "Borrowing a shell for reincarnation, breaking and then being reborn." Worlds, even the most powerful cultivation worlds, like living beings, had an end to their existence. When a world inevitably moved towards decay and demise, even the most skillful physicians would be powerless to reverse its fate, merely watching it perish. This was the normal, theoretical situation. However, the Heavenly Doctor proposed a possibility for saving worlds: finding another cultivation world in its prime and performing a "soul transference."

"The Heavenly Dao changes, and the world transforms."

"Although it seems absurd and incredible, for the Heavenly Doctor, it might not be impossible."

"Moreover..." As Li Fan recalled the scenes witnessed since entering the Xuanhuang Realm, they flashed rapidly before his eyes.

"The phenomena predicted in the Record of Mending the Heavens during world reincarnation strongly resemble the current state of the Xuanhuang Realm."

"Anomalies arise, and the Heavenly Dao undergoes sudden changes."

"More importantly..."

"The Heavenly Doctor is from the Heavenly Law Realm, yet attaches such importance to the Xuanhuang Realm, desperately wandering the bleakest reaches of the sea, collecting fragments of other worlds."

"Coupled with the Heavenly Doctor's previous actions..." Li Fan's eyes flickered.

"The accuracy of the Heavenly Doctor's 'World Mending Plan' is almost certain."

"The only chilling aspect is the attitude of Dharma Transmission."

"If he knew that the Heavenly Doctor was from another world and intended to 'borrow' the Xuanhuang Realm for rebirth, yet Dharma Transmission did not interfere at all."

"Instead, like the Heavenly Doctor, he also went out to collect world fragments in the star sea..."

"... " Li Fan's heart felt heavy.

"Either it's possible that Dharma Transmission, lacking any better method to save the Xuanhuang Realm, was forced to act this way."

"Or..."

"Dharma Transmission and the Heavenly Doctor are actually the same person!"

"Or rather, Dharma Transmission is a clone of the Heavenly Doctor!" A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. In the Xuanhuang Realm, countless cultivators harbored a question: Why did Dharma Transmission, while roaming the heavens, not leave behind a clone? If there were only a clone, it would be enough to suppress all scoundrels in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Chapter 1139: Sun Family's Last Resort

The Sun Family's Hidden Hand

Li Fan lay on the bed with his eyes closed, seemingly oblivious to Wu Ninglu's words.

Wu Ninglu's beautiful eyes darted around, about to shed her clothes and climb onto the bed herself.

However, just as her body was about to approach Li Fan, an bone-chilling coldness made her instinctively shiver and retreat.

Upon closer inspection, Wu Ninglu was horrified to discover that a layer of frost had inexplicably formed on her skin at that very moment.

If she hadn't instinctively dodged, Wu Ninglu had no doubt that her husband would have frozen her into an ice sculpture!

She was both pleased and angered.

Though she had a thousand unsaid words, Li Fan suddenly spoke softly, "I just broke through and cannot yet perfectly control my power. It's best if you don't approach me casually for now."

Rejected in her attempt to offer warmth, Wu Ninglu was no longer angry.

Her face lit up with joy, and she nodded repeatedly. "Okay, okay. I didn't expect you, Sun Lang, to give me such a big surprise after disappearing for over half a year. This is a major event, and the clan must be informed!"

Just as Wu Ninglu was about to leave, an ice wall inexplicably appeared, blocking the door and obstructing her path.

Turning back, she looked at Li Fan.

Li Fan still had his eyes closed, but he spoke a seemingly unrelated sentence.

"Regarding the matter of which of the three elders in the clan will take up the post at the Law Enforcement Hall, has a decision been made?"

Wu Ninglu paused for a moment, then immediately understood.

"The Patriarch naturally cannot leave. Elder Uncle and Third Uncle have been pushing the responsibility back and forth for a while, but recently, it's said that Elder Uncle finally relented and compromised..."

Saying this, Wu Ninglu couldn't help but retract her foot.

"Our branch is not exactly well-regarded in the clan. If my promotion to Dao Integration becomes known, they might send me to the Law Enforcement Hall in their stead. At least three hundred years of confinement outside..."

"Hmph."

"If it weren't for the fact that I sustained injuries during my breakthrough and my realm is unstable, fearing that outsiders might detect it and reap the rewards. I wouldn't have returned prematurely."

Li Fan sighed slightly.

"Although taking up a position at the Law Enforcement Hall will come with certain material compensation from the clan and the Immortal Alliance, most of that is already useless to me. Moreover, three hundred years is far too long."

Li Fan suddenly opened his eyes and looked at Wu Ninglu.

"Therefore, my advancement must be kept secret for now."

When their eyes met, Wu Ninglu's body trembled violently, and she subconsciously nodded.

Li Fan closed his eyes again to recuperate.

Silence descended upon the room once more.

The faint ice-sealing field caused Wu Ninglu to operate her spiritual energy at full capacity just to maintain her body temperature.

Curled up in a corner of the room, Wu Ninglu felt both wronged and envious.

"Is this the might of Dao Integration? I never thought he would actually reach Dao Integration. I originally thought Sun Weizhou would be the first among the younger generation to break through."

Wu Ninglu looked at her husband, who was recuperating and cultivating, her mind racing with thoughts.

Only when the fluctuations of his aura gradually subsided did she realize he was still meditating with his eyes closed.

Feeling sulky, Wu Ninglu quietly left the room.

...

"If I'm not mistaken, this foolish woman will soon leak the news that her dao companion is a Dao Integration expert."

"It's all for a little benefit promised by Sun Lushang."

"It's not that she's truly foolish. After all, benefits held in hand are real. As long as Sun Ang is a Dao Integration expert, no matter where he is, people will treat her, the wife of a Dao Integration expert, with respect." Li Fan's gaze was profound, as if he could see through time.

Just as Li Fan predicted.

Half a month later, when Wu Ninglu personally witnessed the generous offers made by her Elder Uncle and Third Uncle to avoid serving at the Law Enforcement Hall, she couldn't help but feel tempted.

After all, her life with Sun Ang had not been particularly smooth in the past. They had no say in the clan's decisions, and good fortune always went to others first.

However, due to Li Fan's previous instructions, she did not speak directly.

But Wu Ninglu's unusual expression did not escape the eyes of the Sun family's several Dao Integration elders.

Coupled with the subtle fluctuation that Li Fan had deliberately emitted upon his return earlier, it led them to have implicit suspicions.

After some inquiries, Wu Ninglu reluctantly revealed the matter.

Sun Lushang was overjoyed and immediately dragged his two brothers to visit.

Li Fan feigned helplessness and anger, looking at Wu Ninglu.

The three elders at the Dao Integration stage took the initiative to intercede for her.

Then, appealing to reason and emotion, they persuaded Li Fan one after another.

For the overall benefit of the clan, he finally had to agree to go to the Law Enforcement Hall in their stead.

"Don't worry, Lu'er. During your absence, we will take good care of Ninglu and ensure she doesn't suffer any grievances." Sun Lushang promised.

Lu'er was Sun Ang's given name.

Logically speaking, as fellow Dao Integration cultivators, even as elders, calling him by his given name was inappropriate. However, Sun Lushang continued to use it, perhaps to remind "Sun Ang" of his status as a disciple of the Sun family.

To ensure that "Sun Ang" could pass the Myriad Immortals Alliance's review, the three Sun family Dao Integration elders jointly tested "Sun Ang's" actual combat strength.

Li Fan mainly focused on defense, occasionally unleashing one or two low-power techniques.

After persisting for hundreds of rounds, he gradually showed signs of faltering.

"Lu'er, the Essence of Heaven and Earth you absorbed is truly extraordinary. Although its offensive power is lacking, its field effect of freezing everything around can block most offensive maneuvers."

The three Sun family Dao Integration elders were quite satisfied with Li Fan's performance.

Even as a newly advanced Dao Integration cultivator, this level of strength was enough to satisfy the Immortal Alliance's requirements.

Before heading to the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters, Li Fan secretly called Wu Ninglu to his side.

"I know you've been avoiding me lately, afraid I'll blame you?"

"How could I?"

"Actually, I know that even if you didn't tell me, my breakthrough to Dao Integration couldn't be hidden for long. Some things are inevitable."

"Besides, we are one. If I work hard for three hundred years to gain some benefits for you, it's nothing."

Wu Ninglu was greatly surprised by Li Fan's words and was momentarily stunned.

She was even a little moved.

"While I'm away, you must be careful on your own."

"Those old guys in the family say nice things, but who knows what they're really like."

"During this trip, I made a friend who helped me greatly in my breakthrough."

As Li Fan spoke, he handed her a communication jade talisman.

"If you encounter any insurmountable problems, contact him."

"He should be able to help you resolve them."

"However, this person is also a Dao Integration cultivator and has a rather eccentric personality. Don't ask for his help unless absolutely necessary."

"Remember this, remember this."

...
